Ma2-Thai3 Hok-Im

Te7 1 ChiuN

Ia5-sou Ki-tok e5 Chok8-phou2: (Lou7 3:23-38)
1) Che si7 Ia5-sou Ki-tok e5 chok8-phou2. Ia5-sou si7 Tai7-pit8 e5 kiaN2-sun, Tai7-pit8 si7 A-pek-lah8-han2 e5 kiaN2-sun.
2) A-pek-lah8-han2 seN I2-sat; I2-sat seN Nga2-kok; Nga2-kok seN Iu5-tai7 kap i e5 hiaN-ti7;  3) Iu5-tai7 seN Hoat-lek8-su kap Sat-lah8 (in e5 lau7-bo2 si7 Tai7-ma2); Hoat-lek8-su seN I2-su7-lun5; I2-su7-lun5 seN A-lan5;  4) A-lan5 seN A-bi2-na2-tat8; A-bi2-na2-tat8 seN Na2-sun7; Na2-sun7 seN Sat-bun5;  5) Sat-bun5 seN Pho-su7 (Pho-su7 e5 lau7-bo2 si7 Lat-hap8); Pho-su7 seN O-pek (O-pek e5 lau7-bo2 si7 Lou7-tek); O-pek seN Ia5-se;  6) Ia5-se seN Tai7-pit8 Ong5.
	Tai7-pit8 seN Sou2-lo5-bun5 (Sou2-lo5-bun5 e5 lau7-bo2, i2-cheng5 si7 Ou-li7-a e5 bou2);  7) Sou2-lo5-bun5 seN Lo5-pho-am3; Lo5-pho-am3 seN A-pi2-a; A-pi2-a seN A-sat;  8) A-sat seN Iok-sa-hoat; Iok-sa-hoat seN Iok-lan5; Iok-lan5 seN Ou-se-a;  9) Ou-se-a seN Iok-tan3; Iok-tan3 seN A-khap-su7; A-khap-su7 seN Hi-se-ka;  10) Hi-se-ka seN Ma2-na2-se; Ma2-na2-se seN A-bun5; A-bun5 seN Iok-se-a;  11) I2-sek-liat bin5-chok8 hou7 lang5 liah8-khi3 Pa-pi2-lun5 e5 si5, Iok-se-a seN Ia5-ko-ni5-a kap i e5 hiaN-ti7.
	12) I2-sek-liat8 bin5-chok8 hou7 lang5 liah8-khi3 Pa-pi2-lun5 liau2-au7, Ia5-ko-ni5-a seN Sat-liap8-thiat; Sat-liap8-thiat seN Sou2-lo5-pa2-pek;  13) Sou2-lo5-pa2-pek seN A-pi2-ut; A-pi2-ut seN I2-li7-a-kim; I2-li7-a-kim seN A-sou2;  14) A-sou2 seN Sat-tok8; Sat-tok8 seN A-kim; A-kim seN I2-lut8;  15) I2-lut8 seN I2-li7-a-sat; I2-li7-a-sat seN Ma2-tan3; Ma2-tan3 seN Nga2-kok;  16) Nga2-kok seN Ma2-li7-a e5 tiong7-hu Iok-sek.  Ma2-li7-a si7 Ia5-sou e5 lau7-bo2.  Chit e5 Ia5-sou hou7 lang5 chheng-hou cho3 Bi2-sai3-a.
	17) An2-ne tui3 A-pek-lah8-han2 kau3 Tai7-pit8, long2-chong2 u7 chap8-si3 tai7, tui3 Tai7-pit8 kau3 I2-sek-liat8 bin5-chok8 hou7 lang5 liah8-khi3 Pa-pi2-lun5, ia7 u7 chap8-si3 tai7, tui3 I2-sek-liat8 bin5-chok8 hou7 lang5 liah8-khi3 Pa-pi2-lun5 kau3 Bi2-sai3-a e5 tan3-seng ia7 u7 chap8-si3 tai7.

Ia5-sou Ki-tok e5 tan3-seng: (Lou7 2:1-7)
	18) Ia5-sou Ki-tok tan3-seng e5 cheng5-heng5 si7 an2-ne.  I e5 lau7-bo2 Ma2-li7-a kap Iok-sek teng7-hun, tan7-si7 in iau2-boe7 kiat-hun i2-cheng5, Seng3 Leng5 chiu7 hou7 Ma2-li7-a hoai5-in7.  19) I e5 bi7-hun-hu Iok-sek si7 chit8 e5 gi7-jin5, bo5 ai3 hian2-jian5 hou7 i kian3-siau3, siuN7 boeh am3-tiong ka7 i hoe3-chhin.  20) I tu2-teh kho2-li7 chit hang7 tai7-chi3 e5 si5, Chu2 e5 thian-sai3 ti7 bang7-tiong hian2-hian7 lai5 ka7 i kong2: “Tai7-pit8 e5 kiaN2-sun Iok-sek a3, m7-bian2 kiaN chhoa7 Ma2-li7-a cho3 li2 e5 bou2, in-ui7 i si7 Seng3 Leng5 hou7 i hoai-in7 e5.  21) I e7 seN cha-pou-kiaN2. Li2 tioh8 ka7 I ho7-mia5 kio3-cho3 Ia5-sou, in-ui7 I e7 kiu3 I e5 peh-seN3 thoat-li7 in e5 choe7-ok.”
	22) Che it-chhe3 e5 tai7-chi3, long2 si7 boeh eng3-giam7 Chu2 thok tai7-gian5-jin5 sou2 kong2 e5 oe7, kong2:
23) “Li2 khoaN3! U7 chit8 ui7 chai7-sek-li2 e7 hoai5-in7 seN chit8 e5 cha-pou-kiaN2; lang5 e7 kio3 I cho3 I2-ma2-loe7-li7.” --- (i3-su3 chiu7-si7 kong2: “Siong7-chu2 kap lan2 tong5-chai7.”)
	24) Iok-sek chheN2 khi2-lai5 liau2-au7, chun-chiau3 Chu2 e5 thian-sai3 e5 beng7-leng7 khi3 chhoa7 Ma2-li7-a cho3 bou2.  25) Tan7-si7 chit e5 cha-pou-kiaN2 chhut-si3 i2-cheng5, Iok-sek kap Ma2-li7-a long2 bo5 jiok8-the2 e5 koan-he7.  Iok-sek chiu7 ka7 I ho7-mia5 kio3-cho3 Ia5-sou.

Te7 2 ChiuN

Hak8-chia2 lai5 tiau5-pai3:
1) Hi-lut8 teh cho3 ong5 e5 si5, Ia5-sou ti7 Iu5-thai3 Seng2 e5 Pek-li7-heng5-siaN5 chhut-si3.  I chhut-si3 liau2 bo5 loa7-ku2 chiu7 u7 thian-bun5 hak8-chia2 tui3 tang-hng lai5 kau3 Ia5-lou7-sat-leng2.  2) In mng7 kong2: “chhut-si3 boeh cho3 Iu5-thai3-lang5 e5 ong5 e5 ang-eN-a2 ti7 tah-ui7? In-ui7 goan2 ti7 tang-hng e5 si5 u7 khoaN3-kiN3 I e5 chheN chhut-hian7, sou2-i2 goan2 lai5 boeh pai3 I.”  3) Hi-lut8 ong5 chit8-e7 thiaN-kiN3 chit hang7 tai7-chi3 chiu7 sim-sin5 put-an, thong Ia5-lou7-sat-leng2-siaN5 e5 lang5 ia7 long2 kap i kang7-khoan2 khi2 put-an.  4) Ong5 chiu7 tiau3-chip8 sou2 u7 e5 che3-si-tiuN2 i2-kip8 I2-sek-liat8 peh-seN3 tiong e5 keng-hak8-chia2 lai5, mng7 in kong2, “Bi2-sai3-a eng-kai tioh8 toa3 sim2-mih sou2-chai7 chhut-si3?”  5) In in3 i kong2: “Ti7 Iu5-thai3 Seng2 e5 Pek-li7-heng5-siaN5, In-ui7 ti7 tai7-gian5-jin5 e5 chheh u7 an2-ne ki3-chai3 kong2: 
6) ‘Li2, Iu5-thai3 te7 e5 Pek-li7-heng5 a3, li2 chai7 Iu5-thai3 e5 thong2-ti7-chia2 tiong, choat8-tui3 m7-si7 siong7 se3 e5, in-ui7 tui3 li2 chia e7 chhut chit8 ui7 leng2-siu7.  I e7 lai5 bok8-iong2 Goa2 e5 peh-seN3 I2-sek-liat8-lang5.’”
	7) Hi-lut8 chiu7 pi2-bit8 tiau3 hiah-e5 thian-bun5 hak8-chia2 lai5, siong5-se3 tham3-mng7 in hit liap8 chheN khak-sit8 si7 sim2-mih si5-jit8 chhut-hian7 e5.  8) Jian5-au7 i chiu7 chhe in khi3 Pek-li7-heng5-siaN5, hoan-hu3 in kong2: “Lin2 khi3 siong5-se3 tham3-thiaN hit-e5 se3-han3 gin2-na2 e5 su7. Lin2 na7 chhoe7-tioh8, tioh8 tng2-lai5 ka7 goa2 po3-ko3. Goa2 ia7 thang khi3 tiau5-pai3 I.”
	9) In thiaN ong5 e5 oe7, chiu7 chhut-hoat khi3. In ti7 tang-hng sou2 khoaN3-kiN3 hit liap8 chheN, ke3-siok8 ti7 in e5 thau5-cheng5 ka7 in chhoa7-lou7, kau3 se3-han3 gin2-na2 toa3 e5 sou2-chai7 chiu7 theng5 toa3 hit teng2-bin7.  10) In chit8-e7 khoaN3-kiN3 hit liap8 chheN chiu7 hui-siong5 heng-hun3 koh hoaN-hi2.  11) In jip8-khi3 chhu3-lai7, khoaN3-kiN3 hit e5 gin2-na2 kap I e5 lau7-bo2 Ma2-li7-a, chiu7 kui7 loh8-khi3 ka7 I keng3-pai3. Jian5-au7 in chiu7 hian-khui in e5 po2-ap8, hian3 ng5-kim, ju2-hiuN, but8-ioh8 cho3 le2-but8 hou7 I.
	12) Siong7-chu2 ti7 in e5 bin5-bang7-tiong keng2-ko3 in m7-thang tng2-khi3 Hi-lut8 hia; in chiu7 tui3 pat8 tiau5 lou7 tng2-khi3 in pun2-kok.

To5-bong5 khi3 Ai-kip8:
	13) In tng2-khi3 liau2-au7, Chu2 e5 thian-sai3 chiu7 hian2-hian7 lai5 ka7 Iok-sek thok-bang7 kong2: “Khi2-lai5! Chhoa7 chit e5 se3-han3 gin2-na2 kap I e5 lau7-bo2, to5-chau2 khi3 Ai-kip8, toa3 hia toa3 kau3 goa2 koh ka7 li2 thong-ti ui5-chi2! Hi-lut8 teh-boeh chhoe7 chit e5 se3-han3 gin2-na2, boeh ka7 I sat-hai7!”  14) Iok-sek chiu7 khi2-lai5, thau3-me5 chhoa7 se3-han3 gin2-na2 kap gin2-na2 e5 lau7-bo2, to5-chau2 khi3 Ai-kip8,  15) toa3 hia toa3 kau3 Hi-lut8 si2-khi3.
	An2-ne chiu7-si7 ui7-tioh8 boeh eng3-giam7 Chu2 thok tai7-gian5-jin5 sou2 kong2 e5 oe7, “Goa2 tui3 Ai-kip8 tiau3 Goa2 e5 KiaN2 chhut-lai5.”

Chan5-sat eng-hai5:
	16) Hi-lut8 chit8-e7 chai-iaN2 hou7 thian-bun5 hak8-chia2 phian3-khi3, chiu7 toa7 siu7-khi3. I ha7-leng7 chiong Pek-li7-heng5-siaN5 kap hu7-kun7 sou2 u7 nng7 hoe3 i2-ha7 e5 cha-pou-gin2-na2 long2 ka7 in thai5-si2. I chit e5 beng7-leng7 si7 kin-ki3 thian-bun5 hak8-chia2 sou2 po3-ko3 chheN chhut-hian7 e5 si5-jit8 chhui-sng3 chhut-lai5 e5.
	17) Che chiu7-si7 eng3-giam7 tai7-gian5-jin5 Ia5-li7-bi2 sou2 kong2 e5 oe7: 
18) “Ti7 Liap8-ma2 u7 thiaN-kiN3 chit8 e5 siaN, Si7 toa7 siaN thi5-khau3 ai-oan3 e5 siaN; Liap8-kiat ui7-tioh8 i e5 kiaN2-ji5 teh khau3. I bo5 ai3 siu7 an-ui3, In-ui7 i e5 kiaN2-ji5 long2 si2-khi3 a3.”

Tui3 Ai-kip8 tng2 lai5:
	19) Hi-lut8 si2 liau2-au7, Chu2 e5 thian-sai3 hian2-hian7 lai5 ka7 ti7 Ai-kip8 e5 Iok-sek thok-bang7,  20) kong2: “Khi2-lai5! Chhoa7 chit e5 gin2-na2 kap gin2-na2 e5 lau7-bo2 to3-tng2-khi3 I2-sek-liat8 e5 te7-thou2, in-ui7 siuN7-boeh sat-hai7 chit e5 gin2-na2 hiah-e5 lang5 i2-keng si2-khi3 a3.”  21) Iok-sek chiu7 khi2-lai5, chhoa7 chit e5 gin2-na2 kap gin2-na2 e5 lau7-bo2, tng2-khi3 I2-sek-liat8 e5 te7-thou2.
	22) Iok-sek chit8-e7 thiaN-kiN3 kong2 A-ki-lo2 ke3-seng5 in lau7-pe7 Hi-lut8 cho3 Iu5-thai3-ong5, chiu7 m7-kaN2 tng2-khi3 hia. I koh ti7 bin5-bang7 tiong tit-tioh8 chi2-si7, chiu7 siam2-pi7 khi3 Ka-li7-li7 Seng2 e5 keng2-lai7.  23) Khi3 kau3 chit8 e5 kio3-cho3 Na2-sat-liat8 e5 siaN5, chiu7 toa3 hit e5 sou2-chai7 ki-chu7. An2-ne chiu7-si7 ui7-tioh8 boeh eng3-giam7 tai7-gian5-jin5 sou2 kong2 e5 oe7, “I e7 hou7 lang5 kio3-cho3 Na2-sat-lek8-lang5.”

Te7 3 ChiuN

Si-sian2-chia2 Iok-han7 e5 Thoan5-to7: (Kho2 1:1-8; Lou7 3:1-18; Iok 1:19-28)
1) Hit e5 si5, si-sian2-chia2 Iok-han7 lai5 kau3 Iu5-thai3 e5 khong3-ia2 teh soan-kang2 to7-li2,  2) kong2, “Lin2 tioh8 hoe2-kai2, in-ui7 Thian-kok teh-boeh kau3 a3.”  3) Chit ui7 chiu7-si7 tai7-gian5-jin5 I2-sai3-a sou2 kong2 hit ui7. I kong2:
	“Ti7 khong3-ia2 u7 lang5 teh hoah kong2:
	‘ Tioh8 ui7 Chu2 chun2-pi7 to7-lou7,
siu-tit8 I sou2 boeh kiaN5 e5 sio2-lou7.’”
4) Chit e5 Iok-han7 chheng7 lok8-to5-mng5 e5 saN, io ha5 phoe5-toa3. I sou2 chiah8 e5 si7 chhau2-meh kap ia2-bit8.  5) Hit e5 si5, Ia5-lou7-sat-leng2-siaN5, choan5 Iu5-thai3 Seng2 i2-kip8 Iok-tan3-ho5 it-tai3 e5 lang5 long2 chhut-khi3 kiN3 Iok-han7.  6) In seng5-jin7 in e5 choe7-ko3; Iok-han7 chiu7 toa3 Iok-tan3-ho5 ka7 in se2-le2.
7) Iok-han7 khoaN3-kiN3 u7 chin che7 Hoat-li7-sai3-phai3 kap Sat-thou2-kai-tong2 e5 lang5 lai5 boeh hou7 i se2-le2 e5 si5, chiu7 tui3 in kong2: “Lin2 chiah-e5 tok8-choa5 a3! Sim2-mih lang5 keng2-ko3 lin2 siam2-pi7 Siong7-chu2 teh-boeh hoat e5 toa7 siu7-khi3 a3?  8) TaN lin2 tioh8 eng7 lin2 e5 heng5-ui5 lai5 cheng3-beng5 lin2 chin-chiaN3 u7 hoe2-kai2!  9) M7-thang ka-ti7 siuN7 kong2, ‘A-pek-lah8-han2 si7 goan2 e5 chou2-sian.’ Goa2 ka7 lin2 kong2, Siong7-chu2 e7-tang3 tui3 chiah-e5 chioh8-thau5 lai5 seN chhut A-pek-lah8-han2 e5 kiaN2-sun.  10) Pou2-thau5 i2-keng tui3-chun2 chhiu7-thau5 a7. Na7 bo5 kiat ho2 koe2-chi2 e5, long2 e7 chho3 khi2-lai5 hiat loh8-khi3 hoe2-nih.  11) Ui7-tioh8 boeh piau2-beng5 lin2 u7 hoe2-kai2, goa2 eng7 chui2 ka7 lin2 se2-le2; tan7-si7 toe3 goa2 e5 au7-bin7 lai5 Hit-ui7, pi2 goa2 khah u7 koan5-leng5. Goa2 lian5 ka7 I koaN7 e5 ia7 be7-kham-tit. I e7 eng7 Seng3 Leng5 kap hoe2 ka7 lin2 se2-le2.  12) I chhiu2-nih theh8 chhiah-ki, boeh chiong tiu7-tiaN5 long2 put hou7 chheng-khi3. I e5 siu chhek-a2 jip8-khi3 chhek-chhng, eng7 be7 hoa-khi3 e5 hoe2 chiong chhau2-khou3 sio-tiau7!”
Ia5-sou siu7 se2-le2: (Kho2 1:9-11; Lou7 3:21-22)
	13) Hit e5 si5, Ia5-sou tui3 Ka-li7-li7 Seng2 lai5 kau3 Iok-tan3-ho5 hia kiN3 Iok-han7, boeh hou7 i se2-le2.  14) Iok-han7 siuN7 boeh ka7 I the-si5, kong2, “Goa2 eng-kai tui3 Li2 nia2-siu7 se2-le2, Li2 an3-choaN2 tian-to3 lai5 goa2 chia?”  15) Ia5-sou in3 i kong2, “TaN chiam-si5 an2-ne cho3. Lan2 na7 an2-ne cho3 si7 tong-jian5 e5, in-ui7 che si7 hu5-hap Siong7-chu2 sou2 iau-kiu5 e5.” Iok-han7 chiu7 chun-chiau3 Ia5-sou e5 i3-su3 khi3 cho3.
	16) Ia5-sou siu7 se2-le2 liau2-au7, chiu7 sui5-si5 tui3 chui2-nih khi2-lai5. Hut-jian5-kan thiN chiu7 hian3-khui. I chiu7 khoaN3-kiN3 Siong7-chu2 e5 Seng3 Leng5, chhin-chhiuN7 chit8 chiah hun2-chiau2 kang3 loh8-lai5 hioh toa3 I e5 seng-khu.  17) Ia7 u7 siaN tui3 thiN-teng2 lai5, kong2:
	“Chit e5 si7 Goa2 sim-ai3 e5 KiaN2, Goa2 chin-chiaN3 kah-i3 e5.”

Te7 4 ChiuN

Ia5-sou siu7 chhi3-tham3: (Kho2 1:12-13; Lou7 4:1-13)
1) Jian5-au7 Seng3 Leng5 chhoa7 Ia5-sou khi3 khong3-ia2, khi3 siu7 Mou5-kui2 e5 chhi3-tham3.  2) Ia5-sou kim3-chiah8 si3-chap8 me5-jit8 liau2-au7, pak-tou2 hui-siong5 iau.  3) Hit e5 chhi3-tham3-chia2 chiu7 oa2-lai5 ka7 I kong2, “Li2 na7-si7 Siong7-chu2 e5 KiaN2, chiu7 tioh8 beng7-leng7 chiah-e5 chioh8-thau5 pian3-cho3 mi7-pau.”
	4) Ia5-sou in3 i kong2, “Seng3-keng u7 ki3-chai3 kong2, ‘Lang5 m7-si7 kan-taN oa2-kho3 mi7-pau lai5 oah8, si7 oa2-kho3 tui3 Siong7-chu2 e5 chhui3 sou2 kong2 chhut-lai5 e5 mui2 chit8 ku3 oe7.’”
	5) Soa3 loh8-khi3, Mou5-kui2 chiu7 chhoa7 Ia5-sou khi3 Seng3-siaN5, hou7 i khia7 toa3 Seng3-tian7 siong7-koan5  e5 sou2-chai7,  5) ka7 i kong2, “Li2 na7-si7 Siong7-chu2 e5 KiaN2, tui3 chia thiau3 loh8-khi3; in-ui7 Seng3-keng u7 ki3-chai3 kong2: ‘siong7-chu2 e7 beng7-leng7 I e5 thian-sai3 lai5 po2-hou7 Li2. In e7 eng7 chhiu2 ka7 Li2 hu5 le7, hou7 Li2 e5 kha be7 pong7-tioh8 chioh8-thau5 lai5 siu7 siong.’”  7) Ia5-sou in3 i kong2, “Seng3-keng ia7 u7 ki3-chai3 kong2, ‘Li2 m7-thang chhi3-tham3 Chu2, Li2 e5 Siong7-chu2.’”
	8) Mou5-kui2 choe3-au7 koh chhoa7 Ia5-sou khi3 chit8 e5 chin koan5 e5 soaN-teng2, hou7 I khoaN3 se3-siong7 ban7-kok kap ban7-kok e5 eng5-hoa5 hu3-kui3,  9) ka7 I kong2, “Li2 na7 phak loh8-khi3 pai3 goa2, chiah-e5 it-chhe3, goa2 long2 boeh hou7 Li2.”  10) Ia5-sou chiu7 ka7 i kong2, “Sat-tan3! chau2! Chau2! Seng3-keng u7 ki3-chai3 kong2, ‘Li2 tioh8 keng3-pai3 Chu2, li2 e5 Siong7-chu2, chi2-u7 tioh8 su7-hong7 I!’”
	11) Mou5-kui2 chiu7 li7-khui Ia5-sou, sui5-si5 chiu7 u7 thian-sai3 lai5 su7-hau7 I.

Ia5-sou chai7 Ka-li7-li7 Seng2 khai-si2 kang-chok: (Kho2 1:14-15; Lou7 4:14-15)
	12) Ia5-sou chit8-e7 thiaN-kiN3 Iok-han7 i2-keng hou7 lang5 koaiN ti7 kaN-gak8, chiu7 siam2-pi7 khi3 Ka-li7-li7 Seng2.  13) I li7-khui Na2-sat-lek8-siaN5, khi3 toa3 ti7 oa2-kin7 Ka-li7-li7-ou5 e5 Ka-pek-long5-siaN5.  Chit e5 siaN5 si7 siok8 ti7 Se-pou3-lun5 kap Na2-hut-tha-li7 e5 keng2-lai7.  14) Che si7 boeh eng3-giam7 tai7-gian5-jin5 I2-sai3-a sou2 kong2 e5 oe7, kong2:
	15) “Se-pou3-lun5-chok8 e5 te7-thou2! Na2-hut-tha-li7-chok8 e5 te7-thou2! Si7 ti7 ian5-hai2 e5 te7-khu, ti7 Iok-tan3-ho5 e5 tui3-hoaN7, si7 Goa7-pang-lang5 teh toa3 e5 Ka-li7-li7 Seng2!  16) Hiah-e5 toa3 ti7 ou-am3 tiong e5 peh-seN3, i2-keng khoaN3-tioh8 ui2-tai7 e5 kng! Chit e5 kng i2-keng chhut-hian7, lai5 chio3 hiah-e5 toa3 ti7 si2-bong5 ou-iaN2 tiong e5 lang5!”
	17) tui3 hit e5 si5 khi2, Ia5-sou khai-si2 soan-kang2 kong2: “Lin2 tioh8 hoe2-kai2, in-ui7 Thian-kok teh-boeh lai5-lim5 a7!”

Ia5-sou tiau3 si3 e5 hi5-hu: (Kho2 1:16-20; Lou7 5:1-11)
	18) U7 chit8 jit8, Ia5-sou sun7 Ka-li7-li7 ou5-piN teh kiaN5 e5 si5, khoaN3-kiN3 nng7 e5 hiaN-ti7, chiu7-si7 kio3-cho3 Se-bun5 (piat8-mia5 Pi2-tek), kap i e5 sio2-ti7 An-tek-liat8, tu2 ti7 ou5-nih8 teh pha-bang7, in-ui7 in si7 hi5-hu.  19) Ia5-sou ka7 in kong2, “Lai5 toe3 Goa2! Goa2 boeh hou7 lin2 chhin-chhiuN7 hi5-hu teh liah8-hi5 an2-ne, khi3 in2-chhoa7 lang5 lai5 sin3 Siong7-chu2.”  20) In sui5-si5 pang3-sak hi5-bang7-a2, lai5 toe3 I.
	21) Tui3 hia koh kiaN5-khi3, I iu7-koh khoaN3-kiN3 nng7 e5 hiaN-ti7, chiu7-si7 Se-pi2-thai3 e5 kiaN2 Nga2-kok kap i e5 sio2-ti7 Iok-han7, tu2 ti7 chun5-nih8 kap in lau7-pe7 teh pou2-bang7.  Ia5-sou ia7 kio3 in lai5 toe3 I.  22) In chiu7 sui5-si5 pang3-sak chun5, li7-khui in lau7-pe7, toe3 Ia5-sou khi3.

Ia5-sou khai-si2 kau3-to7, thoan5-kau3 kap i-peN7: (Lou7 6:17-19)
	23) Ia5-sou Ka-li7-li7 Seng2 long2 kiaN5 than3-than3, jip8-khi3 Iu5-thai3-lang5 e5 hoe7-tng5 ka3-si7 lang5, soan-kang2 Thian-kok e5 Hok-im, i-ho2 cheng3-lang5 kok-chiong2 e5 peN7-cheng3.  24) I e5 mia5-siaN thoan5-kau3 choan5 Su7-li7-a e5 kok sou2-chai7.  Sou2-i2 lang5 chiu7 chiong it-chhe3 u7 peN7 e5, u7 kok-chiong2 cheng3-thau5 peN7-thiaN3 e5, bo5-lun7 si7 tioh8-iau e5, iuN5-hin5 e5, a2-si7 poan3-sui7-e5, long2 chhoa7-khi3 kau3 I hia.  I chiu7 long2 ka7 in i-ho2 khi3.  25) Tui3 Ka-li7-li7, Te-ka-pho-li7, Ia5-lou7-sat-leng2, Iu5-thai3 i2-kip8 Iok-tan3-ho5 e5 tui3-hoaN7, u7 chin toa7 tin7 lang5 lai5 toe3 I.

Te7 5 ChiuN

San-siong7 e5 kau3-hun3:
1) Ia5-sou khoaN3-kiN3 hiah toa7 tin7 e5 lang5, chiu7 peh-chiuN7 soaN, che7 loh8-khi3.  Bun5-tou5 chiu7 oa2-lai5.  2) I khai-si2 ka3-si7 in:

Sit8-chai7 e5 hok-khi3: (Lou7 6:20-23)
	3) “Chai-iaN2 tioh8 oa2-kho3 Siong7-chu2 e5 lang5, sit8-chai7 u7 hok-khi3, in-ui7 in e7 chiaN5-cho3 Thian-kok e5 chu2-bin5!
	4) Ui7-tioh8 choe7-ko3 pi-siong e5 lang5, sit8-chai7 u7 hok-khi3, in-ui7 Siong7-chu2 e7 an-ui3 in!
	5) Un-jiu5 e5 lang5, sit8-chai7 u7 hok-khi3, in-ui7 Siong7-chu2 e7 siuN2-su3 in I sou2 eng3-un2 e5!
	6) Jiat8-chhiat khat-bong7 boeh sit8-heng5 Siong7-chu2 e5 chi2-i3 e5 lang5, sit8-chai7 u7 hok-khi3, in-ui7 Siong7-chu2 e7 hou7 in boan2-chiok!
	7) Eng7 jin5-chu5 tui3-thai7 lang5 e5, sit8-chai7 u7 hok-khi3, in-ui7 Siong7-chu2 e7 eng7 chu5-pi tui3-thai7 in!
	8) Sim-koaN sun5-kiat e5 lang5, sit8-chai7 u7 hok-khi3, in-ui7 in e7 khoaN3-kiN3 Siong7-chu2!
	9) Chhiok-chin3 ho5-peng5 e5 lang5, sit8-chai7 u7 hok-khi3, in-ui7 Siong7-chu2 e7 seng5-jin7 in cho3 kiaN2!
10) Ui7-tioh8 sit8-heng5 Siong7-chu2 e5 chi2-i3 lai5 siu7 pek-hai7 e5 lang5, sit8-chai7 u7 hok-khi3, in-ui7 in e7 chiaN5-cho3 Thian-kok e5 chu2-bin5!
11) Lin2 na7 ui7-tioh8 Goa2, hou7 lang5 bu2-jiok8, pek-hai7, eng7 chiong2-chiong2 e5 phaiN2-oe7 hui2-pong3, chiu7 sit8-chai7 u7 hok-khi3.  12) Tioh8 hoaN-hi2 khoai3-lok8, in-ui7 ti7 thiN-teng2 u7 chin toa7 e5 po3-siuN2 boeh hou7 lin2, in-ui7 kou2-cha2 hiah-e5 tai7-gian5-jin5 ia7-si7 an2-ne hou7 lang5 pek-hai7.

Iam5 kap kng: (Kho2 9:50; Lou7 14:34-35)
	13) “lin2 si7 chhin-chhiuN7 se3-kan-lang5 e5 iam5. Iam5 na7 sit-bi7, boeh an3-choaN2 koh hou7 i u7 kiam5-bi7.  Sit-khi3 hau7-leng5 e5 iam5 i2-keng bo5 lou7-eng7 a7, chi2-u7 hiat chhut-khi3 goa7-bin7, hou7 lang5 tah8-lai5 tah8-khi3 na7-tiaN7.”
	14) “Lin2 si7 chhin-chhiuN7 se3-kan e5 kng. Kian3-siat ti7 soaN-teng2 e5 siaN5-chhi7 be7-tang3 am-kham3.  15) Bo5 lang5 tiam2-teng kham3 toa3 bi2-tau2 lai7, long2 si7 chhai7 toa3 teng hoe2-tai5, lai5 chio3 kng hou7 chhu3-lai7 e5 lang5 u7 khoaN3-kiN3.  16) Chhin-chhiuN7 an2-ne lin2 e5 kng tioh8 chio3 toa3 cheng3-lang5 e5 bin7-cheng5, hou7 in thang khoaN3 lin2 sou2 cho3 e5 ho2 heng5-ui5 lai5 chan3-bi2 lin2 e5 Thian-hu7.”

Koan-he7 Lut8-hoat e5 kau3-hun3: 
	17) “M7-thang siuN7 kong2 Goa2 lai5 e5 bok8-tek si7 boeh hoe3-tiau7 Mou5-se e5 Lut8-hoat i2-kip8 tai7-gian5-jin5 e5 ka3-si7. Goa2 m7-si7 boeh lai5 hoe3-tiau7, si7 boeh lai5 seng5-choan5.  18) Goa2 sit8-chai7 ka7 lin2 kong2, chiu7-si7 kau3 thiN-te7 biat8-bong5, it-tit8 kau3 tat8-seng5 Lut8-hoat e5 bok8-tek ui5-chi2, Lut8-hoat e5 chit8-tiam2 chit8-oeh8 ia7 be7 siau-sit khi3.  19) Sui-jian5 si7 kai3-beng7 tiong siong7-se3 e5 chit8 tiau5, lang5 na7 khi3 hoan7-tioh8, iu7-koh ka3 pat8-lang5 ia7 an2-ne khi3 hoan7, i ti7 Thian-kok chiu7 e7 sng3-cho3 si7 siong7 se3 e5. Tan7-si7 lang5 na7 sit8-heng5 kai3-beng7, iu7-koh ka3 lang5 ia7 an2-ne khi3 sit8-heng5, i ti7 Thian-kok chiu7 e7 sng3-cho3 si7 siong7 ui2-tai7 e5.  20) Goa2 ka7 lin2 kong2, lin2 na7 bo5 pi2 keng-hak8-chia2 kap Hoat-li7-sai3-phai3 e5 lang5 khah tiong-sit8 lai5 chun-heng5 Siong7-chu2 sou2 iau-kiu5 e5, lin2 it-teng7 be7-tang3 chin3-jip8 Thian-kok.”

Koan-he7 siu7-khi3 e5 kau3-hun3:
	21) “Lin2 bat thiaN-kiN3 Lut8-hoat kau3-hun3 kou2-cha2 lang5 kong2, ‘M7-thang thai5-si2 lang5. Na7 thai5-si2 lang5 it-teng7 tioh8 siu7 sim2-phoaN3.’  22) Tan7-si7 Goa2 ka7 lin2 kong2: tui3 ka-ti7 e5 hiaN-ti7 siu7-khi3 e5 lang5, it-teng7 tioh8 siu7 sim2-phoaN3; me7 ka-ti7 e5 hiaN-ti7 ‘png7-thang2’ e5 lang5, it-teng7 tioh8 siu7 Kong-gi7-hoe7 teng7-choe7; me7 i e5 hiaN-ti7 ‘goan7-tai’ e5 lang5, it-teng7 tioh8 siu7 te7-gak8 e5 hoe2-heng5.  23) Sou2-i2 li2 khi3 che3-toaN5 cheng5 boeh hian3 che3-phin2 e5 si5, na7 siuN7-khi2 li2 e5 hiaN-ti7 tui3 li2 u7 phau7 sim2-mih hoan2-kam2,  24) li2 tioh8 chiong che3-phin2 pang3 toa3 che3-toaN5-cheng5, tai7-seng khi3 kap li2 e5 hiaN-ti7 ho5-ho2, jian5-au7 chiah koh tng2-lai5 hian3 li2 e5 che3-phin2.”
	25) “Na7 u7 lang5 khong3-ko3 li2, boeh thao li2 khi3 hoat-teng5, iau2 ti7 lou7-nih8 e5 si5, tioh8 than3-cha2 kap i ho5-kai2; na7 bo5, khong3-ko3 li2 e5 lang5 e7 chiong li2 kau hou7 hoat-keng3, li2 chiu7 e7 hou7 lang5 koaiN-loh8 kaN-gak8.  26) Goa2 sit8-chai7 ka7 li2 kong2, choe3-au7 e5 chit8 sian2-chiN5 li2 na7 bo5 kiau2 kah chheng-chho2, li2 it-teng7 be7-tang3 tui3 hia chhut-lai5.”

Koan-he7 kan-im e5 kau3-hun3:
	27) “Lin2 bat thiaN-kiN3 Lut8-hoat kau3-hun3 lang5 kong2, ‘M7-thang hoan7 kan-im5.’  28) Tan7-si7 Goa2 ka7 lin2 kong2: na7 u7 lang5 phau7 sia5-iok8 lai5 khoaN3 hu7-jin5-lang5, i ti7 sim-lai7 i2-keng kap i hoan7 kan-im5 a7.  29) Li2 e5 chiaN3-bak8 na7 in2-iu2 li2 hoan7-choe7, li2 tioh8 ka7 i ou2 chhut-lai5 tan3 hiat-kak8! Sit-khi3 li2 seng-khu e5 chit8 pou7-hun7, pi2 li2 kui seng-khu ho2-ho2 loh8 te7-gak8 koh-khah iaN5.  30) Li2 e5 chiaN3-chhiu2 na7 in2-iu2 li2 hoan7-choe7, li2 tioh8 ka7 i cham7 khi2-lai5 tan3 hiat-kak8! Sit-khi3 li2 seng-khu e5 chit8 pou7-hun7, pi2 li2 kui seng-khu ho2-ho2 loh8 te7-gak8 koh-khah iaN5.”

Koan-he7 li7-hun e5 kau3-hun3: (Ma2 19:9; Kho2 10:11-12; Lou7 16:18)
	31) “Lut8-hoat e5 kau3-hun3 iu7-koh kong2, ‘Na7 u7 lang5 boeh kap i e5 bou2 li7-hun, tioh8 li7-hun cheng3-su hou7 i.’  32) Tan7-si7 Goa2 ka7 lin2 kong2: lang5 na7 m7-si7 in-ui7 i e5 bou2 kap lang5 su-thong lai5 ka7 i li7-hun, chit e5 hu7-jin5-lang5 na7 koh ke3, i chiu7-si7 hai7 chit e5 hu7-jin5-lang5 hoan7-kan-im5; na7 u7 lang5 kap chit e5 hu7-jin5-lang5 kiat-hun ia7 si7 hoan7 kan-im5.”

Koan-he7 chiu3-choa7 e5 kau3-hun3:
	33) “Lin2 ia7 bat thiaN-kiN3 Lut8-hoat kau3-hun3 kou2-cha2-lang5 kong2, ‘M7-thang ui5-poe7 se3-goan7. Li2 ti7 Siong7-chu2 e5 bin7-cheng5 sou2 lip8 e5 se3-goan7 it-teng7 tioh8 sit8-heng5.’  34) Tan7-si7 Goa2 ka7 lin2 kong2: long2 m7-thang chiu3-choa7; m7-thang ki2 thiN lai5 chiu3-choa7, in-ui7 thiN si7 Siong7-chu2 e5 po2-cho7;  35) ia7 m7-thang ki2 te7 lai5 chiu3-choa7, in-ui7 te7 si7 Siong7-chu2 e5 kha-tiam7; ia7 m7-thang ki2 Ia5-lou7-sat-leng2 lai5 chiu3-choa7, in-ui7 Ia5-lou7-sat-leng2 si7 toa7 kun-ong5 e5 kiaN-siaN5.  36) Ia7 m7-thang ki2 li2 e5 thau5-khak lai5 chiu3-choa7, in-ui7 li2 be7-tang3 hou7 chit8 ki thau5-mng5 pian3-cho3 peh8 e5, a2-si7 pian3-cho3 ou e5.  37) Lin2 kong2-oe7 eng-kai ‘Si7’ chiu7 kong2 ‘Si7’, ‘M7-si7’ chiu7 kong2 ‘M7-si7’. Na7-si7 ke kong2 e5, lin2 sou2 kong2 e5 si7 tui3 Mou5-kui2 chhut-lai5 e5.”

Koan-he7 po3-hok8 e5 kau3-hun3: (Lou7 6:29-30)
	38) “Lin2 ia7 bat thiaN-kiN3 Lut8-hoat e5 kau3-hun3 kong2, ‘I2 gan2 hoan5 gan2, i2 ge5 hoan5 ge5.’  39) Tan7-si7 Goa2 ka7 lin2 kong2: m7-thang ‘I2 ok po3 ok.’ Na7 u7 lang5 sian3 li2 chiaN3-peng5 e5 chhui3-phe2, tioh8 oat8 to3-peng5 e5 chhui3-phe2 hou7 i sian3.  40) Na7 u7 lang5 khong3-ko3 li2, boeh ai3 li2 e5 lai7-saN, lian5 goa7-saN ia7 tioh8 thng3 hou7 i.  41) Na7 u7 lang5 kiong5-pek li2 gia5 i e5 heng5-li2 kiaN5 chit8 li2 lou7, tioh8 kap i kiaN5 nng7 li2 lou7.  42) Na7 u7 lang5 tui3 li2 kiu5 sim2-mih, tioh8 hou7 i; na7 u7 lang5 boeh ka7 li2 chioh sim2-mih, m7-thang ka7 i the-si5.”

Ai3 tek8-jin5: (Lou7 6:27-28, 32-36)
	43) “Lin2 ia7 bat thiaN-kiN3 Lut8-hoat e5 kau3-hun3 kong2, ‘Tioh8 ai3 li2 e5 lin5-jin5, oan3-hun7 li2 e5 tek8-jin5.’  44) Tan7-si7 Goa2 ka7 lin2 kong2: tioh8 ai3 lin2 e5 tek8-jin5, tioh8 ui7 pek-hai7 lin2 e5 lang5 ki5-to2.  45) Lin2 na7 an2-ne cho3, lin2 chiu7 e7 chiaN5-cho3 Thian-hu7 e5 kiaN2-ji5, in-ui7 I hou7 I e5 jit8-thau5 chhut-lai5 chio3 ho2-lang5, ia7 chio3 phaiN2-lang5, peN5-peN5 ui7-tioh8 kong-gi7 kap put-gi7 e5 lang5 loh8-hou7.  46) Lin2 na7 kan-taN ai3 hiah-e5 ai3 lin2 e5 lang5, kam2 e7-tang3 tit-tioh8 sim2-mih po3-siuN2? Lian5 hiah-e5 thiu-soe3 e5 lang5 ma7 e7-hiau2 an2-ne cho3.  47) Lin2 na7 chi2-u7 tui3 lin2 e5 hiaN-ti7 chheng2-an, an2-ne kam2 u7 sim2-mih hi-han2? Lian5 bo5 sin3 Siong7-chu2 e5 lang5 ma7 it-teng7 e7 hiau2 an2-ne cho3.  48) Sou2-i2 lin2 tioh8 cho3 oan5-sian7 e5 lang5, chhin-chhiuN7 lin2 e5 Thian-hu7 si7 oan5-sian7 e5.”

Te7 6 ChiuN

Koan-he7 heng5-sian7 e5 kau3-hun3:
1) n2 tioh8 kin2-sin7, m7-thang ui7-tioh8 boeh hou7 lang5 khoaN3, kou3-i3 toa3 lang5 e5 bin7-cheng5 hian2-si7 lin2 e5 sian7-heng5.  Lin2 na7 an2-ne cho3, lin2 chiu7 be7-tang3 tui3 Thian-hu7 tit-tioh8 po3-siuN2.  2) Sou2-i2 li2 boeh chin2-che3 e5 si5, m7-thang chhin-chhiuN7 gui7-sian7-chia2 toa3 hoe7-tng5 kap ke-lou7 pun5 kou2-chhoe soan-thoan5, ai3 hou7 lang5 o-lo2. Goa2 sit8-chai7 ka7 li2 kong2, in i2-keng tit-tioh8 in e5 po3-siuN2 a3.  3) Li2 chin2-che3 lang5 e5 si5, lian5 li2 e5 chiaN3-chhiu2 sou2 cho3 e5 to m7-thang hou7 li2 e5 to3-chhiu2 chai-iaN2.  4) Li2 na7 an2-ne tiam7-tiam7-a2 lai5 kiu3-che3 lang5, Hit-ui7 khoaN3-kiN3 li2 ti7 am3-tiong sou2 choe3 e5 Thian-hu7, chiu7 e7 po3-tap li2.”

Koan-he7 ki5-to2 e5 kau3-hun3: (Lou7 11:2-4)
	5) “lin2 ki5-to2 e5 si5 m7-thang oh8 hiah-e5 gui7-sian7-chia2! In ai3 khia7 toa3 hoe7-tng5 a2-si7 sip8-ji7 lou7-khau2 ki5-to2, kou3-i3 boeh hou7 lang5 khoaN3. Goa2 sit8-chai7 ka7 lin2 kong2, in i2-keng tit-tioh8 in e5 po3-siuN2 a3.  6) Tan7-si7 li2 ki5-to2 e5 si5, tioh8 jip8-khi3 li2 e5 pang5-keng lai7, mng5 koaiN khi2-lai5, lai5 tui3 li2 sou2 khoaN3 be7-tioh8 e5 Thian-hu7 ki5-kiu5. An2-ne Hit-ui7 khoaN3-kiN3 li2 ti7 am3-tiong sou2 cho3 e5 Thian-hu7, chiu7 e7 po3-tap li2.”
	7) “Lin2 ki5-to2 e5 si5, m7-thang chhin-chhiuN7 bo5 sin3 Siong7-chu2 e5 lang5 lo5-lo5 so-so, in-ui7 in siuN7 kong2 tioh8-ai3 ki5-to2 chin ku2, Siong7-chu2 chiah e7 thiaN in e5 ki5-kiu5.  8) Sou2-i2 lin2 m7-thang kap in kang7-khoan2; in-ui7 lin2 boeh kiu5 i2-cheng5, lin2 e5 Thian-hu7 chiu7 i2-keng chai-iaN2lin2 sou2 su-iau3 e5 si7 sim2-mih.  9) Sou2-i2 lin2 tioh8 an2-ne ki5-to2:
‘Goan2 ti7 thiN-nih e5 Hu7-chhin!
Goan7 Li2 e5 mia5 hou7 lang5 chun-tiong7 cho3 chi3-seng3 e5,
10) Goan7 Li2 e5 ong5-kok lai5-lim5,
Goan7 Li2 e5 chi2-i3 chai7 te7-siong7 sit8-heng5 chhin-chhiuN7 chai7 thian-siong7.
11) Kiu5 Li2 kin-na2-jit8 siuN2-su3 goan2 mui2-jit8 sou2 su-iau3 e5 chiah8-mih8.
12) Kiu5 Li2 sia3-bian2 goan2 it-chhe3 e5 choe7-ko3, chhin-chhiuN7 goan2u sia3-bian2 hiah-e5 tek-choe7 goan2 e5 lang5.
13) M7-thang hou7 goan2 ham7-loh8 iu2-hek8, kiu3 goan2 thoat-li7 hit e5 hiong-ok-chia2.’
(In-ui7 ong5-kok, koan5-leng5, eng5-iau7 long2 siok8 Li2, kau3 ban7-se3 ban7-tai7. Amen.)”
14) “Lin2 na7 sia3-bian2 pat8-lang5 e5 choe7-ko3, lin2 e5 Thian-hu7 ia7 e7 sia3-bian2 lin2.  15) Lin2 na7 bo5 sia3-bian2 lang5, lin2 e5 Thian-hu7 ia7 be7 sia3-bian2 lin2 e5 choe7-ko3.”

Koan-he7 kim3-chiah8 e5 kau3-hun3:
	16) “Lin2 kim3-chiah8 e5 si5, m7-thang chhin-chhiuN7 gui7-sian7-chia2 bin7 tai3 iu-chhiu5. In thau5-mng5 bo5 loah8, bin7 bo5 se2, moas2i-ke3 kiaN5, kou3-i3 boeh hou7 lang5 chai-iaN2 in teh kim3-chiah8. Goa2 sit8-chai7 ka7 lin2 kong2, in i2-keng tit-tioh8 po3-siuN2 a3.  17) Tan7-si7 li2 kim3-chiah8 e5 si5, bin7 tioh8 se2 chheng-khi3, thau5-mng5 tioh8 loah8,  18) m7-thang hou7 lang5 chai-iaN2 li2 teh kim3-chiah8, chi2-u7 hou7 khoaN3 be7-tioh8 e5 Thian-hu7 chai-iaN2. An2-ne Hit-ui7 khoaN3-kiN3 li2 ti7 am3-tiong sou2 cho3 e5 Thian-hu7, chiu7 e7 po3-siuN2 li.”

Thian-siong7 e5 chai5-po2: (Lou7 12:33-34)
	19) “M7-thang ui7-tioh8 ka-ti7 chek-thiok chai5-po2 toa3 te7-siong7, in-ui7 ti7 chia u7 chiu3-thang5 e7 ka7, e7 seN-sian, chhat8-a2 ia7 e7 ou2-khang jip8-lai5 thau-theh8.  20) Tioh8 ui7 ka-ti7 chek-thiok chai5-po2 toa3 thiN-teng2, in-ui7 ti7 hia bo5 chiu3-thang5 e7 ka7, be7 seN-sian, ia7 bochh5at-a2 e7 ou2-khang jip8-khi3 thau-theh8.  21) In-ui7 li2 e5 chai5-po2 na7 ti7 hia, li2 e5 sim ia7 it-teng7 e7 ti7 hia.”

Seng-khu e5 teng-hoe2: (Lou7 11:34-36)
	22) “Bak8-chiu chhin-chhiuN7 lang5 e5 seng-khu e5 teng-hoe2. Li2 e5 bak8-chiu na7 kim, kui seng-khu chiu7 e7 kng.  23) Li2 e5 bak8-chiu na7 hoe, kui seng-khu chiu7 ou-am3. An2-ne ka2-su2 li2 lai7-sim e5 kng na7 piN3-cho3 ou-am3, chit e5 ou-am3 m7-chai loa7-nih li7-hai7!”

Siong7-chu2 kap chiN5-chai5: (Lou7 16:13; 12:22-31)
	24) “Chit8 e5 lang5 be7-tang3 hong7-su7 nng7 e5 chu2-lang5. Hong7-su7 nng7 e5 chu2-lang5 e5 si5, na7 m7-si7 oan3-hin7 chit e5, keng3-ai3 hit e5, chiu7-si7 khoaN3-tang7 chit e5, khoaN3-khin hit e5. Sou2-i2 lin2 be7-tang3 kang7-si5 hong7-su7 Siong7-chu2 ia7 boeh hong7-su7 chiN5-chai5.”
	25) “In-ui7 an2-ne Goa2 ka7 lin2 kong2: m7-thang ui7-tioh8 lin2 e5 seN3-mia7 hoan5-lo2 boeh chiah8 sim2-mih, lim sim2-mih, seng-khu boeh chheng7 sim2-mih. Lin2 e5 seN3-mia7 kam2 m7-si2 pi2 chiah8-mih8 khah u7 ke3-tat8, seng-khu kam2 m7-si7 pi2 saN-khpp3 khah u7 ke3-tat8?  26) Lin2 khoaN3khong-tiong e5 chiau2-a2, in bo5 cheng3-choh, bo5 siu-seng5, ia7 bo5 chek-niu5 toa3 chhng-khou3; siong7-chhiaN2 lin2 e5 Thian-hu7 ia7 teh ka7 in iuN2-chhi7. Lin2 kam2 bo5 pi2 hiah-e5 chiau2-a2 khah kui3-tiong7?  27) Lin2 sim2-mih lang5 chhau-hoan5 chiu7 e7-tang3 hou7 ka-ti7 e5 seN3-mia7 ke oah8 chit8 si5-a2 ku2?”
	28) “Lin2 ho5-pit ui7 saN-khou3 lai5 chhau-hoan5? Lin2 siuN7 khoaN3-bai7-le3, ia2-seng e5 pek-hap8-hoe choaN2-iuN7 teh toa7-chang5! In bo5 lo5-khou2, ia7 bo5 phang2-chit.  29) Tan7-si7 Goa2 ka7 lin2 kong2, lian5 hiah-nih8 eng5-hoa5 hu3-kui3 e5 Sou2-lo5-bun5-ong5 sou2 chheng7 e5 saN to be7 pi2 chiah-e5 hoe e5 chit8-lui2 koh-khah sui2.  30) kin-na2-jit8 teh oah8, bin5-na2-chai3 hou7 lang5 hiat loh8-khi3 hoe2-lou5 chiah e5 ia2-seng e5 hoe-chhau2, Siong7-chu2 siong7-chhiaN2 to an2-ne teh ka7 in chng-chhah, I kam2 be7 koh-khah ka7 lin2 khoaN3-kou3? Lin2 na2 e7 hiah-nih8 bo5 sin3-sim!  31) Sou2-i2 lin2 m7-thang chhau-hoan5 kong2: ‘Goan2 boeh chiah8 sim2-mih, boeh lim sim2-mih, boeh chheng sim2-mih?’  32) (In-ui7 chiah-e5 long2 si7 bi7-sin3-chia2 sou2 teh tui-kiu5 e5.) Lin2 e5 Thian-hu7 chai-iaN2 lin2 u7 su-iau3 chiah e5 it-chhe3 e5 mih8-kiaN7.  33) Lin2 tioh8 tai7-seng tui-kiu5 Siong7-chu2 e5 kok i2-kip8 chun-heng5 I e5 chi2-i3, I chu7-jian5 ia7 e7 chiong ki5-tha it-chhe3 e5 mih8 long2 siuN2-su3 lin2.  34) Sou2-i2 m7-thang hoan5-lo2 bin5-na2-chai3 e5 tai7-chi3. Bin5-na2-chai3 ia7 u7 leng7-goa7 e5 tai7-chi3 thang hoan5-lo2. Chit8-jit8 e5 khun3-lan5, hit jit8 lai5 tam-tng chiu7 u7 kau3-giah8.”

Te7 7 ChiuN

Phe-pheng5 pat8-lang5: (Lou7 6:37-38; 41-42)
	1) “M7-thang phe-pheng5 pat8-lang5, lin2 chiah be7 siu7 phe-pheng5;  2) in-ui7 lin2 na7 an3-choaN2 lai5 phe-pheng5 lang5, ia7 e7 an2-ne lai5 siu7 phe-pheng5. Lin2 eng7 sim2-mih chhun3-chhioh lai5 niu5 hou7 lang5, ia7 e7 eng7 kang7-khoan2 e5 chhun3-chhioh lai5 niu5 hou7 lin2.  3) Li2 an3-choaN2 kan-taN teh khoaN3 li2 e5 hiaN-ti7 bak8-chiu-lai7 e5 chhau2-sap-a2, iah bo5 chu3-i3 tioh8 li2 ka-ti7 bak8-chiu-lai7 e5 toa7 ki sam2-a2-khou?  4) Li2 ka-ti7 e5 bak8-chiu lai7 ki3-jian5 u7 sam-a2-khou, li2 an3-choaN2 kaN2 tui3 li2 e5 hiaN-ti7 kong2, ‘Goa2 ka7 li2 theh8 bak8-chiu-lai7 e5 chhau2-sap-a2 chhut-lai5.’  5) Gui7-sian7-chia2 a3! Li2 tioh8 tai7-seng chiong li2 bak8-chiu lai7 e5 toa7 ki sam-a2-khou theh8 chhut-lai5, jian5-au7 li2 chiah e7-tang3 khoaN3 kah beng5-beng5-beng5, thang theh8 li2 hiaN-ti7 bak8-chiu lai7 e5 chhau2-sap-a2 chhut-lai5.”
	6). “M7-thang chiong sin5-seng3 e5 mih8-kiaN7 theh8 hou7 kau2 chiah8---i e7 oat8 koe3-lai5 ka7 lin2 ka7! M7-thang chiong lin2 e5 chin-chu hiat toa3 ti e5 thau5-cheng5 --- i e7 eng7 kha lai5 thun2-tah8!”

Tioh8 kiu5, tioh8 chhoe7, tioh8 phah-mng5: (Lou7 11:9-13)
	7) “Tioh8 kiu5, lin2 chiu7 e7 tit-tioh8; tiohchh8oe, lin2 chiu7 e7 chhoe7-tioh8; tioh8 phah-mng5, chiu7 e7 ka7 lin2 khui.  8) In-ui7 mui2 chit8 e5 lang5 na7 kiu5, chiu7 e7 tit-tioh8; mui2 chit8 e5 lang5 na7 chhoe7, chiu7 e7 chhoe7-tioh8; mui2 chit8 e5 lang5 na7 phah-mng5, chiu7 e7 ka7 i khui.  9) Lin2 cho3 lau7-pe7 e5 lang5, ka-ti7 e5 kiaN2 ka7 li2 tho2 mi7-pau e5 si5, lin2 kam2 e7 theh8 chioh8-thau5 hou7 i?  10) A2-si7 ka7 lin2 tho2 ni5-a2 e5 si5, lin2 kam2 e7 liah8 choa5 hou7 i?  11) Lin2 sui-jian5 si7 phaiN2 e5 lang5, siong7-chhiaN2 e7-hiau2 eng7 ho2-mih8 hou7 lin2 e5 kiaN2-ji5, ho5-hong3 lin2 e5 Thian-hu7, I kam2 be7 eng7 koh-khah ho2 e5 mih8 lai5 siuN2-su3 hou7 hiah-e5 tui3 I ki5-kiu5 e5 lang5?”
	12) “Sou2-i2 bo5-lun7 ami2-mih tai7-chi3, lin2 ai3 pat8-lang5 an3-choaN2 lai5 tui3-thai7 lin2, lin2 ia7 tioh8 chiau3 an2-ne lai5 tui3-thai7 pat8-lang5! Che chiu7-si7 Mou5-se e5 Lut8-hoat i2-kip8 chiong3 tai7-gian5-jin5 e5 ka3-si7 e5 iau3-tiam2.”

Eh8 e5 mng5: (Lou7 13:24)
	13) “Tioh8 tui3 eh8 e5 mng5 jip8-khi3, in-ui7 thau3-kau3 biat8-bong5 hit e5 mng5 chinkhoah. Hit tiau5 lou7 chin ho2 kiaN5. KiaN5 hit tiau5 lou7 e5 lang5 chin che7.  14) Thau3-kau3 eng2-seng hit e5 mng5 chin eh8. Hit tiau5 lou7 chin phaiN2 kiaN5. Chhoe7 tioh8 hit tiau5 lou7 e5 lang5 chin chio2!”

Chhiu7 kap koe2-chi2: (Lou7 6:43-44)
	15) “Tioh8 keng2-kai3 ke2 tai7-gian5-jin5. In lai5 lin2 chia e5 si5, goa7-piau2 ke2 kah chhin-chhiuN7 mi5-iuN5, tan7-si7 in e5 lai7-sim chhin-chhiuN7 hiong-ok e5 chhai5-long5.  16) Lin2 khoaN3 in e5 heng5-ui5 chiu7 e7 jin7-chhut in si7 sim2-mih khoan2 e5 lang5. Tui3 chhi3-phe3 kam2 e7-tang3 ban2 phu5-to5? A2-si7 tui3 chit8-le5 kam2 e7-tang3 ban2 bu5-hoa-ko2?  17) Sou2-i2 ho2 chhiu7 long2 e7 kiat ho2 koe2-chi2. PhaiN2 chhiu7 it-teng7 e7 kiat phaiN2 koe2-chi2. 18) Ho2 chhiu7 be7 kiat phaiN2 koe2-chi2. PhaiN2 chhiu7 ia7 be7 kiat ho2 koe2-chi2.  19) Be7 kiat ho2 koe2-chi2 e5 chhiu7 long2 tioh8 chho3 khi2-lai5, hiat loh8-khi3 hoe2-nih sio.  20) Sou2-i2 khoaN3 in e5 heng5-ui5, lin2 chiu7 e7-tang3 jin7-chhut in si7 sim2-mih khoan2 e5 lang5.”

Goa2 m7-bat lin2: (Lou7 13:25-27)
	21) “M7-si7 chheng-hou Goa2 ‘Chu2 a3! Chu2 a3!’ e5 lang5, chiu7 long2 e7-tang3 chin3 jip8-khi3 Thian-kok; chi2-u7 sit8-heng5 Goa2 e5 Thian-hu7 e5 chi2-i3 e5 lang5 chiah e7 tang3 jip8-khi3.  22) Hit Jit8 kau3 e5 si5, it-teng7 u7 chin-che7 lang5 e7 tui3 Goa2 kong2, ‘hu2 a3! Chu2 a3! Goan2 kam2 m7-si7 u7 hong7 Li2 e5 mia5 thoan5 Siong7-chu2 e5 sin3-sek, u7 hong7 Li2 e5 mia5 koaN2-chhut chin-che7 kui2, iu7-koh u7 cho3 chin-che7 sin5-chek?’  23) Hit e5 si5 Goa2 boeh beng5-beng5 ka7 in kong2, ‘Goa2 long2 m7-bat lin2. Lin2 chiah-e5 bu5-ok put-chok e5 lang5! Li7-khui Goa2! Chau2! Chau2!”

Nng7-chiong2 e5 te7-ki: (Lou7 6:47-49)
	24) “Sou2-i2 it chhe3 thiaN Goa2 chiah-e5 oe7, chiau3 an2-ne khi3 sit8-heng5 e5 lang5, si7 chhin-chhiuN7 chit8 e5 chhong-beng5 e5 lang5, khi2 chhu3 khi2 toa3 chioh8-poaN5 teng2.  25) Sui-jian5 toa7-hou7 phoah, toa7-chui2 chhiong, toa7-hong sau3 hit keng chhu3, chhu3 ia7 be7 to2-khi3, in-ui7 hit keng chhu3 khi2 ti7 chioh8-poaN5 teng2.  26) It-chhe3 thiaN Goa2 chiah-e5 oe7 bo5 sit8-heng5 e5 lang5, si7 chhin-chhiuN7 chit8 e5 gong7-lang5, khi2 chhu3 khi2 toa3 soa-a2 teng2.  27) It-tan3 toa7-hou7 phoah, toa7-chui2 chhiong, toa7-hong sau3 hit keng chhu3, chhu3 chiu7 to2 loh8-khi3, ji5-chhiaN2to2 kah peN5-peN5-peN5!”

Ia5-sou e5 koan5-ui:
	28) Ia5-sou kong2 chiah-e5 oe7 soah e5 si5, cheng3-lang5 tui3 I e5 ka3-si7 long2 chin siu7 kam2-tong7,  29) in-ui7 I kau3-hun3 in e5 hoat-tou7, chhin-chhiuN7 chit8 ui7 u7 koan5-ui e5 lang5, long2 bo5 chhin-chhiuN7 in e5 keng-hak8-chia2.

Te7 8 ChiuN7

	1) Ia5-sou tui3 soaN-teng2 loh8-lai5 e5 si5, u7 kui toa7-tin7 e5 lang5 kin-toe3 I.  2) Hit e5 si5, u7 chit8 e5 ba5-hong-peN7-lang5 lai5 phak toa3 I e5 bin7-cheng5 kong2,”sin-seN a3, Li2 na7 kheng2, chiu7 e7-tang3 i-ho2 goa2 e5 peN7.”  3) Ia5-sou chiu7 chhun-chhiu2 ka7 i bong, kong2, “Goa2 tong-jian5 kheng2, hou7 li2 ho2-khi3.” Hit e5 lang5 e5 ba5-hong-peN7 sui5-si5 chiu7 ho2-khi3.  4) Ia5-sou ka7 i kong2: “Li2 choat8-tui3 m7-thang ka7 lang5 kong2, tan7-si7 tioh8 khi3 hou7 che3-si giam7, ia7 tioh8 khi3 hian3 Mou5-se sou2 kui-teng7 e5 che3-phin2, tui3 cheng3-lang5 cheng3-beng5 li2 i2-keng ho2-khi3 a3.”

Ia5-sou i-ho2 lian5-tiU82 e5 lou5-pok8: (Lou7 7:1-10)
	5) Ia5-sou jip8-khi3 Ka-pek-long5 e5 si5, u7 chit8 e5 Lo5-ma2 e5 lian5-tiuN2 lai5 kiu5 I,  6) kong2: “Sin-seN a3, goa2 e5 lou5-pok8 poan3-sui7, ti7 chhu3-nih teh to2, hui-siong5 kan-khou2.”  7) Ia5-sou chiu7 ka7 i kong2, “Goa2 boeh lai5 khi3 ka7 i i hou7 ho2.”  8) Lian5-tiuN2 in3 I kong2: “Sin-seN a3! Hou7 Li2 khi3 goan2 chhu3, goa2 tng-be7-khi2. Li2 kan-taN kong2 chit8 ku3 oe7, goa2 e5 lou5-pok8 chiu7 e7 ho2-khi3.  9) In-ui7 goa2 ia7-si7 chit8 e5 teng2-bin7 u7 siong7-si, e7-bin7 u7 peng-a2 e5 lang5. Goa2 ka7 chit e5 kong2, ‘Li2 khi3’ , i chiu7 khi3; ka7 hit e5 kong2, ‘Li2 lai5’, i chiu7 lai5; ka7 goa2 e5 lou5-pok8 kong2, ‘Li2 an2-ne cho3,’ i chiu7 an2-ne cho3.” 10) Ia5-sou thiaN-liau2 chin kam2-sim, chiu7 ka7 toe3 I e5 lang5 kong2: “Goa2 sit8-chai7 ka7 lin2 kong2,chai7 I2-sek-liat8-lang5 e5 tiong-kan, Goa2 ia7 m7-bat khoaN3-kiN3 chit8 e5 u7 chhin-chhiuN7 chit khoan2 e5 sin3-sim.  11) Goa2 koh ka7 lin2 kong2, u7 chin-che7 lang5 e7 tui3 tang-peng5 tui3 sai-peng5 lai5, boeh toa3 Thian-kok kap A-pek-lah8-han2, I2-sat, Nga2-kok cho3-hoe2 che7 toh;  12) tan7-si7 hiah-e5 eng-kai siok8 Thian-kok e5 lang5, tian-to3 e7 pi7 koaN2 chhut-khi3 goa7-bin7 ou-am3 e5 sou2-chai7. Ti7 hia in e7 thi5-khau3, ka7-ge5 chhiat-khi2.”  13) Ia5-sou chiu7 ka7 hit e5 lian5-tiuN2kong2, “Li2 tng2-khi3! Li2 sou2 sin3 e5, chiau3 an2-ne hou7 li2 seng5-chiu7.” Tu2-tu2 hit e5 si5, i e5 lou7-pok8 chiu7 ho2-khi3.

Ia5-sou i-ho2 chin-che7 lang5: (Kho2 1:29-34; Lou7 4: 38-41)
	14) Ia5-sou jip8-khi3 Pi2-tek e5 chhu3-nih e5 si5, khoaN3-kiN3 Pi2-tek e5 tiuN7-m2 tioh8 jiat8-peN7 teh to2.  15) Ia5-sou chit8-e7 bong i e5 chhiu2, jiat8 chiu7 the3-khi3; i chiu7 khi2-lai5 khai-si2 chiap-thai7 Ia5-sou.
	16) Hong5-hun e5 si5, cheng3-lang5 chhoa7 chin-che7 tioh8-iau e5 lang5 lai5 Ia5-sou hia. I eng7 chit8 ku3 oe7 chiu7 koaN2-chhut hiah-e5 sia5-sin5, ia7 i-ho2 sou2 u7 e5 peN7-lang5.  17) Che chiu7-si7 boeh eng3-giam7 tai7-gian5-jin5 I2-sai3-a sou2 kong2 e5 oe7, kong2:
“I pun2-sin the3 lan2 jim2-siu7 loan2-jiok8, tam-tng lan2 kok-chiong2 e5 peN7-cheng.”

Cho3 Ia5-sou e5 bun5-tou5 e5 iau3-kiaN7: (Lou7 9:57-62)
	18) Ia5-sou khoaN3-kiN3 chin-che7 lang5 lai5 ti7 I e5 sin-piN, chiu7 hoan-hu3 I e5 bun5-toukhui5-chun5 koe3-khi3 ou5 e5 hit-peng5 hoaN7.  19) U7 chit8 e5 keng-hak8-chia2 lai5 ka7 I kong2,”Lau7-su, Li2 bo5-lun7 khi3 tah-ui7, goa2 long2 boeh toe3 Li2 khi3.”  20) Ia5-sou in3 i kong2, “Hou5-li5 u7 khang, poe-chiau2 u7 siu7; tan7-si7 Jin5-chu2 bo5 an-sin e5 sou2-chai7.”  21) Leng7-goa7 chit8 e5 bun5-tou5 ka7 I kong2, “Sin-seN a3, hou7 goa2 tai7-seng tng2-khi3 bai5-chong3 goa2 e5 lau7-pe7.”  22) Tan7-si7 Ia5-sou in3 i kong2, “Li2 tioh8 toe3 Goa2, pang3 hou7 hiah-e5 cheng-sin5-siong7 e5 si2-lang5, khi3 bai5-chong3 in jiok8-the2-siong7 e5 si2-lang5.”

Ia5-sou tin3-ap hong-eng2: (Kho2 4:35-41; Lou7 8:22-25)
23). Ia5-sou chiuN7-chun5, I e5 bun5-tou5 chiu7 toe3 I khi3.  24) Hut-jian5-kan ou5-nih8 khi2 toa7 hong-eng2, chun5 soah giong7-giong7 boeh hou7 pho-long7 kham3-khi3; tan7-si7 Ia5-sou khun3 kah chin ho2 khun3.  25) Bun5-tou5 kin2 khi3 kio3-chheN2 Ia5-sou, kong2, “Chu2 a3, kiu3-mia7 le3! Goan2 teh-boeh bo5 mia7 lou3!”  26) Ia5-sou chiu7 ka7 in kong2, “Lin2 na2 e7 chiah-nih8 bo5 taN2? Lin2 na2 e7 chiah-nih8 bo5 sin3-sim!” I chiu7 khi2-lai5 toa7-siaN chek-pi7 hong kap eng2, hong-eng2 chiu7 sui5-si5 peng5-cheng7 khi3.  27) Cheng3-lang5 toa7 tioh8-kiaN kong2, “Chit e5 lang5 si7 sim2-mih khoan2 e5 lang5? Lian5 hong kap eng2 to sun7-chiong5 I!”

Ia5-sou i-ho2 nng7 e5 tioh8-iau e5: (Kho2 5:1-20; Lou7 8:26-39)
	28) Ia5-sou koe3-khi3 ou5 e5 hit peng5 hoaN7, khi3 kau3 Ka-tai7-liap8-lang5 e5 te7-hng e5 si5, u7 tu2-tioh8 nng7 e5 tioh8-iau e5 lang5, tui3 bong7-nih chhut-lai5. In hui-siong5 hiong-ok, sou2-i2 bo5 lang5 kaN2 tui3 hit tiau5 lou7 keng-koe3.  29) In hut-jian5-kan toa7-siaN hoah kong2, “Siong7-chu2 e5 KiaN2 a3, Li2 ho5-pit lai5 kan-siap8 goan2? Si5-hau7 iau2-boe7 kau3, Li2 chiu7 lai5 chia boeh chek-hoat8 goan2 si7 bo5?”  30) Li7 in bo5 lao7 hng7, u7 chit8 toa7 tin7 ti ti7 hia teh tho2-chiah8.  31) Hiah-e5 sia5-mou5 chiu7 kiu5 Ia5-sou kong2, “Li2 na7 boeh ka7 goan2 koaN2 chhut-khi3, chiu7 hou7 goan2 jip8-khi3 hit tin7 ti e5 lai7-bin7!”  32) Ia5-sou ka7 in kong2, “Lin2 khi3!” Hiah-e5 sia5-mou5 chiu7 li7-khui hit nng7 e5 lang5, jip8-khi3 hit tin7 ti e5 lai7-bin7. Hut-jian5-kan kui tin7 ti tui3 soaN-phiaN5 chong5 loh8-khi3 ou5-nih8, hou7 chui2 kek-si2.
	33) Chhi7-ti-e5 chiu7 chau2 khi3 kau3 siaN5-nih8, chiong it-chhe3 e5 su7-cheng5, iu5-ki5-si7 koan-he7 tioh8-iau e5 lang5 e5 tai7-chi3, long2 po3-ko3 hou7 lang5 chai-iaN2.  34) Sou2-i2 thong siaN5 e5 lang5 long2 chhut-lai5 chhoe7 Ia5-sou. In khoaN3-tioh8 Ia5-sou e5 si5 chiu7 kiu5 I li7-khui in e5 te7-hng.

Te7 9 ChiuN

Ia5-sou i-ho2 poan3-sui7 e5: (Kho2 2:1-12; Lou7 5:17-26)
	1) Ia5-sou che7 chun5 koe3 ou5, tng2-khi3 ka-ti7 e5 kou3-hiong.  2) U7 lang5 kng chit8 e5 to2 ti7 chhng5-phou-teng2 e5 poan3-sui7 e5 lai5 I e5 bin7-cheng5. Ia5-sou khoaN3-khiN3 in chiah-nih8 u7 sin3-sim, chiu7 ka7 poan3-sui7 e5 kong2, “Siau3-lian5-lang5 a3! M7-bian2 hoan5-lo2. Li2 e5 choe7 tit-tioh8 sia3-bian2 a3.”  3) U7 kui2-na7 e5 keng-hak8-chia2, sim-lai7 siuN7 kong2, “Chit e5 lang5 kong2 siat-tok8 e5 oe7!”  4) Ia5-sou khoaN3-chhut in sim-lai7 sou2 siuN7 e5 tai7-chi3 chiu7 kong2: “Lin2 sim-lai7 an3-choaN2 teh siuN7 chit khoan2 phaiN2 tai7-chi3?  5) Si7 kong2, ‘Li2 e5 choe7 tit-tioh8 sia3-bian2 a3,’ a2-si7 kong2, ‘Li2 peh khi2-lai5 kiaN5,’ tah chit8 hang7 khah iong5-i7?  6) Goa2 boeh hou7 lin2 chai-iaN2 Jin5-chu2 chai7 te7-siong7 u7 sia3-choe7 e5 koan5.” Jian5-au7 I chiu7 tui3 poan3-sui7 e5 kong2, “Khi2-lai5, gia5 li2 e5 chhng-phou tng2-khi3 lin2 chhu3!”  7) Hit e5 lang5 chiu7 khi2-lai5, tng2-khi3 in chhu3.  8) Cheng3-lang5 chit8-e7 khoaN3-kiN3 an2-ne chiu7 khi2 toa7 kiaN; in chan3-bi2 Siong7-chu2 siuN2-su3 chit khoan2 e5 koan5-peng3 hou7 lang5.

Ia5-sou keng2-tiau3 Ma2-thai3: (Kho2 2:13-17; Lou7 5:27-32)
	9) Ia5-sou li7-khui hia, I teh kiaN5 e5 si5,khoaN3-kiN3 chit8 e5 lang5, mia5 kio3-cho3 Ma2-thai3, che7 ti7 soe3-koan teh pan7-kong, chiu7 ka7 i kong2, “Lai5 toe3 Goa2!” Ma2-thai3 chiu7 peh khi2-lai5, toe3 Ia5-sou khi3.
	10) Ia5-sou ti7 Ma2-thai3 e5 chhu3-nih teh chiah8-png7 e5 si5, u7 chin-che7 thiu-soe3 e5 lang5 i2-kip8 choe7-jin5 lai5 kap Ia5-sou i2-kip8 I e5 bun5-tou5 cho3-hoe2 che7-toh.  11) Hoat-li7-sai3-phai3 e5 lang5 chit8-e7 khoaN3-kiN3, chiu7 ka7 Ia5-sou e5 bun5-tou5 kong2, “Lin2 lau7-su an3-choaN2 kap thiu-soe3 e5 lang5 i2-kip8 choe7-jin5 cho3-hoe2 chiah8-png7?”  12) Ia5-sou thiaN-kiN3, chiu7 in3 kong2: “Kian7-khong e5 lang5 bo5 khiam3-eng7 i-seng, tan7-si7 u7 peN7 e5 lang5 chiah u7 su7-iau3.  13) ‘Goa2 sou2 ai3 e5 m7-si7 che3-phin2, si7 jin5-chu5,’ Seng3-keng sou2 ki3-chai3 chit ku3 oe7 si7 sim2-mih i3-su3, lin2 khi3 gian2-kiu3 khoaN3-bai7 le3. In-ui7 Goa2 lai5 se3-kan e5 bok8-tek m7-si7 boeh keng2-tiau3 gi7-jin5, si7 boeh keng2-tiau3 choe7-jin5.”

Kona-he7 kim3-chiah8 e5 bun7-te5: (Kho2 2:18-22; Lou7 5:33-39)
	14) Jian5-au7 si-sian2-chia2 Iok-han7 e5 bun5-tou5 lai5 kiN3 Ia5-sou, mng7 I kong2, “Goan2 kap Hoat-li7-sai3-phai3 e5 lang5 siong5-siong5 kim3-chiah8. Li2 e5 bun5-tou5 an3-choaN2 long2 bo5 kim3-chiah8?”  15) Ia5-sou in3 kong2: “Sin-long5 iau2 kap in cho3-hoe2 e5 si5, chham-ka hun-ian3 e5 lang5-kheh kam2 e7 pi-siong? Tong-jian5 be7! Tan7-si7 sin-long5 e7 tui3 in e5 tiong-kan hou7 lang5 liah8-khi3, an2-ne in chiu7 e7 kim3-chiah8. Hit e5 si5 teh-boeh kau3 a3.”
	16) “Bo5 lang5 eng7 iau2-boe7 kiu-chui2 e5 pou3 lai5 pou2 ku7 saN, in-ui7 hit te3 sin pou3 e7 thiah-phoa3 ku7 saN, ji5-chhiaN2 phoa3-khang e7 pi2 i2-cheng5 koh-khah toa7.  17) Ia7 bo5 lang5 chiong sin-chiu2 te2 toa3 ku7 phoe-te7-a2 lai7; na7 an2-ne cho3, phoe5-te7-a2 e7 piak-phoa khi3, chiu2 chiu7 e7 lau5 chhut-lai5, phoe5-te7-a2 ia7 e7 sun2-hai7 khi3. Sin-chiu2 eng-kai tioh8 te2 toa3 sin e5 phoe5-te7-al2ai, an2-ne chiu2 kap phoe5-te7-a2 chiah e7-tang3 long2 po2-choan5.”

Hoe7-tng5 e5 leng2-to7-chia2 e5 cha-bou2-kiaN2 kap hiat-lau7-peN7 e5 hu7-jin5-lang5: (Kho2 5:21-43; Lou7 8:40-56)
	18) Ia5-sou tui3 in teh kong2-oe7 e5 si5, u7 chit8 e5 hoe7-tng5 e5 chu2-sek8 lai5 phak toa3 I e5 bin7-cheng5 kong2, “Goa2 e5 cha-bou2-kiaN2 tu2 si2-khi3. Tan7-si7 chhiaN2 Li2 lai5-khi3 ka7 i an3-chhiu2, i chiu7 it-teng7 e7 oah8 khi2-lai5.:  19) Ia5-sou chiu7 khi2-lai5, toe3 i khi3. I e5 bun5-tou5 ia7 toe3 khi3.
	20) Tu2 u7 chit8 e5 hoan7-tioh8 hiat-lau7-peN7 i2-keng chap8-ji7 ni5 ku2 e5 hu7-jin5-lang5, hut-jian5-kan kiaN5 oa2-lai5 Ia-sou e5 au7-bin7, bong I e5 saN-a2-ki e5 chhiu.  21) In-ui7 i sim-lai7 siuN7 kong2, “Goa2 na7 kan-taN bong-tioh8 I e5 saN, goa2 chiu7 e7 ho2-khi3.”  22) Ia5-sou oat8 koe3-lai5 khoaN3 i, ka7 i kong2, “Hu7-jin5-lang5 a3! M7-bian2 hoan5-lo2! Li2 e5 sin3-sim hou7 li2 ho2-khi3 a3.” Hit e5 si5, hu7-jin5-lang5 e5 peN7 chek-si5 ho2-khi3.
	23) Ia5-sou lai5 kau3 hit e5 hoe7-tng5 e5 chu2-sek8 e5 chhu3. I khoaN3-kiN3 chong3-sek e5 gak8-tui7 kap kui toa7 tin7 lang5 teh long7-long7-kun2,  24) chiu7 kong2, “Lin2 long2 chhut-khi3! chit e5 cha-bou2-gin2-na2 m7-si7 si2-khi3, si7 teh khun3.” In chiu7 ka7 I thi2-chhio3.  25) Chit8-e7 koaN2 cheng3-lang5 chhut-khi3 liau2-au7, Ia5-sou chiu7 jip8-khi3 cha-bou2-gin2-na2 e5 pang5-keng lai7 khan i e5 chhiu2, i chiu7 peh khi2-lai5.  26) Chit e5 siau-sit chiu7 thoan5 kau3 chit e5 te7-hng e5 kok sou2-chai7 khi3.

Ia5-sou i-ho2 nng7 e5 chheN-me5-e5:
	27) Ia5-sou li7-khui hia koh ke3-siok8 teh kiaN5 e5 si5, u7 nng7 e5 chheN-me5-e5 toe3 I khi3. In toa7-siaN hoah kong2, “Tai7-pit8 e5 kiaN2-sun, kho2-lin5 goan2!”  28) Ia5-sou jip8-khi3 chhu3-lai7, chheN-me5-e5 chiu7 lai5-kau3 I e5 bin7-cheng5. Ia5-sou ka7 in kong2, “Lin2 siong-sin3 kong2 Goa2 e7-tang3 cho3 chit hang7 tai7-chi3 si7 bo5?” In ka7 I kong2, “Sin-seN a3! Li2 it-teng7 e7!”  29) Ia5-sou chiu7 bong in e5 bak8-chiu kong2, “Chiau3 lin2 sou2 sin3 e5, ka7 lin2 seng5-chiu7.”  30) In e5 bak8-chiu chiu7 u7 khoaN3-kiN3. Ia5-sou giam5-kim3 in kong2, “Lin2 chhian-ban7 m7-thang hou7 lang5 chai-iaN2 chit hang7 tai7-chi3.”  31) Tan7-si7 in chit8-e7 chhut-khi3, chiu7 khi3 hit te7-hng e5 kok sou2-chai7 soan-thoan5 Ia5-sou e5 tai7-chi3.

Ia5-sou i-ho2 chit8 e5 e2-kau2-e5:
	32) Ia5-sou kap in teh-boeh chhut-khi3 e5 si5, u7 lang5 chhoa7 chit8 e5 tioh8-iau be7 kong2-oe7 e5 lang5 lai5 Ia5-sou hia.  33) Hit e5 iau-mou5 chit8-e7 hou7 Ia5-sou koaN2 chhut-khi3, hit e5 lang5 chiu7 sui5-si5 e7 kong2-oe7. Cheng3-lang5 long2 tioh8-kiaN kong2, “Ti7 i2-sek-liat8 goan2 iau2 m7-bat khoaN3-kiN3 chhin-chhiuN7 chit khoan2 e5 tai7-chi3.”  34) Tan7-si7 Hoat-li7-sai3-phai3 e5 lang5 kong2, “I si7 oa2-kho3 Mou5-kui2-ong5 e5 se3-lek8 lai5 teh koaN2-kui2.”

Ia5-sou lin5-gin2 cheng-lang5:
	35) Ia5-sou kiaN5-thau3 kok siaN5-chhi7 kok hiong-chhoan, toa3 in e5 hoe7-tng5 lai7 kau3-hun3 lang5, soan-iong5 Thian-kok e5 Hok-im, i-ho2 it-chhe3 e5 cheng3-thau5 peN7-thiaN3.  36) I chit8-e7 khoaN3-kiN3 hiah toa7 tin7 e5 kun5-chiong3, chiu7 lin5-bin2 in; in-ui7 in iu-chhiu5 song3-khi3, chhin-chhiuN7 bo5 bok8-chia2 e5 iuN5-kun5.  37) Ia5-sou chiu7 ka7 I e5 bun5-tou5 kong2, “Tioh8 siu-koah e5 chin hong-hu3, tan7-si7 siu-koah e5 kang-lang5 chin chio2.  38) Sou2-i2 lin2 tioh8 kiu5 chhan5-thau5-ke phai3 khah che7 kang-lang5 khi3 ka7 i siu-seng5.”

Te7 10 ChiuN

Ia5-sou e5 chap8-ji7 e5 su3-tou5: (Kho2 3:13-19; Lou7 6:12-16)
	1) Ia5-sou tiau3-chip I e5 chap8-ji7 e5 bun5-tou5 lai5, siuN2-su3 in koan5-peng3 thang koaN2 sia5-sin5 i2-kip8 i-ti7 it-chhe3 e5 cheng3-thau5 peN7-thiaN3.  2) Chit chap8-ji7 e5 Su3-tou5 e5 mia5 chiu7-si7:
	Te7-it e5 si7 Se-bun5, (piat8-ho7 kio3-cho3 Pi2-tek); kap i e5 sio2-ti7 An-tek-liat8; Se-pi2-thai3 e5 kiaN2 Nga2-kok; kap i e5 sio2-ti7 Iok-han7;  3) Hui-lek8, kap Pa-to-lo5-mai2; To-ma2, kap thiu-soe3 e5 lang5 Ma2-thai3; Nga2-kok, chiu7-si7 A-lek8-hui e5 kiaN2, kap Tat8-thai3;  4) Ai3-kok tong2-oan5 e5 Se-bun5; kap au7-lai5 chhut-be7 Ia5-sou hit e5 Ka-liok8 e5 Iu5-tai7.

Chap8-ji7 Su3-to5 e5 su3-beng7: (Kho2 6:7-13; Lou7 9:1-6)
	5) Ia5-sou chhe-phai3 chit chap8-ji7 e5 lang5 chhut-khi3, hoan-hu3 in kong2: “M7-thang hong2-bun7 Goa7-pang-lang5 e5 te7-hng, ia7 m7-thang jip8-khi3 Sat-ma2-li7-a-lang5 e5 siaN5-chhi7.  6) Lin2 eng-kai tioh8 khi3 chhoe7 I2-sek-liat8-chok8 sit-be5 e5 iuN5.  7) Lin2 tioh8 na2 kiaN5 na2 soan-iong5 kong2, ‘Thian-kok teh-boeh kau3 a3!’  8) Tioh8 i-ti7 peN7-lang5, hou7 si2-lang5 kok-oah8, tioh8 i-ho2 ba5-hong-peN7 e5 lang5, tioh8 koaN2-kui2.  Lin2 bian2-hui3 tit-tioh8 e5, ia7 tioh8 bian2-hui3 hou7 lang5.  9) Te7-a2 lai7 m7-thang toa3 kim, gin5 a2-si7 tang5-chiN5;  10) m7-thang toa3 li2-heng5-te7, m7-thang ke toa3 lai7-saN, m7-thang toa3 e5, m7-thang giah8 koai2-a2; in-ui7 cho3-kang e5 lang5 tit-tioh8 i sou2 su-iau3 e5 si7 tong-jian5 e5.”
	11) “Lin2 bo5-lun7 jip8-khi3 tah chit8 e5 siaN5-chhi7, tah chit8 e5 hiong-chhoan, tioh8 chhoe7 khoaN3 u7 sim2-mih sek-tong3 e5 lang5, chiu7 toa3 in chhu3, toa3 kau3 lin2 li7-khui hit e5 te7-hng.  12) Lin2 jip8-khi3 i e5 chhu3, tioh8 ka7 hit e5 ka-teng5 e5 lang5 kong2, ‘Goan7 lin2 peng5-an.’  13) Hit e5 ka-teng5 na7 e7 kham-tit, lin2 e5 chiok-hok chiu7 e7 seng5-hau7; na7 be7 kham-tit, lin2 e5 chiok-hok chiu7 e7 to3-tng2 lai5 kui lin2.  14) Na7 u7 lang5 m7 hoan-geng5 lin2, m7 thiaN lin2 kong2 e5 oe7, lin2 li7-khui hit keng chhu3 a2-si7 hit e5 siaN5-chhi7 e5 si5, kha e5 thou5-hun2 long2 tioh8 poaN7 hou7 i chheng-khi3.  15) Goa2 sit8-chai7 ka7 lin2 kong2, chai7 Sim2-phoaN3 e5 Jit8-chi2, hit e5 siaN5-chhi7 sou2 siu7 e5 chek-hoat8, it-teng7 e7 pi2 Sou2-to-ma2 kap Gou5-mou5--lah8-siaN5 sou2 siu7 e5 khah tang7!”

Pek-hai7 e5 lai5-lim5: (Kho2 13:9-13; Lou7 21:12-17)
	16) Lin2 tioh8 chu3-i3 thiaN! Goa2 chhe-phai3 lin2 chhut-khi3, chhin-chhiuN7 sang3 iuN5 jip8-khi3 chhai5-long5 e5 tiong-kan. Sou2-i2 lin2 tioh8 chhin-chhiuN7 choa5 hiah-nih8 leng5-khiau2, chhin-chhiuN7 hun2-chiau2 hiah-nih8 sun5-liong5.  17) Tioh8 hong5-pi7, in-ui7 lang5 e7 liah8 lin2 khi3 kau hou7 kong-gi7-hoe7, ia7 e7 toa3 in e5 hoe7-tng5 eng7 piN phah lin2.  18) Peng3-chhiaN2 lin2 e7 in-ui7 Goa2 e5 ian5-kou3 hou7 lang5 thoa-khi3 kau3 chong2-tok kap kun-ong5 e5 bin7-cheng5, hou7 lin2 u7 ki-hoe7 thang tui3 Iu5-thai3-lang5 kap goa7-pang-lang5 ui7 Goa2 cho3 kian3-cheng3.  19) In liah8 lin2 khi3 sim2-phoaN3 e5 si5, lin2 m7-bian2 hoan5-lo2 boeh an3-choaN2 kong2, a2-si7 boeh kong2 sim2-mih; in-ui7 hit e5 si5 na7 kau3, Seng3 Leng5 e7 chi2-si7 lin2 tioh8 kong2 sim2-mih.  20) Su7-sit8-siong7 teh kong2-oe7 e5 m7-si7 lin2 ka-ti7, si7 lin2 Thian-hu7 e5 Segn3 Leng5 toa3 ti7 lin2 lai7-bin7 teh kong2 e5.”
	21) “HiaN-ti7 e7 chhut-be7 hiaN-ti7 hou7 i khi3 si2. Lau7-pe7 ia7 e7 an2-ne hou7 i e5 kiaN2-ji5 khi3 si2. Kia2-ji5 e7 khi2-lai5 kong-kek pe7-bo2, kau in khi3 hou7 lang5 chhu2-si2.  22) Lin2 ui7-tioh8 Goa2, e7 hou7 cheng3-lang5 oan3-hin7. Tan7-si7 kian-jim2 kau3 choe3-au7 e5 lang5, it-teng7 e7 tit-tioh8 kiu3.  23) Lang5 na7 ti7 chit e5 siaN5-chhi7 pek-hai7 lin2, lin2 tioh8 chau2-khi3 pat8 e5 siaN5-chhi7. Goa2 sit8-chai7 ka7 lin2 kong2, lin2 iau2-boe7 kiaN5-thau3 I2-sek-liat8 mui2 chit8 e5 siaN5-chhi7, Jin5-chu2 chiu7 e7 kau3.”
	24) “Bo5 chit8 e5 hak8-seng pi2 lau7-su khahgau5, bo5 chit8 e5 lou5-pok8 pi2 chu2-lang5 khah toa7.  25) Hak8-seng na7 e7-tang3 chhin-chhiuN7 lau7-su, lou5-pok8 na7 e7-tang3 chhin-chhiuN7 chu2-lang5, an2-ne chiu7 tioh8 boan2-chiok a3. Chit8 ke e5 chu2-lang5 na7 hou7 lang5 me7 cho3 kui2-ong5 Piat8-se-pok, i e5 ka-chok8 kam2 be7 hou7 lang5 me7 koh-khah phaiN2-thiaN!”

Tioh8-keng3-ui3 Siong7-chu2: (Lou7 12:2-7)
	26) “Sou2-i2 lin2 m7-thang kiaN hiah-e5 lang5. Mui2 chit8 hang7 kham3-bat8 e5 su7, au7-lai5 it-teng7 e7 lou7-hian7 chhut-lai5. Mui2 chit8 hang7 pi3-bit8 e5 su7, au7-lai5 it-teng7 e7 hou7 lang5 chai-iaN2.  27) Goa2 ti7 am3-tiong ka7 lin2 kong2 e5, lin2 tioh8 toa3 kng-thiN peh8-jit8 e5 sou2-chai7 kong2 chhut-lai5. Se3-siaN ka7 lin2 kong2 e5, tioh8 toa3 chhu3-teng2 kong-khai soan-pou3 chhut-lai5.  28) M7-bian2 kiaN hiah-e5 chi2-u7 e7-tang3 sat-hai7 jiok8-sin, tan7-si7 bo5 leng5-lek8 thang hai7-si2 leng5-hun5 e5 lang5. Chi2-u7 tioh8 kiaN Siong7-chu2. I u7 leng5-lek8 e7-tang3 hui2-biat8 ti7 te7-gak8 e5 leng5-hun5 kap jiok8-sin.  29) Chit8 kak-gin5 kam2 m7-si7 e7-tang3 be2 nng7 chiah chhek-chiau2-a2? Tan7-si7 na7 bo5 lin2 e5 Thian-hu7 e5 tong5-i3, lian5 chit8 chiah chhek-chiau2-a2 ia7 be7 poah8 loh8-lai5 thou5-kha.  30) Thian-hu7 lian5 lin2 e5 thau5-mng5 ma7 chit8 ki chit8 ki ka7 lin2 sng3 koe3 a3.  31) Sou2-i2 lin2 chian-ban7 m7-bian2 kiaN, in-ui7 lin2 pi2 kui tin7 e5 chhek-chiau2-a2 koh-khah u7 ke3-tat8!”

Kong-khai seng5-jin7 Ki-tok: (Lou7 12:8-9)
	32) “It-chhe3 ti7 lang5 e5 bin7-cheng5 kong-khai seng5-jin7 Goa2 e5 lang5, Goa2 ia7 boeh toa3 Goa2 e5 Thian-hu7 e5 bin7-cheng5 seng5-jin7 i.  33) It-chhe3 ti7 lang5 e5 bin7-cheng5 m7 seng5-jin7 Goa2 e5 lang5, Goa2 toa3 Goa2 e5 Thian-hu7 e5 bin7-cheng5 ia7 m7 seng5-jin7 i.”

M7-si7 ho5-peng5, si7 to-kiam3: (Lou7 12:51-53; 14:26-27)
	34) “M7-thang siuN7 kong2 Goa2 lai5 si7 boeh hou7 se3-kan ho5-peng5; Goa2 lai5 m7-si7 toa3 ho5-peng5 lai5, si7 toa3 to-kiam3 lai5.  35) Goa2 lai5 chiu7-si7 boeh hou7 kiaN2 ngou2-gek8 i e5 lau7-pe7, hou7 cha-bou2-kiaN2 hoan2-khong3 i e5 lau7-bo2, hou7 sim-pu7 hoan2-gek8 i e5 ta-ke;  36) su7-sit8-siong7 lang5 e5 tek8-jin5 chiu7-si7 i ka-ti7 ke -lai7 e5 lang5.”
	37) “Keng3-ai3 pe7-bo2 iaN5-koe3 keng3-ai3 Goa2 e5 lang5, be7-kham-tit cho3 Goa2 e5 bun5-tou5; thiaN3 kiaN2-ji5 khah iaN5-koe3 keng3-ai3 Goa2 e5, be7-kham-tit cho3 Goa2 e5 bun5-tou5.  38) M7 poe7 ka-ti7 e5 sip8-ji7-ke3 lai5 toe3 Goa2 kiaN5 e5 lang5, ia7 be7-kham-tit cho3 Goa2 e5 bun5-tou5.  39) Ai3 po2-choan5 ka-ti7 e5 seN3-mia7 e5 lang5, tian-to3 e7 song3-sit seN3-mia7; ui7-tioh8 Goa2 lai5 hi-seng ka-ti7 e5 seN3-mia7 e5 lang5, tian-to3 e7 tit-tioh8 seN3-mia7.”

Po3-siuN2: (Kho2 9:41)
	40) “Hoan-geng5 lin2 e5 lang5 chiu7-si7 hoan-geng5 Goa2; hoan-geng5 Goa2 e5 lang5 chiu7-si7 hoan-geng5 chhe-phai3 goa2 lai5 Hit-ui7.  41) Chiong chit8 e5 tai7-gian5-jint, khoaN3-cho3 tai7-gian5-jin5 lai5 ka7 i hoan-geng5 e5 lang5, e7 hun-hiong2 tai7-gian5-jin5 e5 po3-siuN2; chiong chit8 e5 gi7-jin5, khoaN3-cho3 gi7-jin5 lai5 ka7 i hoan-geng5 e5 lang5, e7 hun-hiong2 gi7-jin5 e5 po3-siuN2.  42) Goa2 sit8-chaik7a lin2 kong2, na7 u7 lang5 tai3-liam7 i si7 Goa2 e5 bun5-tou5, lai5 phang5 chit8 poe leng2-chui2 hou7 bun5-tou5 tiong siong7 se3 e5 chit8 e5 lim, chit e5 lang5 it-teng7 e7 tit-tioh8 po3-siuN2.”

Te7 11 ChiuN

Si-sian2-chia2 Iok-han7 e5 Su3-chia2: (Lou7 7:18-35)
	1) Ia5-sou ka7 I chap8-ji7 e5 bun5-tou5 hoan-hu3 chiah-e5 tai7-chi3 liau2-au7, chiu7 li7-khui hia, khi3 hu7-kin7 e5 siaN5-chhi7 kau3-hun3 lang5, tui3 in soan-iong5 Hok-im.
	2) Iok-han7 ti7 kaN-gak8 lai7 thiaN-kiN3 Ki-tok sou2 cho3 e5 tai7-chi3, chiu7 chhe i e5 bun5-tou5 khi3 mng7 Ia5-sou kong2,  3) “Li2 chiu7-si7 Iok-han7 sou2 kong2 teh-boeh lai5 Hit-ui7 a2 m7-si7? A2-si7 goan2 tioh8 koh tan2 leng7-goa7 chit8 ui7?”  4) Ia5-sou in3 kong2: “Chiong lin2 sou2 khoaN3-kiN3, sou2 thiaN-kiN3 e5, tng2-khi3 ka7 Iok-han7 po3-ko3:  5) chiu7-si7 chheN-me5-e5 u7 khoaN3-kiN3, pai2-kha-e5 e7 kiaN5-lou7, ba5-hong-peN7 e5 lang5 ho2-khi3, chhau3-hiN7-lang5 u7 thiaN-kiN3, si2-lang5 koh-oah8 khi2-lai5, san3-chhiah-lang5 thiaN-tioh8 Hok-im a.  6) Bo5 hoai5-gi5 Goa2 e5 lang5, sit8-chai7 u7 hok-khi3!"
	7) Iok-han7 e5 bun5-tou5 teh-boeh tng2-khi3 e5 si5, Ia5-sou khai-si2 tui3 cheng3-lang5 kong2-khi2 Iok-han7 e5 tia7-chi3. I kong2: “Lin2 chhut-khi3 khong3-ia2 si7 boeh khoaN3 sim2-mih? Si7 hou7 hong chhoe tin2-tang7 e5 lou5-tek a2 m7-si7?  8) Lin2 kiu3-keng3 si7 chhut-khi3 khoaN3 sim2-mih? Si7 khi3 khoaN3 chheng7 chhia-hoa e5 i-hok8 e5 lang5 a2 m7-si7? Na7-si7 chheng7 chit khoan2 chhia-hoa e5 i-hok e5 lang5 si7 toa3 ti7 ong5-kiong lai7!  9) An2-ne lin2 kiu3-keng3 si7 chhut-khi3 boeh khoaN3 sim2-mih? Si7 boeh khoaN3 tai7-gian5-jin5 a2 m7-si7? Si7 la3! Goa2 ka7 lin2 kong2, i pi2 tai7-gian5-jin5 koh-khah ui2-tai7.  10) Koan-he7 chit e5 lang5, Seng3-keng u7 ki3-chai3 kong2:
‘Lin2 khoaN3, Goa2 boeh chhe Goa2 e5 su3-chia2 cho3 Li2 e5 thau5-cheng5. I boeh cho3 Li2 e5 sian-hong chun2-pi7 Li2 e5 to7-lou7.’
11) goa2 sit8-chai7 ka7 lin2 kong2, iu2-su2 i2-lai5 m7-bat u7 chit8 e5 lang5 pi2 si-sian2-chia2 Iok-han7 koh-khah ui2-tai7. Tan7-si7 chai7 thian-kok siong7 se3 e5, iau2 pi2 i koh-khah ui2-tai7.  12) Tui3 si-sian2-chia2 Iok-han7 chhut-lai5 thoan5-to7 hit e5 si5 kau3 hian7-chai7, Thian-kok siu7 tioh8 kiong5-beng2 e5 kong-kek, Kiong5-beng2 e5 lang5 kek-liatboeh8 chhiuN2-toat8 Thian-kok.  13) In-ui7 chiong3 tai7-gian5-jin5 i2-kip8 Mou5-se e5 Lut8-hoat long2 i7-gian5 kau3 Iok-han7 e5 si5 ui5-chi2.  14) Lin2 na7 goan7-i3 chiap-siu7 chiah-e5 i7-gian5, Iok-han7 chiu7-si7 hit-ui7 it-teng7 boeh lai5 e5 I2-li7-a.  15) U7 hiN7-khang thang thiaN e5 lang5, tioh8 thiaN!”
	16) “Chit e5 se3-tai7 e5 lang5 Goa2 tau3-te2 tioh8 eng7 sim2-mih lai5 pi2-pheng7? In tu2 chhin-chhiuN7 chit8 tin7 gin2-na2 che7 ti7 chhi7-tiuN5 lai7 teh tui3 in e5 tang5-phoaN7 hoah kong2:
17) ‘goan2 ui7-tioh8 lin2 chau3 kiat-hun e5 im-gak8, lin2 ia7 bo5 boeh thiau3-bu2; goan2 ui7-tioh8 lin2 chhiuN3 chong3-sek e5 ai-koa, lin2 ia7 bo5 boeh pi-siong!’
18) Iok-han7 lai5, ia7 kim3-chiah8 ia7 bo5 lim-chiu2, lang5 chiu7 kong2, ‘I teh khi2-siau2!’  19) Jin5-chu2 lai5, ia7 u7 chiah8 ia7 u7 lim, lang5 chiu7 kong2, ‘Li2 khoaN3! chit e5 tham-chiah8 houN3-chiu2 e5 lang5, si7 thiu-soe3 e5 lang5 kap choe7-jin5 e5 peng5-iu2!’ Tan7-si7 Siong7-chu2 e5 ti3-hui7 si7 eng7 hit e5 ti3-hui7 e5 seng5-ko2 lai5 cheng3-sit8 e5.”

M7 hoe3-kai2 e5 siaN5-chhi7: (Lou7 10:13-15)
	20) Ia5-sou i2-keng ti7 hiah-e5 siaN5-chhi7 cho3 hiah che7 sin5-chek, tan7-si7 in iau2-ku2 long2 bo5 hoe3-kai2, sou2-i2 I chiu7 chek-pi7 in kong2:  21) “Ko-liap8-sin3-lang5 a3, lin2 u7 chai-ho7! Pek-sai3-tai7-lang5 a3, lin2 u7 chai-ho7! In-ui7 ti7 lin2 e5 tiong-kan sou2 cho3 e5 sin5-chek, na7 ti7 Chhui-lo5 kap Se-tun3 cho3, in cha2-cha2 chiu7 chheng7 moa5-saN sam2 hoe2-hu lai5 hoe3-kai2 a3.  22) Goa2 koh ka7 lin2 kong2, chai7 Sim2-phoaN3 e5 Jit8, Chhui-lo5 kap Se-tun3 e7 pi2 lin2 siu7 khah khin e5 heng5-hoat8!  23) Iah li2, Ka-pek-long5 a3! Li2 siuN7 boeh siu7 theh8-ko kau3 thiN-teng2 a2 m7-si7? Li2 it-teng7 e7 pi7 tan3 loh8-khi3 kau3 im-kan, in-ui7 ti7 lin2 tiong-kan sou2 cho3 e5 sin5-chek, na7 ti7 Sou2-to-ma2 cho3, chit e5 siaN5 it-teng7 e7 chun5-chai7 kau3 kin-na2-jit8.  24) Goa2 koh keng2-ko3 lin2, chai7 Sim2-phoaN3 e5 Jit8, Sou2-to-ma2 e7 pi2 lin2 siu7 khah khin e5 heng5-hoat8!”

Lai5 Goa2 chia an-sek: (Lou7 10:21-22)
	25) Hit e5 si5 Ia5-sou ki5-to2 kong2: “Hu7-chhin, thiN-te7 e5 Chu2-chaiN2 a3! Goa2 kam2-sia7 Li2, in-ui7 Li2 chiong chiah-e5 su7, tui3 u7 ti3-hui7 kap u7 hak8-bun7 e5 lang5 am-kham3 khi2-lai5, tui3 tan-sun5 e5 lang5 khe2-si7 chhut-lai5.  26) Hu7-chhin a3! Goa2 sit8-chai7 kam2-sia7 Li2, in-ui7 che long2 si7 chiau3 Li2 e5 ho2-i3 lai5 cho3 e5.”
	27) “Goa2 e5 Thian-hu7 i2-keng chiong it-chhe3 long2 kau-thok goa2.  Thian-hu7 i2-goa7 bo5 lang5 chin-chiaN3 bat KiaN2. Ti5-liau2 KiaN2 kap KiaN2 sou2 boeh khe2-si7 e5 lang5 i2-goa7, bo5 lang54 chin-chiaN3 bat Thian-hu7.”
	28) Lin2 chiah-e5 teh lo5-khou2 taN tang7-taN3 e5, long2 tioh8 lai5 chhoe7 Goa2. Goa2 chiu7 boeh hou7 lin2 the5-sin5 kai2-lo5.  29) In-ui7 Goa2 e5 sim-koaN un-jiu5 khiam-sun3, sou2-i2 lin2 tioh8 gia5 Goa2 e5 ke5 lai5 tui3 Goa2 hak8-sip8, lin2 e5 leng5-hun5 chiu7 e7 tit-tioh8 peng5-an.  30) Goa2 e5 ke5 si7 iong5-i7 gia5 e5. Goa2 boeh hou7 lin2 taN e5 taN3 si7 khin-sang e5.”

Te7 12 ChiuN

Koan-he7 An-hioh-jit8 e5 pian7-lun7: (Kho2 2:23-28; Lou7 6:1-5)
	1) U7 chit8 e5 An-hioh-jit8, Ia5-sou tui3 beh8-a2-hng5 keng-koe3. I e5 bun5-tou5 pak-tou2 iau, chiu7 khai-si2 tiah beh8-a2-sui7 lai5 chiah8.  2) Hoat-li7-sai3-phai3 e5 lang5 chit8-e7 khoaN3-kiN3, chiu7 ka7 Ia5-sou kong2, “Li2 khoaN3! Li2 e5 bun5-tou5 cho3 An-hioh-jit8 sou2 m7 eng-kai cho3 e5 tai7-chi3.”  3) Ia5-sou chiu7 in3 kong2: “Lin2 kam2 m7-bat thak8-tioh8 koan-he7 Tai7-pit8 kap i e5 pou7-ha7 pak-tou2 iau e5 si5 sou2 cho3 e5 tai7-chi3?  4) I jip8-khi3 Siong7-chu2 e5 seng3-tian7 chiah8 che3-toaN5-teng2 e5 mi7-pau. chiau3 Lut8-hoat chi2-u7 che3-si chiah u7 chu-keh thang chiah8 hian3-che3 e5 mi7-pau. Tai7-pit8 kap i e5 pou7-ha7 m7 eng-kai chiah8.  5) A2-si7, Lin2 kam2 m7-bat ti7 Mou5-se e5 Lut8-hoat thak8-tioh8 kong2, mui2 chit8 e5 An-hioh-jit8 che3-si ti7 seng3-tian7 lai7 ui7-tioh8 hian3-che3, sit8-che3-siong7 u7 hoan7-tioh8 An-hioh-jit8 e5 Lut8-hoat, tan7-si7 bo5 sng3-cho3 hoan7-hoat.  6) TaN Goa2 ka7 lin2 kong2, ti7 chia u7 chit8 hang7 pi2 Seng3-tian7 koh-khahtiong7-iau3 e5 tai7-chi3.  7) “Goa2 sou2 ai3 e5 m7-si7 che3-hian3, si7 jin5-chu5.’ Lin2 na7 chin-chiaN3 u7 liau2-kai2 chit ku3 oe7 i3-su3, lin2 chiu7 be7 ka7 bo5 choe7 e5 lang5 teng7-choe7;  8) in-ui7 Jin5-chu2 si7 An-hioh-jit8 e5 Chu2.”

Ia5-sou i-ho2 khoe5-chhiu2-e5: (Kho2 3:1-6; Lou7 6:6-11)
	9) Ia5-sou li7-khui hit e5 sou2-chai7, jip8-khi3 in e5 hoe7-tng5.  10) Ti7 hia tu2 u7 chit8 e5 khoe5-chhiu2 e5 lang5. U7 chit8-koa2 lang5 siuN7-boeh chhoe7 khang-phang7 lai5 ko3 Ia5-sou, chiu7 mng7 I kong2, “An-hioh-jit8 i-peN7 u7 hap8-hoat a2 bo5?”  11). Ia5-sou in3 kong2: “Ka2-su2 lin2 tiong-kan u7 lang5 u7 chit8 chiah iuN5-a2, An-hioh-jit8 poah8 loh8-khi3 chhim-khut e5 lai7-bin7, lin2 kam2 be7 ka7 i thoa khi2-lai5?  12) Lang5 pi2 iuN5-a2 ke chin u7 ke3-tat8! Sou2-i2 An-hioh-jit8 cho3 ho2-su7 si7 hap8-hoat e5.”  13) Ia5-sou chiu7 ka7 hit e5 lang5 kong2, “Chhiu2 chhun chhut-lai5!” I chit8-e7 chhun chhut-khi3, hit ki chhiu2 chiu7 hok8-goan5 kap i iau2 chit8 ki chhiu2 kang7-khoan2.  14) Hoat-li7-sai3-phai3 e5 lang5 chhut-khi3, chiu7 ke3-bou5 boeh an3-choaN2 lai5 hai7-si2 Ia5-sou.

Siong7-chu2 sou2 keng2-soan2 e5 lou5-pok8:
	15) Ia5-sou chai-iaN2 in e5 ke3-bou5, chiu7 li7-khui hit e5 sou2-chai7. U7 chin-che7 lang5 toe3 I khi3. I i-ho2 in it-chhe3 u7 peN7 e5 lang5.  16) Tan7-si7 I kim3-chi2 in m7-thang kong-piau2 I e5 sin-hun7.  17) Che si7 ui7-tioh8 boeh eng3-giam7 tai7-gian5-jin5 I2-sai3-a sou2 kong2 e5 oe7, kong2:
18) “Li2 khoaN3, Goa2 e5 lou5-pok8, I si7 Goa2 keng2-soan2 e5.  I si7 Goa2 sou2 thiong2-ai3 e5 . Goa2 chin-chiaN3 kah-i3 e5.  Goa2 boeh chiong Goa2 e5 Seng3 Leng5 siuN2-su3 I.  I e7 tui3 ban7-bin5 soan-pou3 Goa2 e5 sim2-phoaN3.  19) I bo5 bopeh cheng-lun7, ia7 bo5 boeh toa7-siaN jiang2.  I ia7 bo5 boeh toa3 ke-lou7 toa7-siaN ian2-kang2.  20) Khiau khi3 e5 lou5-tek-a2, I bo5 boeh at-chih8.  Teh-boeh hoa e5 teng-sim, I ia7 bo5 boeh pun5-sit.  I e7 kian-chhi5 kau3 hou7 kong-gi7 tit-tioh8 seng3-li7.  21) Ban7-bin5 e7 giong2-bong7 I.”

Ia5-sou kap kui2-ong5 Piat8-se-pok: (Kho2 3:20-30; Lou7 11:14-23)
	22) Jian5-au7 u7 lang5 chhoa7 chit8 e5 in-ui7 tioh8-iau, chheN-me5 koh e2-kau2 e5 lang5 lai5 Ia5-sou hia. Ia5-sou ka7 i i-ho2, i chiu7 e7 kong2-oe7, ia7 u7 khoaN3-kiN3.  23) Cheng3-lang5 long2 chin tioh8-kiaN kong2, “Chit e5 lang5 kam2 m7-si7 Tai7-pit8 e5 kiaN2-sun?”  24) Tan7-si7 Hoat-li7-sai3-phai3 e5 lang5 chit8-e7 thiaN kiN3 chiu7 in3 kong2, “Chit e5 lang5 put-ko3 si7 kho3 kui2-ong5 Piat8-se-pok e5 se3-lek8 lai5 teh koaN2-kui2.”  25) Ia5-sou chai-iaN2 in sim-lai7 teh siuN7 e5 tai7-chi3, chiu7 tui3 in kong2: “Kok-ka na7 khi2 lai7-loan7, it-teng7 e7 biat8-bong5. Na7-si7 siaN5-chhi7 a2-si7 ka-t6 khi2 hun-cheng, chiu7 be7-tang3 chun5-siok8.  26) Sat-tan3 na7 koaN2 Sat-tan3, chiu7-si7 ka-ti7 kong-kek ka-ti7, an2-ne Sat-tan3 e5 ong5-kok kam2 khia7 e7 tiau5?  27) Goa2 na7-si7 kho3 Piat8-se-pok e5 se3-lek8 lai5 koaN2-kui2, an2-ne lin2 e5 tou5-te7 si7 kho3 sim2-mih lang5 e5 se3-lek8 lai5 koaN2-kui2? Lin2 ka-ti7 e5 tou5-te7 e7 hoan2-pok lin2 e5 koan-tiam2!  28) Tan7-si7 Goa2 si7 oa2-kho3 Siong7-chu2 e5 Leng5 lai5 koaN2-kui2 e5, an2-ne si7 cheng3-beng5 Siong7-chu2 e5 kok i2-keng lai5-kau3 lin2 e5 tiong-kan a3.”
	29) “Bo5 lang5 e7-tang3 chhim jip8-khi3 iong2-su7 e5 chhu3 kiap i e5 chai5-but8. Na7 boeh, i tioh8 tai7-seng pak8 hit e5 iong2-su7 khi2-lai5, jian5-au7 chiah e7-tang3 kiap i chhu3-lai7 e5 chhai5-but8.”
	30) “Na7 bo5 kap Goa2 kang7 sim-chi3 e5, chiu7-si7 hoan2-tui3 Goa2; bo5 hiap8-chou7 Goa2 e5 kang-chok e5, chiu7-si7 teh pho3-hoai7.  31) In-ui7 an2-ne Goa2 ka7 lin2 kong2: lang5 bo5-lun7 hoan7-tioh8 sim2-mih choe7, lian5 hui2-pong3 e5 choe7, ia7 long2 e7 tit-tioh8 sia3-bian2; tan7-si7 siat-tok8 Seng3 Leng5 e5 choe7 it-teng7 be7 tit-tioh8 sia3-bian2.  32) Lang5 na7 kong2-oe7 kong-kek Jin5-chu2, iau2 e7 tit-tioh8 sia3-bian2; tan7-si7 kong2-oe7 kong-kek Seng3 Leng5 e5, bo5-lun7 ti7 hian7-se3 a2-si7 lai5-se3, to be7 tit-tioh8 sia3-bian2.”

Chhiu7 kap i e5 koe2-chi2: (Lou7 6:43-45)
	33) “Ho2 chhiu7 kiat ho2 koe2-chi2. PhaiN2 chhiu7 kiat phaiN2 koe2-chi2. KhoaN3 koe2-chi2 chiu7 e7-tang3 chai-iaN2 chhiu7 e5 ho2-phaiN2.  34) Lin2 chiah-e5 tok8-choa5 a3! Lin2 beng5-beng5 si7 phaiN2 lang5, an3-choaN2 e7-tang3 kong2 ho2 oe7? In-ui7 lang5 sou2 kong2-chhut e5 oe7, long2 si7 tui3 i e5 sim-koaN liu5-lou7 chhut-lai5 e5.  35) Ho2 lang5 tui3 i ka-ti7 sou2 chek-chu7 e5 liong5-sian7 hian2-chhut liong5-sian7. PhaiN2 lang5 tui3 i ka-ti7 sou2 siu-chun5 e5 sia5-ok lou7-chhut sia5-ok.”
	36) “Goa2 koh ka7 lin2 kong2: lang5 lam7-sam2 kong2 e5 oe7, chai7 Sim2-phoaN3 e5 Jit8-chi2 tak8 ku3 long2 tioh8 hu7 chek-jim7;  37) in-ui7 kin-ki3 li2 sou2 kong2 e5 oe7, boeh sim2-phoaN3 li2 u7 choe7 a2-si7 bo5 choe7.”
	38) U7 kui2-na7 e5 keng-hak8-chia2 kap Hoat-li7-sai3-phai3 e5 lang5 tui3 Ia5-sou kong2, “Lau7-su, goan2 ai3 khoaN3 Li2 cho3 chit8 e5 sin5-chek.”  39) Ia5-sou chiu7 in3-tap in kong2: “Chit e5 se3-tai7 e7 lang5 na2 e7 chiah-nih8 sia5-ok koh bo5 sin3-sim! Lin2 ai3 Goa2 cho3 sin5-chek a2 m7-si7? Tai7-gian5-jin5 Iok-na2 e5 sin5-chek i2-goa7, Siong7-chu2 bo5 boeh siuN2-su3 sin5-chek hou7 chit se3-tai7 e5 lang5 khoaN3!  40) Tu2 chhin-chhiuN7 Iok-na2 saN-me5 saN-jit8 toa3 toa7-hi5 e5 pak-tou2 lai7, Jin5-chu2 ia7 e7 saN-me5 saN-jit8 toa3 thou5-kha-te2.  41) Chai7 Sim2-phoaN3 e5 Jit8-chi2, Ni5-ni5-bi5-lang5 e7 kap chit e5 se3-tai7 e5 lang5 cho3-hoe2 oah8 khi2-lai5 khong3-ko3 chit se3-tai7 e5 lang5; in-ui7 Ni5-ni5-bi5-lang5 thiaN Iok-na2 e5 thoan5-to7 liau2-au7 long2 u7 hoe3-kai2. Lin2 khoaN3, ti7 chia u7 chit8-ui7 pi2 Iok-nakoh2-khah ui2-tai7 e5!  42) Chai7 Sim2-phoaN3 e5 Jit8-chi2, lam5-hng e5 li2-ong5 e7 kap chit se3-tai7 e5 lang5 cho3-hoe2 oah8 khi2-lai5 khong3-ko3 chit se3-tai7 e5 lang5; in-ui7 li2-ong5 u7 tui3 thiN-piN hai2-kak lai5 thiaN Sou2-lo5-bun5-ong5 e5 ti3-hui7 e5 oe7. Lin2 khoaN3, ti7 chia u7 Chit8-ui7 pi2 Sou2-lo5-bun5 koh-khah ui2-tai7 e5!”

Sia5-sin5 to3-tng2 lai5: (Lou7 11:24-26)
	43) “Sia5-sin5 li7-khui lang5 liau2-au7 chiu7 khi3 khong3-ia2 si3-ke3 chhoe7 chit8 e5 sou2-chai7 thang hiu-sek. Sia5-sin5 chhoe7 bo5,  44) chiu7 kong2, ‘Goa2 boeh to3-tng2 khi3 goa2 chhut-lai5 e5 chhu3,’ Tng2-khi3 kau3 hia, khoaN3-kiN3 chhu3-lai7 khang-khang, sau3 kah chin chheng-khi3, ia7 cheng2-li2 kah chin ho2-se3,  45) i chiu7 koh chhut-khi3, chhoa7 chhit e5 pi2 i khah sia5-ok e5 lai5, jip8-khi3 hia cho3-hoe2 toa3. Hit e5 lang5 e5 kiat-kiok8 chiu7 pi2 i2-cheng5 koh-khah pi-chham2. Chit e5 sia5-ok e5 se3-tai7 ia7 e7 chhin-chhiuN7 an2-ne.”

Ia5-sou e5 bo2-chhin kap hiaN-ti7: (Kho2 3:31-35; Lou7 8:19-21)
	46) Ia5-sou iau2 teh tui3 cheng3-lang5 kong2-oe7 e5 si5, I e5 lau7-bo2 kap hiaN-ti7 lai5. In khia7 ti7 goa7-bin7 ai3 boeh kap I kong2-oe7.  47) U7 lang5 ka7 Ia5-sou kong2, “Li2 khoaN3! Li2 e5 lau7-bo2 kap Li2 e5 hiaN-ti7 ti7 goa7-bin7 teh tan2 boeh kap Li2 kong2-oe7.”  48) I chiu7 in3 hit e5 lang5 kong2, “Sim2-mih lang5 si7 Goa2 e5 lau7-bo2? Sim2-mih lang5 si7 Goa2 e5 hiaN-ti7?”  49) I chiu7 chhun-chhiu2 ki2 I hiah-e5 bun5-tou5 kong2: “Li2 khoaN3! Chiah-e5 chiu7-si7 Goa2 e5 lau7-bo2, Goa2 e5 hiaN-ti7!  50) Bo5-lun7 sim2-mih lang5 na7 chun-heng5 Goa2 e5 Thian-hu7 e5 chi2-i3, i chiu7-si7 Goa2 e5 hiaN-ti7, Goa2 e5 chi2-moe7, Goa2 e5 lau7-bo2.”

Te7 13 ChiuN

Ia7 cheng2-chi2 e5 phi3-ju7: (Kho2 4:1-9; Lou7 8:4-8)
	1) Kang7 hit jit8 Ia5-sou chhut-mng5, khi3 kau3 ou5-piN teh che7.  2) In-ui7 u7 chin toa7 tin7 e5 lang5 chu7-chip8 lai5 I hia, I soah tioh8 chiuN7-chun5, che7 ti7 chun5-lai7, cheng3-lang5 long2 khia7 ti7 hoaN7-nih8.  3) Ia5-sou chiu7 eng7 phi3-ju7 ka3-si7 in chin-che7 tai7-chi3.
	I kong2: “U7 chit8 pai2 u7 chit8 e5 long5-hu chhut-khi3 ia7 cheng2-chi2.  4) I teh ia7 cheng2-chi2 e5 si5, u7-e5 ka-lauh8 ti7 lou7-piN, chiau2-a2 poe-lai5, chiu7 ka7 i chiah8 liau2-liau2.  5) U7-e5 ka-lauh8 ti7 chioh8-thau5-a2 te7, thou5-bah chhian e5 sou2-chai7. In-ui7 thou5-bah bo5 chhim, cheng2-chi2 chin kin2 chiu7 puh-ge5.  6) TaN iam7-jit8 chit8-e7 phak8, iN2 soah ta-khi3, in-ui7 kin teng3 bo5 chin chhim.  7) Ia7 u7-e5 ka-lauh8 ti7 chhi3-a2 lai7, chhi3-a2 chit8-e7 toa7-chang5 khi2-lai5, iN2 chiu7 hou7 i hip-si2.  8) Tan7-si7 u7-e5 ka-lauh8 ti7 ho2 e5 thou5-bah, chiu7 kiat-sit8, u7-e5 kiat chit8 pah poe7, u7-e5 kiat lak8-chap8 poe7, u7-e5 kiat saN-chap8 poe7.  9) TaN lin2 u7 hiN7-khang thang thiaN e5 lang5 tioh8 thiaN!”

Ia5-sou eng7 phi3-ju7 e5 bok8-tek: (Kho2 4:10-12; Lou7 8:9-10)
	10) Bun5-tou5 lai5 Ia5-sou hia, mng7 I kong2, “Li2 ka3-si7 in e5 si5, an3-choaN2 tioh8 eng7 phi3-ju7?”  11) Ia5-sou in3 kong2: “In-ui7 Siong7-chu2 i2-keng u7 siuN2-su3 lin2 tek8-koan5 lai5 jim7-sek Thian-kok e5 o3-pi3, tan7-si7 bo5 siuN2-su3 in.  12) In-ui7 tui3 u7 e5 lang5, Siong7-chu2 e7 siuN2-su3 i koh-khah che7, hou7 i hu3-ju7 kah u7 thang chhun. Tan7-si7 tui3 bo5 e5 lang5, lian5 i sou2 u7 e5 chit8-sut-la2 ia7 e7 ka7 i chhiuN2-toat8 khi3.  13) In-ui7 in khoaN3 ia7 khoaN3be7 tioh8, thiaN ia7 thiaN be7 beng5, ia7 thiaN be7 liau2-kai2, sou2-i2 Goa2 chiah tioh8 eng7 phi3-ju7 ka7 in kong2.  14) In tu2-tu2 eng3-giam7 tai7-gian5-jin5 I2-sai3-a sou2 kong2 e5 oe7, kong2:
‘Lin2 thiaN sit8-chai7 u7 teh thiaN, tan7-si7 long2 be7 liau2-kai2; lin2 khoaN3 u7 chu3-i3 teh khoaN3, tan7-si7 long2 be7 beng5-pek8.  15) In-ui7 chit e5 bin5-chok8 e5 sim piN3-cho3 chin tun7; in e5 hiN7-khang piN3-cho3 chin tang7; in e5 bak8-chiu pang3 kheh-kheh; kiaN-liau2 in e5 bak8-chiu u7 khoaN3-kiN3, in e5 hiN7-khang u7 thiaN-kiN3, in e5 sim e7 li2-kai2, in e7 hoe3-kai2, lai5 hou7 Goa2 ka7 in i-ho2 khi3.’”
16) Kong2 kah lin2, lin2 sit8-chai7 chin u7 hok-khi3! In-ui7 lin2 e5 bak8-chiu u7 khoaN3-kiN3. Lin2 e5 hiN7-a2 ia7 u7 thiaN-kiN3.  17) Goa2 sit8-chai7 ka7 lin2 kong: i2-cheng5 u7 chin-che7 tai7-gian5-jin5 kap gi7-jin5 chin ai3 khoaN3 lin2 sou2 teh khoaN3 e5, tan7-si7 khoaN3 bo5 tioh8, chin ai3 thiaN lin2 sou2 teh thiaN e5, tan7-si7 thiaN bo5 tioh8.”

Ia5-sou kai2-sek ia7 cheng2-chi2 e5 phi3-ju7: (Kho2 4:13-20; Lou7 8:11-15)
	18) “TaN lin2 tioh8 chu3-i3 thiaN Goa2 kai2-sek chit e5 ia7 cheng2-chi2 e5 phi3-ju7.  19) ThiaN Thian-kok e5 to7-li2, bo5 sit8-chai7 liau2-kai2, chit khoan2 e5 lang5, si7 chhin-chhiuN7 ia7 ti7 lou7-piN e5 cheng2-chi2. Mou5-kui2 chit8-e7 kau3, chiu7 chiong ia7 ti7 i sim-lai7 e5 to7-li2 ka7 i chhiuN2-khi3.  20) Chit8-e7 thiaN-tioh8 to7-li2 chiu7 sui5-si5 hoaN-hi2 chiap-siu7, chit khoan2 e5 lang5, si7 chhin-chhiuN7ia7 ti7 chioh8-thau5-a2 te7 e5 cheng2-chi2.  21) Chit e5 cheng2-chi2 bo5 teng3-kin, sou2-i2 oah8 be7 ku2, chhin-chhiuN7 an2-ne, chit khoan2 lang5 it-tan3 ui7-tioh8 chin-to7 lai5 tu2-tioh8 kan-lan5 a2-si7 pek-hai7, sui5-si5 chiu7 pang3-sak to7-li2.  22) ThiaN tioh8 to7-li2 liau2-au7, in-ui7 siu7-tioh8 chit se3-kan e5 khoa3-li7 i2-kip8 chiN5-chai5 e5 be5-hek8, chiong sou2 thiaN e5 to7-li2 jia-kham3 khi2-lai5, soah long2 be7 kiat koe2-chi2, chit khoan2 e5 lang5, si7 chhin-chhiuN7 ia7 ti7 chhi3-a2 lai7 e5 cheng2-chi2.  23) Tan7-si7 thiaN to7-li2 e7 li2-kai2 e5 lang5, si7 chhin-chhiuN7 ia7 ti7 ho2 thou5-bah e5 cheng2-chi2; u7-e5 kiat-sit8 chit8 pah poe7, u7-e5 lak8-chap8 poe7, u7-e5 saN-chap8 poe7.”

Phe7-a2 e5 phi3-ju7:
	24) Ia5-sou koh ka7 in kong2 chit8 e5 phi3-ju7: “Thian-kok chhin-chhiuN7 lang5 chiong ho2 e5 cheng2-chi2 ia7 ti7 i e5 hng5-nih8.  25) U7 chit8 am3 lang5 long2 khun3-khi3 e5 si5, i e5 tek8-jin5 lai5 ka7 i ia7 phe7-a2 toa3 beh8-hng5 lai7 chiu7 chau2-khi3.  26) Beh8-a2 chiam7-chiam7 toa7-chang5, chhut-sui7 e5 si5, phe7-a2 ia7 chhut-hian7.  27) Long5-hu lai5 po3-ko3 i e5 chu2-lang5 kong2: ‘Thau5-ke a3, li2 kam2 m7-si7 ia7 ho2 cheng2-chi2 ti7 li2 e5 hng5-nih8? Hiah-e5 phe7-a2 si7 tui3 tah-ui7 lai5 e5?’  28) chu2-lang5 in3 kong2, “Che si7 tek8-jin5 sou2 cho3 e5.’ Long5-hu chiu7 kong2, ‘An2-ne li2 ai3 goan2 khi3 khau hiah-e5 phe7-a2 khi2-lai5 bo5?’  29) Chu2-lang5 in3 kong2: ‘M7-bian2, kiaN-liau2 lin2 khau phe7-a2 e5 si5, lian5 beh8-a2 soah khau khi2-lai5.  30) Hou7 beh8-a2 kap phe7-a2 tang5-che5 toak7au siu-tang e5 si5, hit e5 si5 goa2 e7 ka7 siu-koah e5 lang5 kong2: lin2 tai7-seng chiong phe7-a2 khau khi2-lai5, khun2 kui pe2 hiat loh8-khi3 hoe2-nih sio. Jian5-au7 chiah chiong beh8-a2 siu jip8-khi3 goa2 e5 chhng-khou3.’”

Koa3-chhai2-chi2 e5 phi3-ju7: (Kho2 4:30-32; Lou7 13:18-19)
	31) Ia5-sou koh ka7 in kong2 leng7-goa7 chit8 e5 phi3-ju7: “Thian-kok chhin-chhiuN7 chit8 liap8 koa3-chhai3-chi2, si7 sou2 u7 e5 cheng2-chi2 tiong siong7-se3 liap8 e5.  32) Lang5 theh8-khi3 ia7 toa3 hng5-nih8, kau3 toa7 chang5 khi2-lai5, pi2 sou2 u7 e5 chhai3-lui7 to khah toa7 chang5, sim7-chi3 chhin-chhiuN7 chhiu7-a2, lian5 khong-tiong e5 chiau2-a2 to poe lai5 hioh toa3 i e5 chhiu7-ki cho3 siu7.”

KaN3-bo2 e5 phi3-ju7: (Lou7 13:20-21)
	33) Ia5-sou koh ka7 in kong2 iau2 chit8 e5 phi3-ju7: “Thian-kok chhin-chhiuN7 kaN3-bo2. Hu7-jin5-lang5 theh8 chit e5 kaN3-bo2 khi3 chham toa3 saN tau2 mi7-hun2 e5 lai7-bin7, hou7 i long2 hoat khi2-lai5.”

Ia5-sou su2-iong7 phi3-ju7: (Kho2 4:33-34)
	34) Ia5-sou tui3 cheng3-lang5 kong2 chiah-e5 tai7-chi3 e5 si5 long2 si7 eng7 phi3-ju7. I tak8-pai2 kap in kong2-oe7 e5 si5, su7-sit8-siong7 long2 u7 eng7 phi3-ju7.  35) I an2-ne cho3 si7 boeh eng3-giam7 tai7-gian5-jin5 sou2 kong2 e5 oe7, kong2: 
“ Goa2 boeh eng7 phi3-ju7 lai5 tui3 in kong2. Goa2 boeh ka7 in kong2 tui3 chhong3-cho7 u2-tiu7 i2-lai5 e5 o3-pi3.”

Ia5-sou kai2-sek phe7-a2 e5 phi3-ju7:
	36) Jian5-au7 Ia5-sou li7-khui cheng3-lang5, jip8-khi3 chhu3-lai7. I e5 bun5-tou5 lai5 ka7 I kong2, “ChhiaN2 Li2 ka7 goan2 kai2-sek hng5-lai7 phe7-a2 e5 phi3-ju7.”  37) I chiu7 ka7 in kong2: “Hit e5 ia7 ho2 cheng2-chi2 e5, si7 teh chi2 Jin5-chu2;  38) hng5 si7 piau2-si7 se3-kai3; ho2 cheng2-chi2 si7 teh chiThian2-kok e5 peh-seN3; phe7-a2 piau2-si7 Mou5-kui2 e5 pou7-ha7;  39) hit e5 lai5 ia7 phe7-a2 e5 tek8-jin5, si7 teh chi2 Mou5-kui2. Siu-tang e5 si5, si7 piau2-si7 se3-kai3 e5 boat8-jit8; siu-koah e5 lang5, si7 teh chi2 thian-sai3.  40) Chai7 se3-kai3 e5 boat8-jit8 sou2 e7 hoat-seng e5 tai7-chi3, tu2 chhin-chhiuN7 phe7-a2 hou7 lang5 khun2 kui pe2 khi2-lai5 eng7 hoe2 sio an2-ne.  41) Jin5-chu2 e7 chhe-phai3 I e5 chiong3 thian-sai3 khi3 I e5 Ong5-kok, chiong it-chhe3 hai7 lang5 hoan7-choe7 e5 lang5 i2-kip8 it-chhe3 put-hoat e5 lang5, ka7 in liah8-liah8 choch3…t tui,  42) ka7 in hiat jip8-khi3 iam7-jiat8 e5 hoe2-io5 lai7. In e7 toa3 hia thi5-khau3 ka7-ge5 chhiat-khi2.  43) Jian5-au7 gi7-jin5 e7 toa3 in e5 Thian-hu7 e5 Ong5-kok chhin-chhiuN7 jit8-thau5 hoat-kng. U7 hiN7-khang thang thiaN e5 lang5, tioh8 chu3-i3 thiaN!”

Un2-chong5 e5 po2-poe3:
	44) “Thian-kok chhin-chhiuN7 po2-poe3 tai5 ti7 hng5-lai7. U7 chit8 e5 lang5 hoat-kian3 tioh8, chiu7 koh ka7 i kham3 khi2-lai5, hoaN-hoaN-hi2-hi2 khi3 be7 i sou2 u7 e5 it-chhe3, khi3 be2 hit te3 heng5.”

Chin-chu e5 chi3-ju7:
	45) “Thian-kok ia7 chhin-chhiuN7 chit8 e5 seng-li2-lang5, teh chhoe7 chin ho2 e5 chin-chu.  46) I chit8-e7 chhoe7-tioh8 chit8 liap3 po2-kui3 e5 chin-chu, chiu7 khi3 be7 i sou2 u7 e5 it-chhe3, lai5 be2 hit liap8 chin-chu.”

Hi5-bang7-a2 e5 phi3-ju7:
	47) “Thian-kok ia7 chhin-chhiuN7 pha ti7 hai2-nih e5 bang7-a2, teh liah8 kok-chiong2 e5 hi5.  48) Bang7 chit8-e7 moa2, hi5-hu chiu7 thoa bang7 khi2-lai5 phiaN5-teng2, che7 loh8-khi3, keng2 ho2 e5, khng3 toa3 na5-a2 lai7; chiong m7-ho2 e5, tan3 hiat-tiau7.  49) Chai7 se3-kai3 e5 boat8-jit8 ia7 e7 chhin-chhiuN7 an2-ne; thian-sai3 e7 chhut-lai5 chiong gi7-jin5 kap phaiN2-lang5 hun-khui,  50) chiong phaiN2-lang5 hiat jip8-khi3 iam7-jiat8 e5 hoe2-io5 lai7. In e7 toa3 hia thi5-khau3 ka7-ge5 chhiat-khi2.”

Sin kap ku7 e5 chin-li2:
	51) Ia5-sou mng7 I e5 bun5-tou5 kong2, “Chiah-e5 kau3-hun3 lin2 e7 beng5-pek8 be7?” In in3 kong2, “E7.”  52) Ia5-sou chiu7 tui3 in kong2: “Sou2-i2 mui2 chit8 e5 keng-hak8-chia2 na7 cheng-thong Thian-kok e5 to7-li2, chiu7 chhin-chhiuN7 chit8 ke e5 chu2-lang5, tui3 i e5 chhng-khou3 poaN sin e5 kap ku7 e5 mih8-kiaN7 chhut-lai5.”

Ia5-sou chai7 Na2-sat-lek8 pi7 khi3-choat8: (Kho2 6:1-6; Lou7 4:16-30)
	53) Ia5-sou kong2 chiah-e5 phi3-ju7 liau2-au7, chiu7 li7-khui hia.  54) I tng2-khi3 ka-ti7 e5 kou3-hiong. I toa3 hoe7-tng5-lai7 kau3-hun3 lang5, hou7 thiaN-kiN3 e5 lang5 chin tioh8-kiaN kong2: “I tui3 tah-ui7 tit-tioh8 chit khoan2 e5 ti3-hui7 kap chit khoan2 cho3 sin5-chek e5 tai7-leng5?  55) Chit e5 lang5 kam2 m7-si7 bak8-chhiuN7 e5 kiaN2? I e5 lau7-bo2 kam2 m7-si7 kio3-cho3 Ma2-li7-a? I e5 hiaN-ti7 kam2 m7-si7 kio3-cho3 Nga2-kok, Iok-sek, Se-bun5 kap Iu5-tai7?  56) I e5 chi2-moe7 kam2 m7-si7 long2 toa3 ti7 lan2 chia? An2-ne I chiah-e5 pun2-leng2 si7 tui3 tah-ui7 lai5 e5?”  57) In chiu7 tui3 I khi2 hoan2-kam2. Tan7-si7 Ia5-sou ka7 in kong2: “Tai7-gian5-jin5 ti7 ka-ti7 e5 kou3-hiong pun2-ke i2-goa7, khi3 kau3 tah-ui7 to siu7 lang5 chun-keng3.”  58) Ia5-sou in-ui7 in bo5 sin3-sim, sou2-i2 ti7 hia bo5 cho3 chin-che7 sin5-chek.

Te7 14 ChiuN

Si-sian2-chia2 Iok-han7 e5 si2-bong5: (Kho2 6:14-29; Lou7 9:7-9)
	1) Hit e5 si5, Ka-li7-li7 Seng2 e5 thong2-ti7-chia2 Hi-lut8 thiaN-kiN3 Ia5-sou e5 mia5-siaN,  2) chiu7 ka7 i e5 pou7-ha7 kong2: “Chit e5 lang5 chiu7-si7 si-sian2-chia2 Iok-han7. I tui3 si2-lang5 e5 tiong-kan koh-oah8 khi2-lai5; sou2-i2 i chiah u7 cho3 chiah-e5 sin5-chek e5 leng5-lek8.”
	3) I2-cheng5 Hi-lut8 u7 liah8 Iok-han7 eng7 lian7-a2 lian7 khi2-lai5, ka7 i koaiN-loh8 kaN-gak8. Hi-lut8 an2-ne cho3 si7 in-ui7 boeh be2 i e5 sio2-ti7 Hui-lek8 e5 bou2 Hi-lo5-ti2 e5 hoan-sim.  4) In-ui7 Iok-han7 u7 siong5-siong5 ka7 Hi-lut8 tiong-ko3 kong2, “Li2 m7 eng-kai chiam3 chit e5 hu7-jin5-lang5 lai cho3 bou2.”  5) Hi-lut8 pun2-lai5 si7 ai3-boeh ka7 i thai5-si2, m7-ku2 kiaN peh-seN3, in-ui7 in long2 siuN7 kong2 Iok-han7 si7 Siong7-chu2 e5 tai7-gian5-jin5.
	6) Chai7 Hi-lut8 cho3 seN-jit8 hit chit8 jit8, Hi-lo5-ti2 e5 cha-bou2-kiaN2 ti7 lai5-pin e5 bin7-cheng5 thiau3-bu2, hou7 Hi-lut8 hui-siong5 hoaN-hi2.  7) In-ui7 an2-ne, Hi-lut8 chiu7 tui3 i soan-se3 kong2: “Li2 bo5-lun7 iau-kiu5 sim2-mih, goa2 long2 boeh hou7 li2!”  8) I hou7 in lau7-bo2 sai2-so7, chiu7 iau-kiu5 kong2, “ChhiaN2 chiong si-sian2-chia2 Iok-han7 e5 thau5-khak he7 toa3 poaN5-nih8, phang5 lai5 hou7 goa2!”  9) Chit8-e7 thiaN-tioh8 an2-ne, ong5 chiu7 chin3-the3 liong2-lan5, m7-ku2 in-ui7 i i2-keng ti7 lai5-pin e5 bin7-cheng5 u7 soan-se3, sou2-i2 i chiu7 beng7-leng7 lang5 chiau3 chit e5 cha-bou2-gin2-na2 e5 iau-kiu5 khi3 cho3.  10) I phai3 chit8 e5 cham2-siu2 khi3 kaN-gak8 cham2 Iok-han7 e5 thau5.  11) Cham2-siu2 chiong Iok-han7 e5 thau5-khak khng3 toa3 poaN5-nih8 san3-lai5 hou7 cha-bou2-gin2-na2. Cha-bou2-gin2-na2 chiu7 phang5 khi3 hou7 in lau7-bo2.  12) Iok-han7 e5 bun5-tou5 chiu7 lai5 siu i e5 sin-si, khi3 ka7 i bai5-chong3, jian5-au7 khi3 ka7 Ia5-sou po3-ko3 sou2 hoat-seng e5 tai7-chi3.

Ia5-sou hou7 gou7-chheng lang5 chiah8 kah pa2: (Kho2 6:30-44; Lou7 9:10-17; Iok 6:1-14)
	13) Ia5-sou thiaN-kiN3 chit e5 tai7-chi3, chiu7 che7-chun5 li7-khui hia, ka7-ti7 chit8 e5 khi3 phian-phiah e5 sou2-chai7. Cheng3-lang5 chai-iaN2, chiu7 li7-khui in e5 siaN5-chhi7 sun7 liok8-lou7 toe3 I khi3.  14) Ia5-sou chit8-e7 loh8-chun5, khoaN3-kiN3 hiahtoa7 tin7 lang5, chiu7 lin5-bin2 in, i-ho2 in tiong-kan u7 peN7 e5 lang5.
	15) Boeh-am3-a2-si5, bun5-tou5 lai5 ka7 I kong2: “Chia si7 chin phian-phiah e5 sou2-chai7, si5-kan ia7 bo5 cha2 a3. ChhiaN2 kai2-san3 cheng3-lang5, thang hou7 in ka-ti7 khi3 chng-thau5 be2 chiah8-mih8.”  16) Ia5-sou hoe5-tap kong2, “M7-bian2 hou7 in khi3; lin2 tioh8 siat-hoat hou7 in chiah8.”  17) Bun5-tou5 tui3 I kong2, “Lan2 chia chi2-u7 gou7 ki mi7-pau kap nng7 boe2 hi5 na7-tiaN7.”  18) Ia5-sou ka7 in kong2, “Lin2 theh8 lai5 hou7 Goa2.”  19) Ia5-sou chiu7 kio3 cheng3-lang5 che7 toa3 chhau2-pou, jian5-au7 theh8 hit gou7 ki mi7-pau kap nng7 boe2 hi5 khi2-lai5, giong2-bong7 thiN lai5 kam2-sia7 Siong7-chu2 siuN2-su3 chiah-e5 chiah8-mih8. Jian5-au7 I chiu7 chiong mi7-pau peh cho3 chit8 te3 chit8 te3, theh8 hou7 bun5-tou5, bun5-tou5 chiu7 pun hou7 cheng3-lang5.  20) Cheng3-lang5 long2 chiah8 kah chin pa2. Au7-lai5 bun5-tou5 chiong chiah8 chhun e5, siu-chip8 khi2-lai5, long2-chong2 u7 chap8-ji7 lang2 moa2-moa2.  21) Chiah8 e5 lang5, hu7-jin5-lang5 kap gin2-na2 bo5 sng3, tai7-iok u7 gou7-chheng lang5.

Ia5-sou kiaN5 chui2-bin7: (Kho2 6:45-52; Iok 6:15-21)
	22) Ia5-sou sui5-si5 kio3 bun5-tou5 che7-chun5 tai7-seng koe3-khi3 hit peng5 poaN7. I ka-ti7 lau5 toa3 hia lai5 kai2-san3 cheng3-lang5.  23) I sang3 cheng3-lang5 tng2-khi3 liau2-au7, chiu7 ka-ti7 chit8 e5 chiuN7-soaN ki5-to2. ThiN i2-keng am3 a3, chi2-u7 I chit8 e5 iau2 ti7 hia.  24) Hit e5 si5 bun5-tou5 sou2 che7 e5 chun5 i2-keng kau3 ou5 e5 tiong-ng a, in-ui7 chiN3-hong, hou7 hong-eng2 phah-lai5 phah-khi3.  25) Thau3-cha2 chha-put-to saN tiam2 hit e5 si5, Ia5-sou kiaN5 chui2-bin7 lai5 kau3 in hia.  26) Bun5-tou5 chit8-e7 khoaN3-kiN3 I ti7 chui2-bin7 teh kiaN5, chiu7 kiaN kah phih8-phih8-chhoah toa7-siaN hoah kong2, “Kui2 lai5 lo3!”  27) Ia5-sou chiu7 sui5-si5 ka7 in kong2, “Lin2 hong3-sim, si7 Goa2! M7-bian2 kiaN!”  28) Pi2-tek in3 I kong2, “Chu2 a3, na7 sit8-chai7 si7 Li2, chiu7 beng7-leng7 goa2 kiaN5 chui2-bin7 khi3-kau3 Li2 hia.”  29) Ia5-sou kong2, “Lai5!” Pi2-tek chiu7 tui3 chun5 loh8-khi3, khai-si2 kiaN5 chui2-bin7 boeh khi3 Ia5-sou hia.  30) Tan7-si7 i chit8-e7 khoaN3-kiN3 hong hiah-nih8 kiong5, chiu7 khi2 kiaN-hiaN5, giong7-giong7 boeh tim5 loh8-khi3.  I toa7-siaN hoah kong2, “Chu2 a3, kiu3-mia7 ou3!”  31) Ia5-sou sui5-si5 chhun chhiu2 ka7 i khiu2-le3, tui3 i kong2, “Li2 na2 e7 chiah-nih8 bo5 sin3-sim! Li2 an3-choaN2 giau5-gi5?”  32) In nng7 e5 peh khit-khi3 chun5-teng2 liau2-au7, hong chiu7 peng5-cheng7.  33) Ti7 chun5-nih8 e5 bun5-tou5 phak loh8-khi3 keng3-pai3 I kong2, “Li2 chin-chiaN3 si7 Siong7-chu2 e5 KiaN2!”

Ia5-sou chai7 Kek-ni5-sat-lek8 i-ho2 peN7-lang5: (Kho2 6:53-56)
	34) In i2-keng koe3 ou5, chiu7 toa3 Kek-ni5-sat-lek8 te7-hng chiuN7-liok8.  35) Hit e5 te7-hng e5 lang5 chit8-e7 jin7-chhut I si7 Ia5-sou, chiu7 chhe lang5 khi3 hit hu7-kin7 e5 kok te7-hng, chhoa7 it-chhe3 u7 peN7 e5 lang5 lai5 Ia5-sou hia.  36) In kiu5 Ia5-sou chi3-chio2 hou7 peN7-lang5 bong I e5 saN-a2-ki e5 chhiu; it-chhe3 u7 bong-tioh8 e5 lang5, in e5 peN7 long2 ho2-khi3.

Te7 15 ChiuN

Chou2-sian e5 thoan5-thong2: (Kho2 7:1-13)
