	1) U7 chit8 pai2, u7 chit8-koa2 Hoat-li7-sai3-phai3 e5 lang5 kap keng-hak8-chia2, tui3 Ia5-lou7-sat-leng2 lai5 mng7 Ia5-sou kong2:  2) “Li2 e5 bun5-tou5 an3-choaN2 ui5-hoan7 tioh8 chou2-sian e5 thoan5-thong2? In-ui7 in boeh chiah8-png7 i2-cheng5 bo5 chiau3 Lut8-hoat e5 kui-teng7 se2 chhiu2.”  3) Ia5-sou chiu7 in3 kong2: “lin2 an3-choaN2 ui7-tioh8 boeh chip-siu2 lin2 e5 thong5-thong2 lai5 ui5-hoan7 Siong7-chu2 e5 kai3-beng7?  4) In-ui7 Siong7-chu2 u7 kong2, ‘Tioh8 hau3-keng3 pe7-bo2,’ iu7-koh kong2, ‘Me7 lau7-pe7 a2-si7 lau7-bo2 e5 lang5 it-teng7 tioh8 chhu2 si2-heng5!’  5) Tan7-si7 lin2 chu2-tiuN kong2, ‘Lang5 na7 tui3 lau7-pe7 a2-si7 lau7-bo2 kong2: li2 pun2-lai5 e7-tang3 tui3 goa2 tit-tioh8 e5 hu5-iong2-hui3, goa2 i2-keng long2 hian3 hou7 Siong7-chu2 a3. An2-ne i chiu7 m7-bian2 hau3-keng3 pe7-bo2 a3.’  6) Lin2 ui7-tioh8 boeh chun-siu2 lin2 e5 thoan5-thong2, soah lai5 bu5-si7 tioh8 Siong7-chu2 e5 oe7.  7) Lin2 chiah-e5 gui7-sian7-chia2 a3! I2-sai3-a koan-he7 lin2 e5 i7-gian5, sit8-chai7 bo5 chho3; i kong2:
8) ‘Chiah-e5 peh-seN3 eng7 chhui3-tun5-phoe5 chun-kegn3 Goa2, tan7-si7 in e5 sim li7-khui Goa2 chin hng7.  9) In tui3 Goa2 e5 keng3-pai3 si7 khang-hi e5, in-ui7 in eng7 lang5 e5 kui-lut8 chun2 cho3 Siong7-chu2 e5 kai3-beng7 lai5 ka3-si7 lang5,’”

Lun7 chheng-khi3 kap bo5 chheng-khi3: (Kho2 7:14-23)
	10) Jian5-au7 Ia5-sou kio3 cheng3-lang5 lai5 ka7 in kong2: “Lin2 tioh8 thiaN, tioh8 liau2-kai2.  11) M7-si7 tui3 chhui3 jip8-khi3 e5, e7 hou7 lang5 bo5 chheng-khi3, si7 tui3 chhui3 chhut-lai5 e5, e7 hou7 lang5 bo5 chheng-khi3.”
	12) Hit e5 si5 bun5-tou5 lai5 ka7 Ia5-sou kong2, “Hoat-li7-sai3-phai3 e5 lang5 thiaN-kiN3 Li2 sou2 kong2 e5 oe7, chin hun3-khai3, Li2 chai-iaN2 bo5?”  13) Ia5-sou in3 kong2: “Na7 m7-si7 goa2 e5 Thian-hu7 sou2 cheng3 e5, long2 e7 ka7 i khau khi2-lai5.  14) Chhut-chai7 in khi3 kong2. In si7 chheN-me5-e5 teh khan chheN-me5-e5! Na7-si7 chheN-me5-e5 khan chheN-me5-e5, nng7 e5 long2 e7 poah8 loh8-khi3 khut-a2.”  15) Pi2-tek chiu7 tui3 I kong2, “ChhiaN2 Li2 ka7 goan2 kai2-sek chit e5 phi3-ju7.”  16) Ia5-sou chiu7 kong2: “Lian5 lin2 ia7 hiah-nih8 tun7 si7 bo5?  17) Lin2 kam2 m7-chai-iaN2 tui3 chhui3 jip8-khi3 e5, long2 tai7-seng loh8-khi3 kau3 pak-tou2, au7-lai5 chiah pang3 chhut-lai5.  18) Tan7-si7 tui3 chhui3 chhut-lai5 e5, chiu7-si7 tui3 sim-lai7 chhut-lai5 e5; che chiah e7 hou7 lang5 bo5 chheng-khi3.  19) In-ui7 tui3 sim-lai7 chhut-lai5 e5 phaiN2 i3-liam7 e7 in2-khi2 lang5 sat-jin5, su-thong, im5-loan7, cho3-chhat8, gui7-cheng3 kap hui2-pong3.  20) Chit khoan2 tai7-chi3 chiah chin-chiaN3 e7 hou7 lang5 bo5 chheng-khi3. Bo5 chiau3 kui-teng7 bo5 se2 chhiu2 lai5 chiah8-mih8, be7 hou7 lang5 bo5 chheng-khi3.”

U7 chit8 e5 hu7-jin5-lang5 e5 sin3-sim: (Kho2 7:24-30)
	21) Ia5-sou li7-khui hit e5 sou2-chai7, the3-khi3 kau3 Chhui-lo5 kap Se-tun3 e5 keng2-kai3.  22) U7 chit8 e5 toa3 ti7 hit te7-hng e5 Ka-lam5 e5 hu7-jin5-lang5 chhut-lai5, toa7-siaN hoah kong2: “Sin-seN a3, Tai7-pit8 e5 kiaN2-sun, kho2-lin5 goa2! Goa2 e5 cha-bou2-kiaN2 tioh8-iau tioh8 kah chin chheN-chham2.”  23) Ia5-sou bo5 in3 i poaN3 ku2 oe7. I e5 bun5-tou5 chiu7 lai5 kiu5 I kong2, “KoaN2 i chau2, in-ui7 i it-tit8 toe3 ti7 lan2 e5 au7-bin7 teh toa7-siaN hoah bo5 hioh-khun3!”  24) Ia5-sou in3 kong2, “ Goa2 put-ko3 si7 ui7-tioh8 I2-sek-liat8-chok8 sit-be5 e5 iuN5 chiah siu7 chhe-phai3 lai5 e5.”  25) ThiaN-tioh8 an2-ne, hit e5 hu7-jin5-lang5 chiu7 laiphak5 loh8-khi3 Ia5-sou e5 bin7-cheng5 kong2, “Sin-seN a3, pang-chou7 goa2!”  26) Ia5-sou in3 kong2, “Theh8 kiaN2-ji5 e5 mi7-pau hiat hou7 kau2-a2 chiah8 si7 chin m7 eng-kai e5.”  27) Hu7-jin5-lang5 in3 kong2: “Sin-seN a3, an2-ne tioh8, m7-ku2 kau2-a2 ma7 e7-tang3 chiah8 tui3 chu2-lang5 e5 toh-teng2 ka-lauh8 loh8-lai5 e5 m7-pau iu3-a2.”  28) Ia5-sou chiu7 in3 i kong2: “Hu7-jin5-lang5 a3! Li2 e5 sin3-sim chin ui2-tai7. Li2 e5 sim-goan7 e7 chiau3 an2-ne hou7 li2 seng5-chiu7.” Tu2-tu2 hit e5 si5, i e5 cha-bou2-kiaN2 chiu7 ho2-khi3.

Ia5-sou i-ho2 chin-che7 lang5:
	29) Ia5-sou li7-khui hit e5 sou2-chai7, tng2-lai5 Ka-li7-li7 ou5-piN. I chiuN7-soaN, che7 loh8-khi3.  30) Kui toa7 tin7 e5 lang5 lai5 kau3 I hia. In chhoa7 pai2-kha-e5, chheN-me5-e5, phoa3-siuN3-e5, e2-kau2-e5 kap chin-che7 u7 pat8-khoan2 peN7 e5 lang5 lai5 khng3 toa3 Ia5-sou e5 bin7-cheng5; Ia5-sou chiu7 ka7 in i-ho2.  31) Cheng3-lang5 chit8-e7 khoaN3-kiN3 e2-kau2-e5 e7 kong2-oe7, phoa3-siuN3-e5 hok8-goan5, pai2-kha-e5 e7 kiaN5-lou7, chheN-me5-e5 u7 khoaN3-kiN3, chiu7 chin toa7 tioh8-kiaN lai5 chan3-bi2 I2-sek-liat8 e5 Siong7-chu2.

Ia5-sou hou7 si3-chheng lang5 chiah8 kah pa2: (Kho2 8:1-10)
	32) Ia5-sou kio3 I e5 bun5-tou5 lai5, ka7 in kong2: “Goa2 kho2-lin5 chit tin7-lang5, in-ui7 in i2-keng saN-jit8 ku2 kap goa2 cho3-hoe2, taN bo5 sim2-mih thang chiah8. Goa2 m7-kam hou7 in iau-iau tng2-khi3, kiaN-liau2 in ti7 lou7-nih8 e7 hun7-to2-khi3.”  33) Bun5-tou5 chiu7 ka7 I kong2, “Ti7 chit e5 phian-phiah e5 sou2-chai7, lan2 boeh tui3 tah-ui7 theh8 hiah-nih8 che7 mi7-pau lai5 houchiah7 che7 lang5 chiah8 kah pa2?”  34) Ia5-sou hoe5-tap kong2, “Lin2 u7 loa7-che7 mi7-pau?” In in3 I kong2, “Chhit ki, ia7 u7 kui2 boe2-a2 se3 boe2 hi5.”  35) Ia5-sou chiu7 hoan-hu3 cheng3-lang5 che7 loh8-khi3 thou5-kha.  36) Jian5-au7 I theh8 hit chhit ki mi7-pau kap hit kui2 boe2-a2 hi5 khi2-lai5, kam2-sia7 Siong7-chu2 liau2-au7, peh cho3 chit8 te3 chit8 te3, kau hou7 bun5-tou5. Bun5-tou5 chiu7 kau hou7 cheng3-lang5.  37) Tai7-ke long2 chiah8 kah chinpa2. Chiah8 chhun e5 khioh moa2 chhit na5.  38) Chiah8 e5 lang5, hu7-jin5-lang5 kap gin2-na2 bo5 sng3, u7 si3-chheng lang5.  39) Ia5-sou kai2-san3 cheng3-lang5 liau2-au7, chiu7 chiuN7-chun5, khi3 Ma2-ka-tan3 e5 te7-hng.

Te7 16 ChiuN

Iau-kiu5 sin5-chek: (Kho2 8:11-13; Lou7 12:54-56)
	1) U7 chit8 pai2, u7 chit8-koa2 Hoat-li7-sai3-phai3 kap Sat-thou2-kai-tong2 e5 lang5 lai5 chhoe7 Ia5-sou, siuN7-boeh chhi3-tham3 I. In iau-kiu5 I cho3 chit8 e5 tui3 thiN-teng2 lai5 e5 sin5-chek hou7 in khoaN3.  2) Ia5-sou in3 in kong2: “Jit8-thau5 boeh loh8 e5 si5 lin2 kong2, ‘In-ui7 thiN-sek ang, sou2-i2 bin5-na2-chai3 e7 ho2-thiN.’  3) ThiN-kng e5 si5 lin2 kong2, ‘ThiN-sek ang, hun5 ia7 ke7, kin-na2-jit8 it-teng7 u7 hong-hou7.’ Lin2 e7-hiau2 khoaN3 thiN-sek lai5 i7-chhek thiN-khi3 e5 ho2-phaiN2; an3-choaN2 be7-hiau2 pian7-piat8 si5-tai7 e5 chian5-tiau7.  4) Chit e5 se3-tai7 e5 lang5 na2 e7 chiah-nih8 sia3-ok koh bo5 sin3-sim! Lin2 ai3 Goa2 cho3 sin5-chek a2 m7-si7? Tai7-gian5-jin5 Iok-na2 e5 sin5-chek i2-goa7, Siong7-chu2 bo5 boeh siuN2-su3 sin5-chek hou7 chit se3-tai7 e5 lang5!” Kong2 liau2, Ia5-sou chiu7 li7-khui in khi3 pat8-ui7.

Hoat-li7-sai3-phai3 kap Sat-thou2-kai-tong2 e5 kaN3-bo2: (Kho2 8:14-21)
	5) Bun5-tou5 koe3-khi3 tui3-bin7 hoaN7 e5 si5, chiah hoat-kian3 tioh8 in be7-ki3-tit toa3 mi7-pau khi3.  6) Ia5-sou tui3 in kong2, “Tioh8 kin2-sin7 hong5-pi7 Hoat-li7-sai3-phai3 kap Sat-thou2-kai-tong2 e5 kaN3-bo2.”  7) In chiu7 hou7-siong gi7-lun7 kong2: “It-teng7 si7 in-ui7 lan2 bo5 toa3 mi7-pau lai5, I chiah an2-ne kong2.”  8) Ia5-sou chai-iaN2in sim-lai7 teh siuN7 sim2-mih, chiu7 kong2: “Lin2 an3-choaN2 hou7-siong teh gi7-lun7 bo5 toa3 mi7-pau lai5 e5 bun7-te5? Lin2 na2 e7 chiah-nih8 bo5 sin3-sim!  9) Lin2 kam2 iau2 be7 liau2-kai2? Lin2 kam2 be7-ki3-tit Goa2 eng7 gou7 ki mi7-pau hou7 gou7-chheng lang5 chiah8 kah pa2, chiah8 chhun e5 lin2  long2-chong2 khioh kui2 lang2 khi2-lai5?  10) Lin2 kam2 ia7 be7-ki3-tit Goa2 eng7 chhit ki mi7-pau hou7 si3-chheng lang5 chiah8 kah pa2, chiah8 chhun e5 lin2 long2-chong2 khioh kui2 na5 khi2-lai5?  11) Lin2 an3-choaN2 be7 liau2-kai3? Goa2 m7-si7 teh ka7 lin2 kong2-khi2 koan-he7 mi7-pau e5 tai7-chi3. Lin2 tioh8 hong5-pi7 Hoat-li7-sai3-phai3 kap Sat-thou2-kai-tong2 e5 kaN3-bo2!”  12) Jian5-au7 bun5-tou5 chiah beng5-pek8 Ia5-sou m7-si7 kio3 in hong5-pi7 cho3 mi7-pau e5 kaN3-bo2, si7 ai3 in hong5-pi7 Hoat-li7-sai3-phai3 kap Sat-thou2-kai-tong2 e5 ka3-si7.

Pi2-tek seng5-jin7 Ia5-sou si7 Bi2-sai3-a: (Kho2 8:27-30; Lou7 9:18-21)
	13) Ia5-sou lai5 kau3 Kai-sat-li7-a Hui-lip8-pi2 keng2-kai3 e5 si5, mng7 bun5-tou5 kong2, “Lang5 teh kong2 Jin5-chu2 si7 sim2-mih lang5?”  14) Bun5-tou5 in3 kong2, “U7 lang5 kong2 si7 si-sian2-chia2 Iok-han7, u7 lang5 kong2 si7 I2-li7-a, ia7 u7 lang5 kong2 si7 Ia5-li7-bi2 a2-si7 tai7-gian5-jin5 tiong e5 chit8-ui7.”  15) Ia5-sou koh mng7 in kong2, “TaN Goa2 ai3 chai lin2 e5 khoaN3-hoat. Lin2 kong2 Goa2 si7 sim2-mih lang5?”  16) Se-bun5 Pi2-tek chiu7 in3 kong2, “Li2 si7 Bi2-sai3-a, eng2-seng Siong7-chu2 e5 KiaN2.”  17) Ia5-sou ka7 i kong2: “Iok-na2 e5 kiaN2Se-bun5 a3, li2 sit8-chai7 chin u7 hok-khi3! In-ui7 ka7 li2 khe2-si7 chit hang7 tai7-chi3 e5 , si7 Goa2 e5 Thian-hu7, m7-si7 lang5 sou2 cho3 e5.  18( TaN Goa2 ka7 li2 kong2: in-ui7 li2 e5 mia5 kio3-cho3 Pi2-tek, i3-su3 chiu7-si7 chioh8-poaN5, sou2-i2 ti7 chit e5 chioh8-poaN5 teng2 Goa2 boeh kian3-lip8 Goa2 e5 kau3-hoe7. Im-kan si2-bong5 e5 kaon5-lek8 ia7 choat8-tui3 be7 iaN5-koe3 kau3-hoe7.  19) Goa2 boeh chiong Thian-kok e5 so2-si5 kau hou7 li2, li2 ti7 te7-siong7 sou2 kim3 e5, ti7 thiN-nih Goa2 ia7 boeh kim3. Li2 ti7 te7-siong7 sou2 chun2 e5, ti7 thiN-nih Goa2 ia7 boeh chun2.”  20) Jian5-au7 Ia5-sou chiu7 giam5-kim3 bun5-tou5 long2 m7-thang ka7 lang5 kong2 I chiu7-si7 Bi2-sai3-a.

Ia5-sou i7-ko3 I e5 si2-bong5 kap hok8-hoat8: (Kho2 8:31-9:1; Lou7 9:22-27)
	21) Tui3 hit e5 si5 khi2, Ia5-sou khai-si2 beng5-beng5 ka7 I e5 bun5-tou5 kong2 I tek-khak tioh8 khi3 Ia5-lou7-sat-leng2, ti7 hiah-e5 tiuN2-lo2, che3-si-tiuN2 kap keng-hak8-chia2 e5 chhiu2-thau5 siu7 chin-che7 khou2-lan7, it-teng7 e7 hou7 in sat-hai7. Tan7-si7 te7-saN jit8, Siong7-chu2 it-teng7 e7 hou7 I hok8-hoat8.  22) Pi2-tek chiu7 giu2 Ia5-sou khi3 piN-a, khai-si2 khoan3-ko3 chou2-chi2 I kong2, “Chu2 a3! Chhian-ban7 m7-thang an2-ne! Chit hang7 tai7-chi3 choat8-tui3 m7-thang hoat-seng!”  23) Ia5-sou oat8 koe3-lai5 tui3 Pi2-tek kong2: “Sat-tan3! Chau2! Chau2! Li2 teh chou2-tong3 Goa2 e5 lou7, in-ui7 li2 sou2 teh siuN7 e5, m7-si7 Siong7-chu2 e5 kian3-kai2, si7 lang5 e5 siuN7-hoat.”
	24) Jian5-au7 Ia5-sou ka7 I e5 bun5-tou5 kong2: “Lang5 na7 boeh kin-toe3 Goa2, tioh8 pang3-sak ka-ti7, gia5 i ka-ti7 e5 sip8-ji7-ke3 lai5 toe3 Goa2.  25) In-ui7 lang5 na7 boeh kiu3 i ka-ti7 e5 seN3-mia7, tian-to3 e7 song3-sit; tan7-si7 lang5 na7 ui7-tioh8 Goa2 lai5 hi-seng i ka7-ti7 e5 seN3-mia7, tian-to2 e7 tit-tioh8.  26) In-ui7 lang5 sui-jian5 tit-tioh8 choan5 se3-kai3, tan7-si7 na7 song3-sit i ka-ti7 e5 seN3-mia7 u7 sim2-mih li7-ek? A2-si7 lang5 e7-tang3 eng7 sim2-mih tai7-ke3 lai5 be2 i ka-ti7 e5 seN3-mia7?  27) In-ui7 Jin5-chu2 teh-boeh ti7 I e5 Thian-hu7 e5 eng5-iau7 tiong, kap I e5 chiong3 thian-sai3 cho3-hoe2 lai5-lim5, hit e5 si5 I e7 chiau2 mui2 chit8 e5 lang5 e5 heng5-ui5 lai5 po3-tap.  28) Goa2 sit8-chai7 ka7 lin2 kong2, khia7 ti7 chia e5 lang5, u7 lang5 iau2-boe7 si2 i2-cheng5, it-teng7 e7 khoaN3-kiN3 Jin5-chu2 cho3 Ong5 lai5-lim5.”

Te7 17 ChiuN

Ia5-sou kai2-pian3 heng5-siong7: (Kho2 9:2-13; Lou7 9:28-36)
	1) Lak8 jit8 au7, Ia5-sou chi2-u7 chhoa7 Pi2-tek, Nga2-kok kap Nga2-kok e5 sio2-ti7 Iok-han7 peh chiuN7 chit8 cho7 koan5-soaN.  2) Ia5-sou ti7 chiah-e5 bun5-tou5 e5 bin7-cheng5, I e5 heng5-siong7 kai2-pian3. I e5 bin7 chhin-chhiuN7 jit8-thau5 teh hoat-kng. I e5 saN peh8 kah kng iaN3-iaN3.  3) Hit e5 si5, chit saN e5 bun5-tou5 khoaN3-kiN3 Mou5-se kap I2-li7-a hian2-hian7 lai5 teh kap Ia5-sou kong2 oe7.  4) Pi2-tek chiu7 tui3 Ia5-sou kong2: “Chu2 a2! Lan2 toa3 ti7 chia sit8-chai7 chin ho2! Li2 na7 goan7-i3, goa2 boeh toa3 chia tah saN keng liau5-a2, chit8 keng hou7 Li2, chit8 keng hou7 Mou5-se, chit8 keng hou7 I2-li7-a.”  5) I iau2 teh kong2 e5 si5, hut-jian5-kan u7 chit8 phiN3 chin kng e5 hun5 chhut-hian7, eng7 iaN2 ka7 in kham3 khi2-lai5, iu7-koh tui3 hit e5 hun5-tiong hoat-chhut chit8 e5 siaN kong2: 
“Chit e5 si7 Goa2 sim-ai3 e5 KiaN2, Goa2 chin-chiaN3 kah-i3 e5. Lin2 tioh8 thiaN I e5 oe7.”
6) Chit8-e7 thiaN-kiN3 chiah-e5 oe7, bun5-tou5 chin tioh8-kiaN, chiu7 phak loh8-khi3 thou5-kha.  7) Tan7-si7 Ia5-sou oa2-lai5 in hia, eng7 chhiu2 ka7 in bong, kong2, “Khi2-lai5! M7-bian2 kiaN.”  8) In giah8-thau5 chit8-e7 khoaN3, Ia5-sou i2-goa7 long2 bo5 khoaN3-kiN3 poaN3 e5 lang5.
	9) In teh loh8-soaN e5 si5, Ia5-sou beng7-leng7 in kong2: “Siong7-chu2 hou7 Jin5-chu2 tui3 si2-lang5-tiong hok8-hoat8 i2-cheng5, lin2 m7-thang chiong sou2 khoaN3-kiN3 e5 i7-siong7 ka7 lang5 kong2.”  10) Bun5-lou5 chiu7 mng7 Ia5-sou kong2,”Hiah-e5 keng-hak8-chia2 si7 an3-choaN2 kong2 I2-li7-a tek-khak tioh8 tai7-seng lai5?”  11) I in3 kong2, “U7 iaN2, I2-li7-a e7 tai7-seng lai5, ia7 e7 tiong7-cheng2 it-chhe3.  12) Tan7-si7 Goa2 ka7 lin2 kong2, I2-li7-a i2-keng lai5 a7! Lang5 bo5 jim7-sek i, tian-to3 chiau3 in e5 i3-su3 lai5 tui3-thai7 i. Chhin-chhiuN7 an2-ne, Jin5-chu2 ia7 e7 siu7 in gek8-thai7.”  13) Hit e5 si5 bun5-tou5 chiah chai-iaN2 Ia5-sou sou2 kong2 e5, si7 teh chi2 si-sian2-chia2 Iok-han7.

Ia5-sou i-ho2 tioh8-iau e5 gin2-na2: (Kho2 9:14-29; Lou7 9:37-43a)
	14) In lai5-kau3 cheng3-lang5 hia e5 si5, u7 chit8 e5 lang5 lai5 Ia5-sou e5 bin7-cheng5, kui7 loh8-khi3.  15) kong2, “Sin-seN a3! Kho2-lin5 goa2 e5 kiaN2! I tai3 tioh8 giam5-tiong7 e5 iuN5-hin5-cheng3, sou2-i2 i tiaN7-tiaN7 poah8 loh8-khi3 hoe2-nih kap chui2-nih.  16) Goa2 u7 chhoa7 i khi3 chhoe7 Li2 e5 bun5-tou5, tan7-si7 in bo5 hoat-tou7 thang ka7 i i.”  17) Ia5-sou in3 kong2: “Ai a3! Chit se3-tai7 e5 lang5 na2 e7 chiah-nih8 bo5 sin3-sim koh chiah-nih8 sia5-ok! Goa2 tioh8 koh kap lin2 toa3 loa7 ku2? Goa2 tioh8 koh thun-lun2 lin2 loa7 ku2? Chhoa7 hit e5 gin2-na2 lai5 Goa2 chia!”  18) Ia5-sou chit8-e7 beng7-leng7, sia5-mou5 chiu7 tui3 gin2-na2 e5 seng-khu chhut-khi3; gin2-na2 chek-si5 chiu7 ho2-khi3.
	19) Hit e5 si5, bun5-tou5 oa2-khi3 Ia5-sou hia, thau mng7 I kong2. “Goan2 an3-choaN2 be7-tang3 koaN2chit e5 kui2-a2 chhut-khi3?”  20) Ia5-sou ka7 in kong2: “Che si7 in-ui7 lin2 e5 sin3-sim bo5 kau3. Goa2 sit8-chai7 ka7 lin2 kong2: lin2 na7 u7 chhin-chhiuN7 chit8 liap8 koa3-chhai3-chi2 hiah-nih8 toa7 e5 sin3-sim, lin2 e7-tangt3ui chit cho7 soaN kong2: ‘Tui3 chia soa2 koe3-khi3 hia,’ soaN chiu7 e7 soa2  koe3-khi3. Chhin-chhiuN7 an2-ne, lin2 bo5 chit8 hang7 cho3 be7 kau3.  ( 21) Chit khoan2 sia5-mou5, na7 m7-si7 eng7 ki5-to2 kap kim3-chiah8, chiu7 be7-tang3 koaN2 i chhut-khi3.”)

Ia5-sou te7-ji7 chhu3 i7-ho3 I e5 si2-bong5 kap hok8-hoat8: (Kho2 9:30-32; Lou7 9:43b-45)
	22) Ia5-sou kap bun5-tou5 chu7-chip8 ti7 Ka-li7-li7 Seng2 e5 si5, Ia5-sou ka7 bun5-tou5 kong2: “Jin5-chu2 teh-boeh hou7 lang5 chhut-be7 a7.  23) In e7 sat-hai7 I, tan7-si7 te7-saN jit8 Siong7-chu2 e7 hou7 I hok8-hoat8.” ThiaN-tioh8 an2-ne, bun5-tou5 chiu7 chin pi-siong.

Kiau2-lap8 seng3-tian7 soe3:
	24) Ia5-sou kap bun5-tou5 lai5-kau3 Ka-pek-long5 e5 si5, u7 kui2-na7 e5 siu seng3-tian7-soe3 e5 lang5 lai5 ka7 Pi2-tek kong2, “Lin2 lau7-su u7 lap8 seng3-tian7-soe3 a2 bo5?”  25) Pi2-tek in3 kong2, “U7 la3!” I chit8-e7 jip8-khi3 chhu3-lai7, Ia5-sou chiu7 tai7-seng mng7 i kong2: “Se-bun5, li2 e5 i3-kian3 an2-choaN2? Se3-siong7 e5 kun-ong5 tui3 sim2-mih lang5 siu koan-soe3 a2-si7 soe3-kim? Si7 tui3 ka-ti7 e5 kok-bin5 a2-si7 tui3 goa7-kok-lang5?”  26) Pi2-tek in3 kong2, “Tui3 goa7-kok-lang5.” Ia5-sou chiu7 ka7 i kong2: “Na7-si7 an2-ne, ka-ti7 e5 kok-bin5 bo5 ai3 tek-choe7 chiah-e5 lang5, sou2-i2 li2 khi3 ou5-nih8 tio3-hi5. Siong7 tai7-seng tio3-tioh8 e5 hi5, peh-khui i e5 chhui3, li2 chiu7 e7-tang3 tit-tioh8 chit8 e5 gin5-oan5. Li2 theh8 khi3 hou7 in, hit e5 gin5-oan5 u7 kau3 thang kiau2-lap8 Goa2 kap li2 e5 seng3-tian7-soe3.”

Te7 18 ChiuN

Ti7 Thian-kok siong7 ui2-tai7 e5: (Kho2 9:33-37; Lou7 9:46-48)
	1) Hit e5 si5, bun5-tou5 lai5 mng7 Ia5-sou kong2, “Ti7 Thian-kok sim2-mih lang5 siong7 ui2-tai7?”  2) Ia5-sou chiu7 kio3 chit8 e5 gin2-na2 lai5, hou7 i khia7 toa3 in tiong-kan,  3) kong2: “Goa2 sit8-chai7 ka7 lin2 kong2: lin2 na7 bo5 kai2-pian3 chiaN5-cho3 chhin-chhiuN7 gin2-na2, lin2 choat8-tui3 be7 tang3 jip8 Thian-kok.  4) Sou2-i2 lang5 na7 ka-ti7 khiam-pi chhin-chhiuN7 chit e5 gin2-na2, i ti7 Thian-kok si7 siong7 ui2-tai7 e5 lang5.  5) Lang5 na7 ui7-tioh8 Goa2 lai5 hoan-geng5 chhin-chhiuN7 chit khoan2 gin2-na2, chiu7-si7 hoan-geng5 Goa2.”

In2-khi2 lang5 hoan7-choe7: (Kho2 9:42-48; Lou7 17:1-2)
	6) “Na7 u7 lang5 in2-iu2 chiah-e5 sin3 goa2 e5 lang5 e5 tiong-kan hou7 lang5 khoaN3 siong7 bo5 khi2 e5 chit8 e5 hoan7-choe7, i leng5-kho2 tioh8 hou7 lang5 eng7 toa7 chioh8-bo7 pak8 toa3 am7-kun2, ka7 i thiam7-loh8 hai2 khah ho2.  7) E7 hou7 lang5 ham7-loh8 choe7 chit e5 se3-kan, tioh8 u7 chai-ho7! In2-khi2 lang5 hoan7-choe7 e5 tai7-chi3 si7 lan5-bian2 e5, tan7-si7 in2-khi2 lang5 hoan7-choe7 chit e5 lang5, tioh8 u7 chai-ho7!”
	8) “Li2 e5 chit8 ki chhiu2 a2-si7 li2 e5 chit8 ki kha na7 in2-khi2 li2 hoan7-choe7, li2 tioh8 kiam2 chit8 ki chhiu2, a2-si7 khiam3 chit8 ki kha lai5 chin3-jip8 eng2-seng, pi2 siang-chhiu2 siang-kha ho2-ho2 loh8 khi3 eng2-oan2 e5 hoe2 khah iaN5!  9) Li2 e5 chit8 lui2 bak8-chiu na7 in2-khi2 li2 hoan7-choe7, li2 tioh8 ka7 ou2 chhut-lai5, tan3 hiat-kak8.  Li2 leng5-kho2 kiam2 chit8 lui2 bak8-chiu lai5 jip8 eng2-seng, pi2 nng7 lui2 bak8-chiu ho2-ho2 loh8 te7-gak8 siu7 eng2-oan2 e5 hoe2-heng5 khah iaN5!”

Be5-iuN5 e5 phi3-ju7: (Lou7 15:3-7)
	10) “tioh8 kin2-sin7 m7-thang khoaN3-khin chiah-e5 hou7 lang5 khoaN3 siong7 bo5 khi2 e5 lang5 e5 chit8 e5. Goa2 ka7 lin2 kong2: in e5 thian-sai3 ti7 thiN-teng2, siong5-siong5 ti7 Goa2 e5 Thian-hu7 e5 bin7-cheng5.  ( 11) Jin5-chu2 lai5 e5 su3-beng7 si7 boeh kiu3 sit-be5 e5 lang5.”)
	12) “Lin2 siuN7 an3-choaN2? Lang5 na7 u7 chit8 pah chiah iuN5, ki5-tiong u7 chit8 chiah sit-be5 khi3, i kam2 be7 pang3 ki5-tha hit kau2-chap8-kau2 chiah toa3 soaN-phiaN5, khi3 chhoe7 hit chiah sit-be5 khi3 e5 iuN5?  13) Goa2 sit8-chai7 ka7 lin2 kong2: i chhoe7 tioh8 e5 si5, ui7-tioh8 hit chit8 chiah, pi2 ui7-tioh8 hit kau2-chap8-kau2 chiah bo5 sit-be5 e5, koh-khah hoaN_hi2.  14) Lin2 e5 Thian-hu7 ia7-si7 an2-ne. I m7-kam hou7 chiah-e5 hou7 lang5 khoaN3 siong7 bo5 khi2 e5 lang5 e5 chit8 e5 sit-loh8 khi3.”

Hoan7-choe7 e5 hiaN-ti7:
	15) “Li2 e5 hiaN-ti7 na7 u7 tek-choe7 li2 e5 si5, Li2 tioh8 khi3 chhoe7 i, kan-taN li2 kap i ti7-le7 e5 si5, chi2-tiam2 i e5 chho3-gou7. I na7 boeh thiaN li2, li2 chiu7 koh tit-tioh8 li2 e5 hiaN-ti7.  16) Tan7-si7 i na7 m7 thiaN li2, li2 chiu7 tioh8 chhoe7 chit8-nng7 e5 lang5 kap li2 khi3, eng7 an2-ne lai5 hu5-hap8 Lut8-hoat e5 kui-teng7 kong2: ‘It-chhe3 e5 khong3-ko3, tioh8 u7 nng7-saN e5 cheng3-jin5 e5 cheng3-gian5 chiah e7-tang3 seng5-hau7.’  17) I na7 m7 thiaN in, li2 tioh8 ka7 i khoaN3-cho3 chhin-chhiuN7 Goa7-pang-lang5 a2-si7 thiu-soe3 e5 lang5.”

Kim3-chi2 kap in2-chun2:
	18) “Goa2 sit8-chai7 ka7 lin2 kong2: lin2 ti7 te7-siong7 sou2 kim3-chi2 e5, ti7 thiN-nih ia7 e7 siu7 kim3-chi2; lin2 ti7 te7-siong7 sou2 in2-chun2 e5, ti7 thiN-nih ia7 e7 siu7 in2-chun2.”
	19) “Goa2 koh ka7 lin2 kong2: lin2 tiong-kan na7 u7 nng7 e5 lang5 ti7 te7-siong7 tang5-sim hap8-i3 lai5 ki5-kiu5 sim2-mih, Goa2 e5 Thian-hu7 it-teng7 e7 ka7 in seng5-choan5.  20) IN-ui7 na7 u7 nng7-saN e5 lang5 hong7 Goa2 e5 mia5 lai5 chu7-chip8, Goa2 ia7 ti7 hia kap in tong5-chai7.”

Khek-pok8 e5 che3-chu2 e5 phi3-ju7:
	21) Jina5-au7 Pi2-tek oa2-lai5 mng7 Ia5-sou kong2: “Chu2 a3. goa2 e5 hiaN-ti7 na7 tek-choe7 goa2, goa2 tioh8 sia3-bian2 i kui2 pai2? Chhit pai2 u7 kau3 bo5?”  22) Ia5-sou ka7 i kong2: “Bo5 kau3, m7-na7 chhit pai2, tioh8-ai3 chhit pai2 e5 chhit-chap8 poe7.  23) In-ui7 Thian-kok chhin-chhiuN7 kun-ong5 boeh kap i e5 lou7-pok8 kiat-siau3.  24) Khai-si2 sng3-siau3 e5 si5, u7 lang5 chhoa7 chit8 e5 khiam3 i kui2-na7 pah ban7 e5 lang5 lai5.  25) In-ui7 i heng5 be7 khi2, sou2-i2 chu2-lang5 beng7-leng7 i tioh8 chiong pun2-sin kap i e5 bou2-kiaN2 i2-kip8 i sou2 u7 e5 it-chhe3 long2 be7 lai5 heng5-che3.  26) Hit e5 lou5-pok8 chiu7 kui7 loh8-khi3 phak toa3 i e5 chu2-lang5 e5 bin7-cheng5 kiu5 i kong2: ‘ChhiaN2 li2 hou7 goa2 an7 chit8-e7 , goa2 e7 long2 heng5 li2’  27) Hit e5 chu2-lang5 chiu7 lin5-bin2 i, soah bian2-ti5 i e5 che3, pang3 i khi3.”
	28) “Hit e5 lou5-pok8 chhut-khi3 e5 si5, tu2-tioh8 chit8 e5 khiam3 i kui2 khou gin5-na2 e5 tong5-su7, chiu7 ka7 i liah8-le7, teN7 i e5 am7-kun2 kong2, ‘Li2 sou2 khiam3 e5, tioh8-ai3 heng5 goa2!’  29) I e5 tong5-su7 chiu7 kui loh8-khi3 kiu5 i kkong2, ‘ChhiaN2 hou7 goa2 an7 chit8-e7, goa2 e7 long2 heng5 li2.’  30) Tan7-si7 i m7-kheng2, tian-to3 ka7 i liah8-khi3 koaiN-loh8 kaN-gak8, boeh ka7 i koaiN kah che3 long2 heng5 chheng-chho2.  31) Pat8-e5 tong5-su7 chit8-e7 khoaN3-kiN3 an2-ne chiu7 hun3-khai3, chiong chit e5 tai7-chi3 khi3 ka7 in chu2-lang5 po3-ko3.  32) In-ui7 an2-ne chu2-lang5 chiu7 tiau3 hit e5 lou5-pok8 lai5, tui3 i kong2: ‘Li2 chit e5 khou2-ouN3 e5 lou5-pok8 a3! Li2 ka7 goa2 ai-kiu5, goa2 chiu7 chiong li2 sou2 khiam3 e5 che3 long2-chong2 ka7 li2 bian2-ti5.  33) Li2 kam2 m7 eng-kai chhin-chhiuN7 goa2 tong5-cheng5 li2 an2-ne, lai5 tong5-cheng5 li2 e5 tong5-su7.’  34) Chu2-lang5 toa7 siu7-khi3, chiu7 chiong i sang3 khi3 siu7 khou2-heng5, boeh ka7 i koaiN kah sou2 khiam3 e5 che3 long2 heng5 chheng-chho2.”  35) Ia5-sou choe3-au7 kong2, “Lin2 mui2 chit8 e5 lang5 na7 bo5 chin-sim sia3-bian2 ka-ti7 e5 hiaN-ti7, Goa2 e5 Thian-hu7 ia7 e7 an2-ne tui3-thai7 lin2.”

Te7 19 ChiuN

Koan-he7 li7-hun e5 kau3-hun3: (Kho2 10:1-12)
	1) Ia5-sou kong2 chiah-e5 oe7 liau2-au7, chiu7 li7-khui Ka-li7-li7 Seng2, koh tng2-khi3 Iok-tan3-ho5 e5 tui3-hoaN7, Iu5-thai3 e5 te7-hng.  2) U7 chin toa7 tin7 e5 lang5 toe3 I khi3.  I chiu7 toa3 hia i-ho2 chin-che7 peN7-lang5.
	3) U7 chit8 koa2 Hoat-li7-sai3-phai3 e5 lang5 lai5 chhoe7 Ia5-sou, boeh chhi3-tham3 I, chiu7 mng7 I kong2, “Chiau3 lan2 e5 Lut8-hoat, tiong7-hu na7 u7 sim2-mih li2-iu5 chiu7 e7-eng7-tit li5 i e5 bou2 si7 a2 m7-si7?”  4) Ia5-sou in3 in kong2: “Lin2 kam2 bo5 thak8 tioh8 Seng3-keng chiah-e5 oe7, kong2: ‘siong7-chu2 chu7 khi2-thau5 chiu7 chhong3-cho7 lang5, chhong3-cho7 it-lam5 it-li2,’  5) iu7-koh kong2: ‘In-ui7 an2-ne cha-pou-lang5 e7 li7-khui i e5 pe7-bo2 lai5 kap i e5 hu7-jin5-lang5 kiat-hap8, nng7 lang5 e7 chiaN5-cho3 it-the2.’  6) An2-ne khoaN3 khi2-lai5, hu-hu7 i2-keng m7-si7 nng7 e5, si7 it-the2. Sou2-i2 Siong7-chu2 sou2 phoe3-hap8 e5, lang5 m7-thang thiah-soaN3.”  7) Hoat-li7-sai3-phai3 e5 lang5 mng7 I kong2, “Na7-si7 an2-ne Mou5-se an3-choaN2 beng7-leng7 na7 u7 lang5 boeh kap i e5 bou2 li7-hun e5 si5, tioh8 li7-hun cheng3-su hou7 i, chiah hou7 i chhut-khi3?”  8) Ia5-sou in3 kong2: “in-ui7 lin2 e5 sim-koaN chin nge7, sou2-i2 Mou5-se chiah iong5-un2 lin2 kap lin2 e5 hu7-jin5-lang5 li7-hun. Tan7-si7 Siong7-chu2 chhong3-se3 e5 si5, peng3 m7-si7 an2-ne.  9) Goa2 koh ka7 lin2 kong2: na7 m7-si7 hu7-jin5-lang5 bo5 siu2 hu7-to7, tiong7-hu m7-thang ka7 i li7-hun. Tiong7-hu na7 ka7 i li7-hun, koh khi3 chhoa7 pat8 e5 cha-bou2-lang5, tiong7-hu chiu7-si7 hoan7 tioh8 kan-im5 e5 choe7.”
	10) Ia5-sou e5 bun5-tou5 ka7 I kong2, “Hu-hu7 e5 koan-he7 na7-si7 an2-ne, leng5-kho2 mai3 kiat-hun khah ho2!”  11) Ia5-sou chiu7 in3 in kong2: “Chit khoan2 e5 ka3-si7 be7-tang3 sek-iong7 mui2 chit8 e5 lang5, chi2-u7 e7-tang3 sek-iong7 hiah-e5 tit-tioh8 tek8-piat8 e5 in-su3 e5 lang5.  12) U7 lang5 in-ui7 thian-seng e5 khoat-tiam2 be7-tang3 kiat-hun; u7 lang5 in-ui7 jin5-ui5 e5 in-sou3 be7-tang3 kiat-hun; u7 lang5 ui7-tioh8 Thian-kok ka-ti7 bo5 ai3 kiat-hun. E7-tang3 an2-ne cho3 e5 lang5 chiah thang chiap-siu7 chit e5 kau3-hun3.”

Ia5-sou chiok-hok se3-han3 gin2-na2: (Kho2 10:13-16; Lou7 18:15-17)
	13) U7 chit8-koa2 lang5 chhoa7 se3-han3 gin2-na2 lai5 Ia5-sou hia, ai3 I ka7 in an3-chhiu2 ki5-to2. Bun5-tou5 chiu7 chek-pi7 chiah-e5 lang5.  14) Ia5-sou ka7 bun5-tou5 kong2, “Tioh8 hou7 hiah-e5 gin2-na2 lai5 Goa2 chia, m7-thang ka7 in tong3, in-ui7 chhin-chhiuN7 chiah-e5 gin2-na2 e5 lang5 chiah e7-tang3 chiaN5-cho3 Thian-kok e5 chu2-bin5.”  15) Ia5-sou ka7 in an3-chhiu2, chiu7 li7-khui in khi3.

Ho2-giah8 e5 chheng-lian5: (Kho2 10:17-31; Lou7 18:18-30)
	16) U7 chit8 pai2, u7 chit8 e5 lang5 lai5 chhoe7 Ia5-sou kong2, “lau7-su, goa2 tioh8 cho3 sim2-mih ho2-su7 chiah e7-tang3 tit-tioh8 eng2-seng?”  17) Ia5-sou ka7 i kong2: “li2 an3-choaN2 lai5 mng7 goa2 sim2-mih si7 hou7-cho3 ho2-su7? Oan5-choan5 ho2 e5, chi2-u7 si7 Chit8-ui7. Li2 na7 ai3 boeh tit-tioh8 eng2-seng, tioh8 chun-siu2 kai3-beng7.”  18) I mng7 Ia5-sou kong2, “Si7 tah chit8 tiau5 kai3-beng7?” Ia5-sou in3-kong2: “M7-thang thai5-lang5; m7-thang hoan7 kan-im5; m7-thang thau-theh8; m7-thang cho3 gui7-cheng3;  19) tioh8 hau3-keng3 pe7-bo2; koh tioh8 ai3 li2 e5 lin5-jin5 chhin-chhiuN7 ai3 li2 ka-ti7.”  20) Hit e5 siau3-lian5-lang5 ka7 Ia5-sou kong2: “Chiah-ek5ai-beng7 goa2 i2-keng long2 u7 chun-siu2. TaN goa2 iau2 tioh8 koh cho3 sim2-mih?”  21) Ia5-sou ka7 i kong2, “Li2 na7 u7 siuN7-boeh cho3 chit8 e5 oan5-choan5 e5 lang5, tioh8 khi3 be7 li2 sou2 u7 e5 chai5-san2 lai5 chin2-che3 san3-chhiah-lang5, an2-ne, ti7 thiN-teng2 li2 chiu7 e7 u7 chai5-po2; jian5-au7 chiah lai5 toe3 Goa2.”  22) Siau3-lian5-lang5 chit8-e7 thiaN-kiN3 chiah-e5 oe7, chiu7 iu-iu chhiu5-chhiu5 li7-khui Ia5-sou, in-ui7 i u7 chin-che7 chai5-san2.
	23) Ia5-sou chiu7 ka7 I e5 bun5-tou5 kong2: “Goa2 sit8-chai7 ka7 lin2 kong, ho2-giah8-lang5 boeh chin3-jip8 Thian-kok si7 hui-siong5 khun3-lan5.  24) Si7 la3, Goa2 koh ka7 lin2 kong2: lok8-to5 chng3-koe3 chiam-phiN7, ia7 pi2 ho2-giah8-lang5 chin3-jip8 Thian-kok iau2 koh-khah iong5-i7.”  25) Bun5-tou5 thiaN-kiN3 an2-ne chin tioh8-kiaN, chiu7 mng7 I kong2, “Na7-si7 an2-ne, sim2-mih lang5 e7-tang3 tit-tioh8 kiu3?”  26) Ia5-sou liah8 in kim-kim khoaN3, kong2: “Chit hang7 tai7-chi3 lang5 bo5 kho2-leng5 thang cho3, tan7-si7 Siong7-chu2 tak8-hang7 to u7 kho2-l6.”
	27) Pi2-tek chiu7 mng7 Ia5-sou kong2, “Li2 khoaN3! Goan2 i2-keng pang3-sak it-chhe3 lai5 toe3 Li2, kiu3-keng3 goan2 e7-tang3 tit-tioh8 sim2-mih?”  28) Ia5-sou ka7 in kong2: “Goa2 sit8-chai7 ka7 lin2 kong2, sin e5 se3-kai3 lai5-lim5 e5 si5, Jin5-chu2 e7 che7 toa3 I eng5-iau7 e5 po2-cho7. Hit e5 si5 lin2 chiah-e5 toe3 Goa2 e5 lang5 ia7 e7 che7 toa3 chap8-ji7 e5 po2-cho7, lai5 sim2-phoaN3 I2-sek-liat8 e5 chap8-ji7 chi-phai3.  29) Lang5 na7 ui7-tioh8 Goa2 e5 ian5-kou3 pang3-sak ka-teng5, hiaN-ti7, chi2-moe7, lau7-pe7, lau7-bo2, kiaN2-ji5 a2-si7 chhan5-hng5 e5, it-teng7 long2 e7 siu7-tioh8 pah poe7 e5 po3-siuN2, ji5-chhiaN2 ia7 e7 ke3-seng5 eng2-seng.  30) Tan7-si7 u7 chin-che7 hian7-chai7 cho3 thau5-cheng5 e5, e7 piN3-cho3 lou7-boe2, ia7 u7 chin-che7 hian7-chai7 cho3 lou7-boe2 e5, e7 cho3 thau5-cheng5.”

Te7 20 ChiuN

Phu5-to5-hng5 e5 kang-lang5:
	1) “Thian-kok chhin-chhiuN7 e7-bin7 e5 phi3-ju7: U7 chit8 e5 phu5-to5-hng5 e5 chu2-lang5 thau3-cha2 chhut-khi3 chhiaN3 kang-lang5 khi3 i e5 phu5-to5-hng5 cho3-kang.  2) I kap kang-lang5 iok-teng7 chit8 kang chit8 khou-gin5 e5 kang-chiN5, chiu7 chhe in jip8-khi3 i e5 phu5-to5-hng5 cho3-kang.  3) Chai2-khi2-si5 kau2 tiam2, chu2-lang5 koh chhut-khi3,khoaN3-kiN3 iau2 u7 chit8-koa2 lang5 eng5-eng5 khia7 ti7 chhi7-tiuN5 bo5 teh cho3 sim2-mih,  4) chiu7 tui3 in kong2, ‘Lin2 ia7 lai5-khi3 goa2 e5 phu5-to5-hng5 cho3-kang, goa2 boeh kong-to7 e5 kang-chiN5 hou7 lin2.’  5) In chiu7 khi3. Tiong-tau3 chap8-ji7 tiam2 kap e7-pou-si5 saN tiam2, chu2-lang5 iu7-koj chhut-khi3, ia7 chiau3 an2-ne cho3.  6) Choe3-au7, chha-put-to gou7 tiam2 i koh chhut-khi3 e5 si5, khoaN3-kiN3 iau2 u7 lang5 khia7 ti7 hia, chiu7 ka7 in kong2, ‘Lin2 an3-choaN2 kui-jit8 eng5-eng5 ti7 chia bo5 teh cho3 sim2-mih?’  7) In ka7 i kong2, ‘In-ui7 bo5 lang5 chhiaN3 goan2.’ Chu2-lang5 ka7 in kong2, ‘Na7-si7 an2-ne, lin2 ia7 lai5-khi3 goa2 e5 phu5-to5-hng5 cho3-kang.’”
	8) “Kau3 boeh-am3-a2-si5, phu5-to5-hng5 e5 chu2-lang5 ka7 i e5 koan2-li2-jin5 kong2: ‘Li2 kio3 hiah-e5 kang-lang5 long2 lai5, boeh hoat kang-chiN5 hou7 in; tui3 lou7-boe2 lai5 e5 seng hoat, hoat kau3 tai7-seng lai5 e5 ui5-chi2.’  9) Hiat-e5 e7-pou-si5 gou7-tiam2 chiah khai-si2 kang-chouk e5 lang5 lai5, mui2 chit8 e5 lang5 nia2 tioh8 chit8 kang e5 kang-chiN5 chit8 khou-gin5.  10) Hiah-e5 tai7-seng khai-si2 kang-chok e5 lang5 lai5 nia2 kang-chiN5 e5 si5, in sim-lai7 siuN7 kong2 in e7-tang3 nia2 khah che7; tan7-si7 in mui2-lang5 ia7-si7 peN5-peN5 nia2 chit8 kang e5 kang-chiN5 chit8 khou-gin5.  11) In chit8-e7 nia2-tioh8 chiN5, chiu7 khai-si2 tui3 chu2-lang5 phau7 put-peng5,  12) kong2: ‘Hiah-e5 lou7-boe2 lai5 e5, chi2-u7 cho3 chit8 tiam2-cheng e5 khang-khoe3 na7-tiaN7, tan7-si7 goan2 kui jit8 phak8-jit8 lo5-khou2 kang-chok, li2 keng3-jian5 ia7 hou7 in nia2 kap goan2 peN5 che7 chiN5.’  13) Chu2-lang5 chiu7 hoe5-tap ki5-tiong e5 chit8 e5 kong2: ‘Peng5-iu2! Goa2 bo5 hou7 li2 chiah8-khui. Li2 kam2 m7-si7 kap goa2 iok-teng7 chit8 kang chit8 khou-gin5 e5 kang-chiN5?  14) Li2 theh8 li2 e5 kang-chiN5 tng2-khi3! Goa2 kam-goan7 boeh hou7 chiah-e5 lou7-boe2 lai5 e5 lang5 peN5-che7 kang-chiN5.  15) Goa2 eng7 ka-ti7 e5 chiN5 cho3 goa2 sou2 ai3 cho3 e5, kam2 be7-eng7-tit? Goa2 tui3 in khong2-khai3, li2 chiu7 teh bak8-khang-chhiah si7 bo5?’”  16) Ia5-sou choe3-au7 ka7 in kong2, “Lou7-boe2 e5, e7 piN3-cho3 tai7-seng, tai7-seng e5, e7 piN3-cho3 lou7-boe2.”

Ia5-sou te7-saN chhu3 i7-ko3 I e5 si2-bong5 kap hok8-hoat8: (Kho2 10:32-34; Lou7 18:31-34)
	17) Ia5-sou kap chap8-ji7 e5 bun5-tou5 cho3-tin7 teh-boeh khi3 Ia5-lou7-sat-leng2 SiaN5 e5 si5, ti7 lou7-tiong chhoa7 in khi3 piN-a, na2 kiaN5 na2 ka7 in kong2:  18) “Lin2 chu3-i3 thiaN, lan2 chit-chun7 boeh lai5-khi3 Ia5-lou7-sat-leng2, ti7 hia Jin5-chu2 e7 hou7 lang5 kau hou7 hiah-e5 che3-si-tiuN2 kap keng-hak8-chia2. In e7 ka7 I phoaN3-koat si2-heng5,  19) ia7 e7 chiong I kau hou7 Goa7-pang-lang5. Chiah-e5 Goa7-pang-lang5 e7 ka7 I hi3-lang7, eng7 piN ka7 I phah, soah ka7 I teng3 toa3 sip8-ji7-ke3; tan7-si7 te7-saN jit8 Siong7-chu2 it-teng7 e7 hou7 I hok8-hoat8.”

Bo2-chhin e5 iau-kiu5: (Kho2 10:35-45)
	20) Hit e5 si5, Se-pi2-thai3 e5 bou2 chhoa7 i nng7 e5 kiaN2-ji5 lai5 kiN3 Ia5-sou, chiu7 phak loh8-khi3 kiu5 Ia5-sou chit8 hang7 tai7-chi3.  21) Ia5-sou mng7 i kong2, “Li2 boeh kiu5 sim2-mih?” I kong2, “ChhiaN2 Li2 ka7 goa2 tah-eng3 Li2 cho3 Ong5 e5 si5, hou7 goa2 chit nng7 e5 kiaN2, chit8 e5 che7 toa3 Li2 e5 chiaN3-peng5, chit8 e5 che7 toa3 Li2 e5 to3-peng5.”  22) Ia5-sou in3 kong2, “Lin2 m7 chai-iaN2 lin2 teh kiu5 sim2-mih. Goa2 teh-boeh lim e5 khou2-poe, lin2 lim e7 loh8-khi3 be7?” In kong2, “Goan2 e7.”  23) Ia5-sou ka7 inkong2: “Lin2 sit8-chai7 e7 lim Goa2 e5 khou2-poe, tan7-si7 boeh hou7 lin2 che7 Goa2 e5 chiaN3-peng5 a2-si7 to3-peng5, Goa2 be7-tang3 chu2-i3. Chiah-e5 ui7, Goa2 e5 Thian-hu7 i2-keng u7 phah-sng3 boeh hou7 sim2-mih lang5 che7.”
	24) Ki5-tha hit chap8 e5 bun5-tou5 thiaN-tioh8 chit hang7 tai7-chi3, chiu7 siu7-khi3 hit nng7 e5 hiaN-ti7.  25) Ia5-sou chiu7 kio3 in long2 lai5 I e5 bin7-cheng5, kong: “Lin2 chai-iaN2 Goa7-pang-lang5 e5 kun-ong5 si7 teh koan2-li2 in e5 jin5-bin5, ia7 u7 koaN-tiuN2 teh koan2-hat in.  26) Tan7-si7 lin2 e5 tiong-kan khiok m7-si7 an2-ne. Lin2 e5 tiong-kan na7 u7 lang5 ai3 boeh cho3 toa7 e5, i tian-to3 tioh8 chiaN5-cho3 lin2 e5 chhe-eng7 e5.  27) Na7 u7 lang5 ai3 boeh cho3 siu2-leng2 e5, i tian-to3 tioh8 chiaN5-cho3 lin2 e5 lou5-pok8.  28) Chhin-chhiuN7 an2-ne, Jin5-chu2 lai5 chit e5 se3-kan, m7-si7 boeh lai5 hou7 lang5 hong7-thai7, tian-to3 si7 boeh lai5 hok8-bu7 pat8-lang5; peng3-chhiaN2 boeh hi-seng I ka-ti7 e5 seN3-mia7 lai5 siok8-hoe5 chin-che7 lang5.”

Ia5-sou i-ho2 nng7 e5 chheN-me5-e5: (Kho2 10:46-52; Lou7 18:35-43)
	29) In li7-khui Ia5-li7-ko SiaN5 e5 si5, u7 chin toa7 tin7 e5 lang5 toe3 Ia5-sou khi3.  30) U7 nng7 e5 chheN-me5-e5 che7 ti7 lou7-piN. In chit8-e7 thiaN-kiN3 Ia5-sou tui3 hia koe3, chiu7 khai-si2 toa7 siaN hoah kong2, “Sin-seN! Tai7-pit8 e5 kiaN2-sun! Kho2-lin5 goan2!”  31) Cheng3-lang5 chek-pi7 in, kio3 in tioh8 tiam7-tiam. Tan7-si7 in lu2 toa7 siaN hoah kong2, “Sin-seN! Tai7-jit8 e5 kiaN2-sun! Kho2 lin5 goan2!”  32) Ia5-sou chiu7 theng5-kha, kio3 in lai5, mng7 in kong2, “Lin2 ai3 Goa2 ka7 lin2 cho3 sim2-mih?”  33) In ka7 I kong2, “Sin-seN! Kiu5 Li2 khui goan2 e5 bak8-chiu, hou7 goan2 u7 khoaN3-kiN3!”  34) Ia5-sou lin5-bin2 in, chiu7 bong in e5 bak8-chiu. In chek-si5 u7 khoaN3-kiN3, chiu7 toe3 I khi3.

Te7 21 ChiuN

Ia5-sou choe3-au7 chin3-jip8 Ia5-lou7-sat-leng2-siaN5: (Kho2 11:1-11; Lou7 19:28-40; Iok 12:12-19)
	1) Ia5-sou kap I e5 bun5-tou5 teh-boeh kau3 Ia5-lou7-sat-leng2 SiaN5 e5 si5, lai5 kau3 Kan-na2 soaN-kha e5 Pek-hoat-ki5. Ti7 hia Ia5-sou chhe nng7 e5 bun5-tou5 tai7-seng khi3,  2) hoan-hu3 in kong2: “Lin2 khi3 tui3-bin7 e5 chng-thau5, chiu7 sui5-si5 e7 khoaN3-kiN3 chit8 chiah li5-a2-bo2 pak8 ti7 hia, u7 chit8 chiah li5-a2-kiaN2 kap i cho3-hoe2, lin2 ka7 i thau2-khui, khan lai5 Goa2 chia.  3) Na7-u7 lang5 tui3 lin2 kong2 sim2-mih, lin2 chiu7 ka7 i kong2, ‘Chu2 teh khiam3-eng7 in’. Hit e5 lang5 sui5-si5 e7 hou7 lin2 khan lai5.”
	4) Chit e5 su7 chiu7-si7 ui7-tioh8 boeh eng3-giam7 tai7-gian5-jin5 sou2 kong2 e5 oe7, kong2: 
5) “Tioh8 ka7 Sek-an SiaN5 e5 cha-bou2-kiaN2 kong: ‘Li2 khoaN3! Li2 e5 ong5 teh-boeh lai5 li2 chia, I chin un-jiu5 khia5 ti7 li5-a2 teng2, khia5 chit8 chiah li5-a2-kiaN2, chiu7-si7 teh chai3-hoe3 e5 li5-a2 kiaN2.’”
	6) Chit nng7 e5 bun5-tou5 chiu7 chiau3 Ia5-sou hoan-hu3 e5 khi3 cho3.  7) In khan li5-a2-bo2 kap li5-a2-kiaN2 lai5, chiong in e5 goa7-saN phoah8 toa3 hit teng2-bin7, Ia5-sou chiu7 peh khit-khi3 khia5.  8) Chin-che7 kun5-chiong3 chiong ka-ti7 e5 goa7-saN phou toa3 lou7-nih8, ia7 u7 lang5 chho3 chhiu7-ki phou toa3 lou7-nih8.  9) Cheng5-kiaN5 au7-toe3 e5 cheng3-lang5 hoah kong2,
“Ho5-san3-na2! Tai7-pit8 e5 kiaN2-sun, hong7 Chu2 e5 mia5 lai5 e5, eng-kai siu7 chan3-bi2! Chhen-chan3 chi3-kome5 Siong7-chu2!”
	10) Ia5-sou chit8-e7 jip8-khi3 Ia5-lou7-sat-leng2 SiaN5, choan5 siaN5-chhi7 long2 hoa7 khi2-lai5, kong2, “Chit e5 si7 sim2-mih lang5?”  11) Cheng3-lang5 kong2: “Chit e5 si7 tai7-gian5-jin5 Ia5-sou, si7 Ka-li7-li7 Seng2 e5 Na2-sat-lek8-lang5.”

Ia5-sou chheng seng3-tian7: (Kho2 11:15-19; Lou7 19:45-48; Iok 2:13-22)
	12) Ia5-sou jip8-khi3 seng3-tian7, chiong ti7 seng3-tian7 lai7 hiah-e5 teh cho3 seng-li2 e5 lang5 long2 ka7 in koaN2 chhut-khi3, ia7 chiong oaN7-chiN5 e5 lang5 e5 toh-a2, kap be7 hun2-chiau2 e5 lang5 e5 i2-a2 chhia-chhia-to2.  13) I ka7 in kong2: “Seng3-keng u7 ki3-chai3 kong2, ‘goa2 e5 chhu3 tioh8 hou7 lang5 chheng-hou cho3 ki5-to2 e5 chhu3.’ Tan7-si7 lin2 ka7 i pian3-cho3 chhat8-siu7!”
	14) Ti7 seng3-tian7 u7 chheN-me5-e5 kap pai2-kha-e5 oa2-khi3 Ia5-sou hia, I chiu7 ka7 in i-ho2 khi3.  15) Chiah-e5 che3-si-tiuN2 kap keng-hak8-chia2 khoaN3-kiN3 Ia5-sou sou2 cho3 e5 sin5-chek, iu7-koh thiaN-kiN3 gin2-na2 ti7 seng3-tian7 toa7-siaN hoah kong2, “Ho5-san3-na2! Tai7-pit8 e5 kiaN2-sun!” chiu7 toa7 siu7-khi3,  16) ka7 Ia5-sou kong2, “In teh kong2 e5, Li2 u7 thiaN-kiN3 bo5?” Ia5-sou in3 kong2: “U7, tan7-si7 lin2 kam2 m7-bat thak8 tioh8 Seng3-keng kong2, “Li2 hou7 gin2-na2 kap ang-eN-a2 e5 chhui3 lai5 chan3-bi2 Li2.’”  17) Ia5-sou chiu7 li7-khui in, chhut hit e5 siaN5 khi3 kau3 Pek-tai7-ni5 SiaN5, ti7 hia keh-me5.

Ia5-sou chiu3-me7 bu5-hoe-ko2-chhiu7: (Kho2 11:12-14; 20:24)
	18) Keh-tng2 chai2-khi2, Ia5-sou boeh tng2 lai5 Ia5-lou7-sat-leng2 SiaN5 e5 si5, ti7 lou7-nih8 pak-tou2 chin iau.  19) I khoaN3-kiN3 lou7-nih8 u7 chit8 chang5 bu5-hoa-ko2-chhiu7, oa2-khi3 chit8-e7 khoaN3, chi2-u7 khoaN3-kiN3 hoih8, long2 bo5 koe2-chi2, chiu7 tui3 hit chang5 chhiu7 kong2, “Tui3 hian7-chai7 khi2, li2 eng2-oan2 be7 koh kiat koe2-chi2!” Hit chang5 bu5-hoa-ko2-chhiu7 sui5-si5 chiu7 ta-khi3.  20) Bun5-tou5 chit8-e7 khoaN3-kiN3 an2-ne, chiu7 toa7 tioh8-kiaN, kong2, “An3-choaN2 chit chang5 bu5-hoa-ko2-chhiu7 hut-jian5-kan ta-khi3?”  21) Ia5-sou ka7 bun5-tou5 in3 kong2: “Goa2 sit8-chai7 ka7 lin2 kong2, lin2 na7 u7 sin3-sim long2 bo5 giau5-gi5, put-tan7 Goa2 tui3 chit chang5 bu5-hoa-ko2-chhiu7 sou2 cho3 e5 lin2 ia7 e7-tang3 cho3, ji5-chhiaN2 lin2 e7-tang3 tui3 chit cho7 soaN kong2, ‘Khi2-lai5, khi3 thiam7-hai2!’ Chit cho7 soaN ia7 e7 chiau3 an2-ne sit8-hian7.  22) Lin2 na7 eng7 sin3-sim lai5 ki5-to2, lin2 it-teng7 e7 tit-tioh8 lin2 sou2 ki5-kiu5 e5 it-chhe3.”

Lun7 Ia5-sou e5 koan5-peng3: (Kho2 11:27-33; Lou7 20:1-8)
	23) Ia5-sou jip8-khi3 seng3-tian7, ti7 hia teh ka3-si7 lang5 e5 si5, chiah-e5 che3-si-tiuN2 kap I2-sek-liat8-lang5 e5 tiuN2-lo2 lai5 chhoe7 I, mng7 kong2, “Li2 eng7 sim2-mih koan5-peng3 lai5 cho3 chiah-e5 tai7-chi3? Chit e5 koan5-peng3 si7 sim2-mih lang5 hou7 Li2 e5 ?”  24) Ia5-sou in3 in kong2: “Goa2 ia7 boeh mng7 lin2 chit8 ku3 oe7, lin2 na7 ka7 Goa2 tap-hok8, Goa2 chiah boeh ka7 lin2 kong2 Goa2 eng7 sim2-mih koan5-peng3 lai5 cho3 chiah-e5 tai7-chi3.  25) Iok-han7 ka7 lang5 se2-le2 e5 koan5-peng3 si7 tui3 thiN lai5 e5, a2-si7 tui3 lang5 lai5 e5?" In hou7-siong gi7-lun7 kong2: “Lan2 na7-si7 kong2 ‘Tui3 thiN lai5 e5,’ Ia5-sou e7 mng7 lan2 kong2, ‘An2-ne lin2 an3-choaN2 bo5 boeh sin3 Iok-han7?’  26) Tan7-si7 lan2 na7-si7 kong2, ‘Tui3 lang5 lai5 e5,’ lan2 m7-ku2 kiaN cheng3-lang5, in-ui7 in long2 siuN7 kong2 Iok-han7 si7 tai7-gian5-jin5.”  27) In chiu7 in3 Ia5-sou kong2, “Goan2 m7 chai-iaN2.” Ia5-sou chiu7 tui3 in kong2, “An2-ne Goa2 ia7 bo5 boeh ka7 lin2 kong2 Goa2 eng7 sim2-mih koan5-peng3 lai5 cho3 chiah-e5 tai7-chi3.”

Nng7-e5 kiaN2-ji5 e5 phi3-ju7:
	28) “TaN lin2 siuN7 an3-choaN2? U7 chit8 e5 lang5, i u7 nng7-e5 kiaN2-ji5. I khi3 ka7 toa7-kiaN2 kong2, ‘KiaN2 a3! Li2 kin-na2-jit8 khi3 phu5-to5-hng5 cho3 khang-khoe3.’  29) I in3 kong2, ‘Goa2 m7 khi3,’ M7-ku2 au-lai7 i hoe5-sim choan2-i3 chiu7 khi3.  30) In lau7-pe7 ia7 khi3 ka7 te7-ji7 kiaN2 kong2 kang7-khoan2 e5 oe7. Te7-ji7 kiaN2 in3 kong2, ‘A-pa. goa2 boeh khi3.’ Tan7-si7 i bo5 khi3.  31) Chit nng7-e5 kiaN2 tah chit8 e5 sit8-chai7 u7 chiau3 in lau7-pe7 e5 i3-su3 khi3 cho3?” In kong2, “Si7 toa7-kiaN2.” Ia5-sou ka7 in kong2: “Goa2 sit8-chai7 ka7 lin2 kong2, chiah-e5 thiu-soe3 e5 lang5 kap ki-li2 e7 pi2 lin2 khah tai7-seng chin3-jip8 Siong7-chu2 e5 Kok.  32) In-ui7 Iok-han7 lai5 chi2-si7 lin2 kiaN5 Siong7-chu2 sou2 iau-kiu5 e5 lou7, tan7-si7 lin2 bo5 boeh sin3 i; m7-ku2 chiah-e5 thiu-soe3 e5 lang5 kap ki-li2 tian-to3 sin3 i. Sui-jian5 lin2 khoaN3-kiN3 chiah-e5 tai7-chi3, iau2-ku2 bo5 hoan2-hoe2 lai5 sin3 i.”

Phu5-to5-hng5 e5 tian7-long5 e5 phi3-ju7: (Kho2 12:1-12; Lou7 20:9-19)
	33) Ia5-sou kong2: “Lin2 koh thiaN leng7-goa7 chit8 e5 phi3-ju7. U7 chit8 e5 chu2-lang5 u7 chit8 te3 phu5-to5-hng5, eng7 chhiuN5-ui5-a2 ka7 i ui5 khi2-lai5, lai7-bin7 khui chit8 e5 chiu2-khut, khi2 chit8 e5 khan3-siu2-thah, chiong chit te3 hng5 chou hou7 tian7-long5, jian5-au7 chhut-khi3 li2-heng5.  34) Siu-seng5 phu5-to5 e5 si5 kau3, chu2-lang5 chiu7 chhe i kui2-na7 e5 lou5-pok8 khi3 tian7-long5 hia, boeh tui3 in siu hng5-chou.  35) Chiah-e5 tian7-long5 chiong i chiah-e5 lou5-pok8 liah8 khi2-lai5, chit8 e5 hou7 in phah, te7-ji7 e5 hou7 in thai5-si2, te7-saN e5 hou7 in eng7 chioh8-thau5 tim3.  36) Chu2-lang5 iu7-koh chhe chit8 tin7 lou5-pok8 khi3, pi2 te7-it pai2 khah che7 lang5; tan7-si7 chiah-e5 tian7-long5 ia7-si7 an2-ne tui3-thai7 in.  37) Choe3-au7 chu2-lang5 chhe i ka7-ti7 e5 kiaN2 khi3 in hia, I siuN7 kong2, ‘In it-teng7 e7 chun-keng3 goa2 e5 kiaN2.’  38) Tan7-si7 hiah-e5 tian7-long5 khoaN3-kiN3 i e5 kiaN2 lai5, chiu7 hou7-siong kong2, ‘Chit e5 si7 i e5 ke3-seng5-jin5. Lai5, lan2 lai5 ka7 i sat-hai7, thang lai5 tit-tioh8 i sou2 boeh ke3-seng5 e5 san2-giap8!’  39) In chiu7 ka7 i liah8 khi2-lai5, thoa i chhut-khi3 phu5-to5-hng5 e5 goa7-bin7, ka7 i thai5-si2.”
	40) Ia5-sou mng7 in kong2, “TaN phu5-to-hng5 e5 chu2-lang5 lai5 e5 si5, i e7 an3-choaN2 lai5 chhu2-li2 chiah-e5 tian7-long5?”  41) In ka7 I kong2: “I it-teng7 e7 thai5-si2 chiah-e5 phaiN2 lang5, chiong phut-to5-hng5 chou hou7 pat8 e5 e7-tang3 chiau3 siu-tang e5 si5 lap8-chou e5 tian7-long5.”  42) Ia5-sou tui3 in kong2: “Lin2 kam2 m7-bat thak8-tioh8 Seng3-keng u7 ki3-chai3 kong2:
‘Khi2-chhu3 sai-hu7 sou2 tan3-tiau7 e5 chioh8, soah pian3-cho3 siong7 tiong7-iau3 e5 ki-chioh8; che si7 Chu2 e5 chok-ui5, lan2 khoaN3-tioh8 hui-siong5 ki5-biau7.’
43) In-ui7 an2-ne, Goa2 ka7 lin2 kong2,Siong7-chu2 e5 Kok it-teng7 e7 tui3 lin2 tiong-kan ka7 lin2 chhiuN2-khi3, lai5 siuN2-su3 hou7 hiah-e5 heng5-ui5 hu5-hap8 Siong7-chu2 e5 Kok e5 peh-seN3.  ( 44) That-tioh8 chit te3 chioh8-thau5 lai5 poah8-to2 e5 lang5, it-teng7 long2 e7 chhui3-kut hun-sin; hou7 chit te3 chioh8-thau5 teh-tioh8 e5 lang5, it-teng7 long2 e7 chhui3-kou5-kou5.)”
	45) Chiah-e5 che3-si-tiuN2 kap Hoat-li7-sai3-phai3 e5 lang5 thiaN-kiN3 Ia5-sou e5 phi3-ju7, chai-iaN2 Ia5-sou si7 teh kong2 in,  46) chiu7 siuN7 boeh liah8 I, tan7-si7 kiaN cheng-lang5, in-ui7 cheng3-lang5 khoaN3 Ia5-sou si7 chit8 ui7 tai-gian5-jin5.

Te7 22 ChiuN

Hun-ian3 e5 phi2-ju7: (Lou7 14:15-24)
	1) Ia5-sou iu7-koh eng7 phi3-ju7 ka7 in kong2:  2) “Thian-kok chhin-chhiuN7 chit8 e5 kok-ong5 ka7 i e5 kiaN2 pi7-pan7 hun-ian3.  3) I chhe i e5 pok8-jin5 khi3 thong-ti hiah-e5 siu-tioh8 chhiaN2 -thiap e5 lang5-kheh lai5 hu3 hun-ian3, tan7-si7 in m7 lai5.  4) Kok-ong5 iu7-koh chhe chit8-koa2 pok8-jin5, hoan-hu3 in kong2: ‘Khi3 ka7 hiah-e5 sou2 chhiaN2 e5 lang5-kheh kong2, goa2 e5 toh i2-keng long2 pi7-pan7 ho2 a3. Goa2 e5 gu5 kap pui5 e5 gu5-a2-kiaN2 i2-keng thai5 a7. It-chhe3 long2 chun2-pi7 ho2 a3. ChhiaN2 lai5 hu3 hun-ian3!  5) Tan7-si7 hiah-e5 sou2 chhiaN2 e5 lang5-kheh long2 bo5 boeh chhap in, cho3 in khi3, chit8 e5 khi3 choh-sit, chit8 e5 khi3 cho3 seng-li2;  6) ki5-tha e5, liah8 hiah-e5 pok8-jin5 khi2-lai5, ka7 in phah, soah ka7 in thai5-si2.  7) Kok-ong5 hui-siong5 siu7-khi3, chiu7 phai3 kun-tui7 khi3 chau5-biat8 hiah-e5 hiong-hoan7, iu7-koh sio-hui2 in e5 siaN5-chhi7,  8) jian5-au7 ka7 i e5 pok8-jin5 kong2: ‘Hun-ian3 i2-keng chun2-pi7 ho2 a3, tan7-si7 i2-cheng5 sou2 chhiaN2 e5 lang5-kheh long2 be7-kham-tit hou7 lan2 chhiaN2.  9) TaN lin2 khi3 toa7-lou7-khau2, sou2 tu2-tioh8 e5 lang5 long2 ka7 in chhiaN2 lai5 hu3 hun-ian3.’  10) I e5 pok8-jin5 chiu7 chhut-khi3 toa7-lou7-khau2, bo5-lun7 ho2-phaiN2 lang5, in sou2 tu2-tioh8 e5 lang5 long2 ka7 in chhiaN2 lai5; sou2-i2 hun-ian3 e5 le2-tng5 lang5-kheh che7 kah moa2-moa2.”
	11) “Kok-ong5 jip8-lai5 khoaN3 hiah-e5 lang5-kheh e5 si5, khoaN3-kiN3 ti7 hia u7 chit8 e5 lang5 bo5 chheng7 le2-hok8.  12) Kok-ong5 chiu7 ka7 i mng7 kong2, ‘Peng5-iu2 a3! Li2 an3-choaN2 bo5 chheng7 le2-hok8 jip8-lai5 chia?’ Hit e5 lang5 tiam7-tiam7 bo5 oe7 thang in3.  13) Kok-ong5 chiu7 ka7 i pak8 khi2-lai5, ka7 i hiat chhut-khi3 goa7-bin7 ou-am3 e5 sou2-chai7.’ I e7 toa3 hia thi5-khau3 ka7-ge5 chhiat-khi2.”  14) Ia5-sou choe3-au7 ka7 in kong2, “Pi7 tiau3 e5 lang5 che7, tan7-si7 siu7 keng2-soan2 e5 lang5 chio2.”

Lap8 soe3-kim e5 bun7-te5: (Kho2 12:13-17; Lou7 20:20-26)
	15) Jian5-au7 Hoat-li7-sai3-phai3 e5 lang5 chhut-khi3 chham-siong5, siuN7 khoaN3 boeh an3-choaN2 lai5 liah8 Ia5-sou e5 oe7-phang7.  16) In chiu7 chhe in kui2-na7 e5 hak8-seng kap Hi-lut8-tong2 e5 lang5 khi3 Ia5-sou hia, ka7 I kong2: “Lau7-su, goan2 chai-iaN2 Li2 si7 chit8 e5 lau2-sit8-lang5, chiau3 chin-li2 lai5 ka3-si7 Siong7-chu2 e5 to7-li2. Li2 m7-kiaN poaN3-lang5, in-ui7 Li2 bo5 koan lang5 e5 bin7-sek lai5 kong2-oe7.  17) Sou2-i2 chhiaN2 Li2 ka7 goan2 kong2, lap8-soe3 hou7 Lo5-ma2 e5 hong5-te3 u7 hah8 lan2 e5 Lut8-hoat a2 bo5?’  18) Ia5-sou chai-iaN2 in e5 phaiN2 tong7-ki, chiu7 ka7 in kong2: “Gui7-sian7-chia2, lin2 an3-choaN2 siuN7-boeh eng7 kui2-ke3 lai5 ham7-hai7 Goa2?  19) Theh8 lap8-soe3 e5 gin5-oan5 lai5 hou7 Goa2 khoaN3!” In chiu7 theh8 chit8 e5 gin5-oan5 chhut-lai5 hou7 I.  20) Ia5-sou mng7 in kong2, “Chit e5 siong7 kap ji7-ho7 si7 sim2-mih lang5 e5?”  21) In in3 kong2, “Si7 hong5-te3 e5.” Ia5-sou chiu7 tui3 in kong2, “An2-ne, lin2 tioh8 chiong hong5-te3 e5 lap8 hou7 hong5-te3, chiong Siong7-chu2 e5 hian3 hou7 Siong7-chu2.”  22) In chit8-e7 thiaN-kiN3 an2-ne chin tioh8-kiaN, chiu7 li7-khui Ia5-sou cho3 in khi3.

Si2-lang5 hok8-hoat8 e5 bun7-te5: (Kho2 12:18-27; Lou7 20:27-40)
	23) Kang7 hit jit8, u7 chit8-koa2 Sat-thou2-kai-tong2 e5 lang5 lai5 kiN3 Ia5-sou. (In chu2-tiuN kong2 si2-lang5 be7 hok8-hoat8.) In mng7 Ia5-sou kong2:  24) “Lau7-su, Mou5-se kong2: ‘Na7 u7 lang5 bo5 seN kiaN2 chiu7 si2-khi3, i e5 sio2-ti7 tioh8 chhoa7 hiaN-so2 cho3 bou2, ui7-tioh8 a-hiaN lai5 thoan5-chong chiap-tai7.’  25) TaN khah-cha2 u7 chhit e5 hiaN-ti7, toa3 ti7 chia. Toa7 e5 chhoa7 bou2, bo5 seN kiaN2 chiu7 si2-khi3, lau5 i e5 bou2 hou7 i e5 sio2-ti7.  26) Te7-ji7 e5, te7-saN e5, it-tit8 kau3 te7-chhit e5 ia7 long2 si7 kang7-khoan2 cheng5-heng5.  27) Choe3-au7 hit e5 hu7-jin5-lang5 ia7 si2-khi3.  28) In-ui7 in chhit e5 long2 bat kap i kiat-hun koe3, taN hok8-hoat8 hit jit8, chit e5 hu7-jin5-lang5 kiu3-keng3 si7 tah chit8 e5 e5 bou2?’
	29) Ia5-sou in3 in kong2: “Lin2 toa7 m7-tioh8 a7! In-ui7 lin2 m7-bat Seng3-keng, ia7 bo5 beng5-pek8 Siong7-chu2 e5 tai7-leng5.  30) In-ui7 si2-lang5 hok8-hoat8 e5 si5, in e7 chhin-chhiuN7 thian-siong7 e5 thian-sai3, ia7 bo5 chhoa7 ia7 bo5 ke3.  31) Lun7 si2-lang5 hok8-hoat8 e5 su7, lin2 kam2 m7-bat thak8-tioh8 Siong7-chu2 tui3 lin2 sou2 kong2 e5 oe7, kong2:
32) ‘Goa2 chiu7-si7 A-pek-lah8-han2 e5 Siong7-chu2, I2-sat e5 Siong7-chu2, Nga2-kok e5 Siong7-chu2.’
I m7-si7 si2-lang5 e5 Siong7-chu2, si7 oah8-lang5 e5 Siong7-chu2!”  33) Cheng3-lang5 thiaN tioh8 I e5 ka3-si7 chiu7 chin tioh8-kiaN.

Choe3 tiong7-iau3 e5 kai3-beng7: (Kho2 12:28-34; Lou7 10:25-28)
	34) Hoat-li7-sai3-phai3 e5 lang5 thiaN-kiN3 Ia5-sou hou7 Sat-thou2-kai-tong2 e5 lang5 bo5 oe7 thang in3, chiu7 chu7-chip8 cho3-hoe2.  35) Ki5-tiong u7 chit8 e5 Lut8-hoat e5 choan-ka, siuN7-boeh chhi3-tham3 Ia5-sou,  36) chiu7 mng7 I kong2, “Lau7-su, Lut8-hoat e5 tiong-kan tah chit8 tiau5 kai3-beng7 siong7 iau3-kin2?”  37) Ia5-sou ka7 i kong2, ‘Li2 tioh8 choan5-sim, choan5-leng5, choan5-i3 keng3-ai3 Chu2 li2 e5 Siong7-chu2.’  38) Che si7 siong7 iau3-kin2, ia7-si7 te7-it tiau5 e5 kai3-beng7.  39) Te7-ji7 e5 ia7 chhin-chhiuN7 an2-ne: ‘Li2 tioh8 ai3 li2 e5 lin5-jin5 chhin-chhiuN7 ai3 li2 ka-ti7.’  40) It-chhe3 Mou5-se e5 Lut8-hoat kap chiong3 tai7-gian5-jin5 e5 ka3-si7, long2 pau-ham5 ti7 chit nng7 tiau5 kai3-beng7 e5 lai7-bin7.”

Iu2-koan Bi2-sai3-a e5 bun7-te5: (Kho2 12:35-37; Lou7 20:41-44)
	41) Hoat-li7-saiph3ai e5 lang5 chu7-chip8 e5 si5, Ia5-sou mng7 in kong2:  42) “Koan-he7 Bi2-sai3-a, lin2 siuN7 an3-choaN2? I si7 sim2-mih lang5 e5 kiaN2-sun?” In in3 kong2, “Si7 Tai7-pit8 e5 kiaN2-sun.”  43) Ia5-sou koh mng7 in kong2: “An2-ne an3-choaN2 Tai7-pit8 siu7 Seng3 Leng5 e5 kam2-tong7 lai5 chheng-hou Bi2-sai3-a cho3 Chu2? In-ui7 Tai7-pit8 kong2:
44) ‘Siong7-chu2 tui3 goa2 e5 Chu2 kong2: Che7 toa3 Goa2 e5 chiaN3-peng5, it-tit8 kau3 Goa2 chiong Li2 e5 tek8-jin5 cho3 kha-tiam7 lai5 hou7 Li2 khoe3-kha.’
45) Tai7-pit8 ki3-jian5 chheng-hou I cho3 Chu2, bi2-sai3-a na2 e7 lai5 cho3 Tai7-pit8 e5 kiaN2-sun?”  46) Bo5 lang5 e7-tang3 in3 Ia5-sou poaN3 ku3 oe7, tui3 hit jit8 khi2 ia7 bo5 lang5 kaN2 koh lai5 mng7 I. 

Te7 23 ChiuN

Tioh8 ti5-hong5 keng-hak8-chia2 kap Hoat-li7-sai3-phai3 e5 lang5: (Kho2 12:38-39; Lou7 11:43,46; 20:45-46)
	1) Hit e5 si5 Ia5-sou ka7 cheng3-lang5 kap I e5 bun5-tou5 kong2:  2) “Keng-hak8-chia2 kap Hoat-li7-sai3-phai3 e5 lang5 ke3-seng5 Mou5-se e5 koan5-peng3 lai5 kai2-sek Lut8-hoat.  3) Sou2-i2 in sou2 ka7 lin2 kong2 e5, lin2 tioh8 sit8-heng5 chun-siu2, tan7-si7 m7-thang oh8 in e5 heng5-ui5, in-ui7 in bo5 sit8-heng5 in sou2 ka3-si7 e5.  4) In chiong chin tang7, hou7 lang5 taN bo5 hoat-tit e5 taN3, lai5 he7 toa3 pat8-lang5 e5 keng-thau5 teng2; tna7-si7 ka-ti7 lian5 chit8 ki chng2-thau5-a2 ia7 m7-kheng2 tin2-tang7, lai5 kiam2-khin pat8-lang5 e5 tang7-taN3.  5) In sou2 cho3 it-chhe3 e5 tai7-chi3, long2 si7 ui7-tioh8 boeh hou7 cheng3-lang5 khoaN3, in-ui7 in chiong teh ki5-to2 e5 si5 pak8 toa3 thau5-hiah8 a2-si7 tiau3 toa3 chhiu2-au7-khiau e5 keng-ap8-a2 kou3-i3 cho3 khah toa7, chiong goa7-tho3 saN-a2-ki e5 chhiu cho3 kah chin tng5.  6) Ti7 ian3-sek8  che7-toh ai3 che7 toa7-ui7, ti7 hoe7-tng5 ai3 che7 koan5 e5 ui7,  7) ti7 ke-chhi7 ai3 lang5 ka7 in kiaN5 toa7-le2, ai3 lang5 chheng-hou in lau7-su.  8) Tan7-si7, in-ui7 lin2 hou7-siong long2 si7 hiaN-ti7, iu7-koh chi2-u7 chit8 ui7 Lau7-su na7-tiaN7.  9) Ti7 se3-kan ia7 m7-thang sui5-pian7 chheng-hou lang5 cho3 lin2 e5 lau7-pe7, in-ui7 lin2 chi2-u7 chit8 ui7 Thian-hu7.  10) Lin2 ia7 m7-thang hou7 lang5 chheng-hou cho3 leng2-siu7, in-ui7 lin2 e5 leng2-siu7 chi2-u7 chit8-ui7, chiu7-si7 Bi2-sai3-a.  11) Lin2 tiong-kan te7-it ui2-tai7 e5 tioh8 cho3 lin2 e5 pok8-jin5.  12) Chu7-ko e5 lang5 it-teng7 e7 siu7 ap-ke7, chu7-khiam e5 lang5 it-teng7 e7 siu7 the5-ko.”

Ia5-sou chek-pi7 gui7-sian7-chia2: (Kho2 12:40; Lou7 11:39-42,44,52; 20:47)
	13) “Lin2 chiah-e5 gui7-sian7 e5 keng-hak8-chia2 kap Hoat-li7-sai3-phai3 e5 lang5, tioh8 u7 chai-ho7! Lin2 toa3 lang5 e5 bin7-cheng5 chiong Thian-kok e5 mng5 koaiN khi2-lai5. Lin2 pun2-sin bo5 boeh jip8-khi3, iu7-koh boeh jip8-khi3 e5 lang5, lin2 ia7 m7 hou7 in jip8-khi3.”
	( 14) “Lin2 chiah-e5 gui7-sian7 e5 keng-hak8-chia2 kap Hoat-li7-sai3-phai3 e5 lang5, tioh8 u7 chai-ho7! Lin2 chit8 hong-bin7 thun-chiam3 chiu2-koaN2-lang5 e5 ke-hoe2, chit8 hong-bin7 ke2-i3 ki5-to2 chin ku2. Lin2 it-teng7 e7 siu7 tioh8 koh-khah giam5-tiong7 e5 heng5-hoat8.”)
	15) “Lin2 chiah-e5 gui7-sian7 e5 keng-hak8-chia2 kap Hoat-li7-sai3-phai3 e5 lang5, tioh8 u7 chai-ho7! Ui7-tioh8 boeh tit-tioh8 chit8 e5 lang5 kai2-chong jip8-kau3, lin2 kiaN5-thau3 hai2-iuN5 liok8-te7, tan7-si7 i jip8-kau2 liau2-au7, lin2 chiu7 hou7 i pian3-cho3 pi2 lin2 teng5-poe7 sia5-ok, tioh8 loh8 te7-gak8 e5 lang5.”
	16) “Lin2 chiah-e5 chheN-me5 e5 chi2-to7-chia2, tioh8 u7 chai-ho7! Lin2 kong2: ‘Lang5 na7 chi2 Seng3-tian7 lai5 chiu3-choa7 chiu7 bo5 hau7-lek8, tan7-si7 na7 chi2 Seng3-tian7 lai7 e5 ng5-kim lai5 chiu3-choa7 e5 lang5, it-teng7 tioh8 sit8-heng5 sou2 chiu3 e5 choa7.’  17) Lin2 chiah-e5 chheN-me5 koh gong7 e5 lang5 a3! Tau3-te2 ng5-kim khah tiong7-iau3, a2-si7 hit e5 hou7 ng5-kim chiaN5-cho3 sin5-seng3 e5 Seng3-tian7 khah tiong7-iau3?  18) Lin2 ia7 kong2: ‘Lang5 na7 chi2 che3-toaN5 lai5 chiu3-choa7 chiu7 bo5 hau7-lek8, tan7-si7 na7 chi2 che3-toaN5 ten2 e5 seng-le2 lai5 chiu3-choa7 e5 lang5, it-teng7 tioh8 sit8-heng5 sou2 chiu3 e5 choa7.’  19) Lin2 chiah-e5 chheN-me5 e5 lang5 a3! Tau3-te2 seng-le2 khah tiong7-iau3, a2-si7 hit e5 hou7 seng-le2 chiaN5-cho3 sin5-seng3 e5 che3-toaN5 khah tiong7-iau3?  20) Sou2-i2 lang5 na7 chi2 che3-toaN5 lai5 chiu3-choa7, chiu7-si7 chi2 che3-toaN5 kap che3-toaN5 teng2 it-chhe3 sou2 u7 e5 lai5 chiu3-choa7.  21) Lang5 na7 chi2 Seng3-tian7 lai5 chiu3-choa7, chiu7-si7 chi2 Seng3-tian7 kap toa3 ti7 Seng3-tian7 lai7-bin7 e5 Siong7-chu2 lai5 chiu3-choa7.  22) Lang5 na7 chi2 thiN lai5 chiu3-choa7, chiu7-si7 chi2 Siong7-chu2 e5 po2-cho7 kap che7 ti7 po2-cho7 siong7 Hit-ui7 Siong7-chu2 lai5 chiu3-choa7.”
	23) “Lin2 chiah-e5 gui7-sian7 e5 keng-hak8-chia2 kap Hoat-li7-sai3-phai3 e5 lang5, tioh8 u7 chai-ho7! Lin2 chiau3 koan3-le7 to u7 teh hong7-hian3 chap8-hun chi it e5 phang-liau7 --- chhin-chhiuN7 poh8-ho5, pek-kak, sio2-hoe5-hiang teng2 hou7 Siong7-chu2, tan7-si7 lin2 long2 bu5-si7 Lut8-hoat sou2 iau-kiu5 koh-khah tiong7-iau3 e5, chhin-chhiuN7 kong-cheng3, jin5-chu5, sin3-sit8 teng2 e5 ka3-si7. Chiah-e5 ka3-si7 lin2 it-teng7 tioh8 sit8-heng5, tan7-si7 thau5-cheng5 sou2 theh8-khi2 hiah-e5 koan3-le7 ia7 m7-thang hut-liok8.  24) Lin2 chiah-e5 chheN-me5 e5 leng2-to7-chia2! lin2 chit8 chiah bang2-thang5 ia7 sio2-sim tui3 im2-liau7 tiong ka7 i li7 chhut-lai5, tan7-si7 kui chiah lok8-to5 ia7 ka7 i thun loh8-khi3!”
	25) Lin2 chiah-e5 gui7-sian7 e5 keng-hak8-chia2 kap Hoat-li7-sai3-phai3 e5 lang5, tioh8 u7 chai-ho7! Lin2 chiong te5-au-a2 kap oaN2-poaN5 e5 goa7-bin7 chhit kah chin chheng-khi3, m7-ku2 lai7-bin7 chhiong-moa2 tham-iok8 kap hong3-chhiong3.  26) ChheN-me5 e5 Hoat-li7-sai3-phai3 e5 lang5 a3! Lin2 tioh8 tai7-seng chheng te5-au-a2 e5 lai7-bin7 hou7 chheng-khi3, an2-ne goa7-bin7 ia7 chu7-jian5 e7 chheng-khi3!”
	27) “Lin2 chiah-e5 gui7-sian7 e5 keng-hak8-chia2 kap Hoat-li7-sai3-phai3 e5 lang5, tioh8 u7 chai-ho7! Lin2 chhin-chhiuN7 chhat kah peh8-peh8-peh8 e5 bong7, goa7-bin7 khoaN3 khi2-lai5 chin sui2, tan7-si7 lai7-bin7 chhiong-moa2 si2-lang5 e5 kut-thau5 kap kok chiong2 hu2-pai7 e5 mih8-kiaN7.  28) Kap an2-ne kang7-khoan2, lin2 e5 goa7-piau2 chhin-chhiuN7 gi7-jin5, m7-ku2 lai7-bin7 chhiong-moa2 gui7-sian7 kap put-hoat.”

Ia5-sou i7-ko3 gui7-sian7-chia2 kai-siu7 heng5-hoat8: (Lou7 11:47-51)
29) “Lin2 chiah-e5 gui7-sian7 e5 keng-hak8-chia2 kap Hoat-li7-sai3-phai3 e5 lang5, tioh8 u7 chai-ho7! Lin2 kian3-cho7 tai7-gian5-jin5 e5 bong7, chong-sek gi7-jin5 e5 ki3-liam7-pi;  30) lin2 ia7 kong2 ‘Ka2-su2 goan2 na7 chhut-si3 ti7 goan2 e5 chou2-sian e5 si5-tai7, goan2 it-teng7 be7 kap in kiong7-bou5 lai5 sat-hai7 tai7-gian5-jin5.’  31) An2-ne sit8-che3 siong7 lin2 si7 teh cheng3-beng5 lin2 pun2-sin chiu7-si7 hiah-e5 bou5-sat tai7-gian5-lin5 e5 lang5 e5 kiaN2-sun!  32) TaN lin2 khi3 oan5-seng5 lin2 e5 chou2-sian cho3 iau2-boe7 liau2 ok-tok8 e5 tia7-chi3.  33) Lin2 chiah-e5 tok8-choa5 e5 kiaN2-sun! Kan-kui2 e5 lang5 a3! Lin2 kam2 e7-tang3 to5-pi7 te7-gak8 e5 heng5-hoat8?  34) Sou2-i2 Goa2 boeh chhe-phai3 tai7-gian5-jin5, hian5-ti3 e5 lang5 i2-kip8 u7 hak8-bun7 e5 lang5 khi3 lin2 hia; u7-e5 e7 hou7 lin2 sat-hai7, u7-e5 e7 hou7 lin2 teng3 sip8-ji7-ke3, u7-e5 e7 toa3 lin2 e5 hoe7-tng5 hou7 lin2 eng7 piN phah, u7-e5 e7 hou7 lin2 tui3 chit8 e5 siaN5-chhi7 koaN2 koe3 chit8 e5 siaN5-chhi7.  35) An2-ne ti7 chit e5 te7-siong7 thai5-si2 gi7-jin5 e5 hoeh-che3 long2 e7 kui hou7 lin2, chiu7-si7 tui3 bou5-sat gi7-jin5 A-pek khai-si2, it-tit8 kau3 lin2 ti7 seng3-sou2 kap che3-toaN5 e5 tiong-kan sou2 thai5-si2 e5 Pa-liap8-ka e5 kiaN2 Sat-ka-li7-a ui5-chi2.  36) Goa2 sit8-chai7 ka7 lin2 kong2: chiah-e5 hoeh-che3 long2 e7 kui hou7 chit tai7 e5 lang5.”

Ia5-sou ui7 Ia5-lou7-sat-leng2 pi-siong: (Lou7 13:34-35)
	37) “Ia5-lou7-sat-leng2 SiaN5 a3, Ia5-lou7-sat-leng2 SiaN5! Li2 sat-hai7 tai7-gian5-jin5, eng7 chioh8-thau5 tim3-si2 Siong7-chu2 chhe-phai3 lai5 li2 chia e5 su3-chia2! Goa2 loa7-che7 pai2 ai3 boeh chu7-chip8 li2 e5 kiaN2-ji5 jip8 Goa2 e5 hoai5-pau, chhin-chhiuN7 ke-bo2 khou i e5 ke-a2-kiaN2 lai5 aN3 toa3 sit8-kou2-e7, tan7-si7 lin2 ka7 Goa2 ki7-choat8!  38) Lin2 khoaN3! Lin2 e5 chhu3 it-teng7 e7 hong-hoe3.  39) Goa2 ka7 lin2 kong2, chiong5-kim i2-au7, lin2 choat8-tui3 be7-tang3 koh khoaN3-kiN3 Goa2, it-tit8 kau3 lin2 kong2, ‘Hong7 Chu2 e5 mia5 lai5 e5, eng-kai siu7 chan3-bi2!’”

Te7 24 ChiuN

Ia5-sou i7-gian5 Seng3-tian7 e5 hui2-biat8: (Kho2 13:1-2; Lou7 21:5-6)
	1) Ia5-sou tui3 Seng3-tian7 chhut-lai5 teh kiaN5-lou7 e5 si5, I e5 bun5-tou5 chiu7 oa2-lai5 po3 I khoaN3 Seng3-tian7 e5 kian3-tiok-but8.  2) Ia5-sou ka7 in kong2: “Lin2 teh khoaN3 chiah-e5 kian3-tiok-but8, si7 bo5? Goa2 sit8-chai7 ka7 lin2 kong2: chiong-lai5 ti7 chit e5 sou2-chai7 bo5 chit8 te3 chioh8 e7 sio-thah8, long2 e7 to2 kah peN5-peN5 khi3.”

Chai-lan7 e5 khai-si2: (Kho2 13:3-13; Lou7 21:7-19)
	3) Ia5-sou che7 ti7 Kan-na2-soaN teng2 e5 si5, bun5-tou5 thau mng7 Ia5-sou kong2: “ChhiaN2 Li2 ka7 goan2 kong2, sim2-mih si5 e7 hoat-seng chiah-e5 tai7-chi3? Li2 e5 chai3-lim5 kap se3-kai3 e5 boat8-jit8, u7 sim2-mih chian5-tiau7?”
	4) Ia5-sou in3-tap in kong2: “Tioh8 chu3-i3, m7-thang hou7 lang5 be5-hek8 khi3.  5) In-ui7 u7 chin-che7 lang5 e7 mou7-iong7 Goa2 e5 mia5 lai5 kong2, ‘goa2 chiu7-si7 Bi2-sai3-a’ lai5 be5-hek8 chin-che7 lang5.  6) Lin2 e7 thiaN-kiN3 hu7-kin7 chian3-cheng e5 siaN, ia7 e7 thiaN-kiN3 hng7-hng7 u7 chian3-cheng e5 hong-siaN, tan7-si7 tioh8 sio2-sim m7-thang tioh8-kiaN! Chiah-e5 su7-cheng5 it-teng7 tioh8 hoat-seng, tan7-si7 chiong-kiok8 iau2-boe7 kau3.  7) In-ui7 bin5-chok8 e7 khi2-lai5 kong-kek bin5-chok8, kok-ka kong-kek kok-ka; chin-che7 sou2-chai7 e7 hoat-seng ki-hng kap te7-tang7.  8) Che it-chhe3 put-ko3 si7 ui7-tioh8 boeh san2-seng sin ki2-goan5 thong3-khou2 e5 khai-si2 na7-tiaN7.”
	9) “Hit e5 si5 lang5 e7 liah8 lin2 khi3 kau hou7 lang5 heng5-hoat8. In ia7 e7 sat-hai7 lin2. Lin2 ui7-tioh8 Goa2 e5 ian5-kou3 e7 siu7 ban7-bin5 e5 oan3-hin7.  10) Hit e5 si5 u7 chin-che7 lang5 e7 sit-loh8 sin3-sim. In e7 hou7-siong chhut-be7, hou7-siong oan3-hin7,  11) ia7 u7 chin-che7 ke2 tai7-gian5-jin5 e7 chhut-hian7 lai5 be5-hek8 chin-che7 lang5.  12) Put-hoat e5 tai7-chi3 e7 lu2 cheng7-ka. Chin-che7 lang5 e5 ai3-sim chiu7 e7 leng2-tam7 khi3.  13) Tan7-si7 kian-jim2 kau3 choe3-au7 e5 lang5, it-teng7 e7 tit-tioh8 kiu3.  14) Chit e5 Thian-kok e5 Hok-im e7 thoan5-iong5 kau3 phou2 thian-ha7, tui3 ban7-bin5 cho3 kian3-cheng3, jian5-au7 chiong-kiok8 chiu7 e7 kau3.”

Toa7 chai-lan7: (Kho2 13:14-23; Lou7 21:20-24)
	15) “Lin2 na7 thiaN-kiN3 tai7-gian5-jin5 Tan7-i2-li2 sou2 kong2 ‘Hit e5 kho2-ouN3 e5 hui2-biat8-chia2’ khia7 toa3 seng3 e5 sou2-chai7, --- ( thak8 e5 lang5 tioh8 li2-kai2) ---  16) hit e5 si5 toa3 ti7 Iu5-thai3 Seng2 e5 lang5, tioh8 to5-chau2 khi3 soaN-teng2;  17) ti7 chhu3-teng2 e5 lang5, m7-thang loh8-lai5 theh8 chhu3-lai7 e5 mih8-kiaN7;  18) ti7 chhan5-nih8 e5 lang5, ia7 m7-thang tng2-khi3 hiahN i e5 goa7-saN.  19) Hit e5 si5-ki5, u7 sin-in7 e5 hu7-jin5-lang5 kap hou7 eN-a2 chiah8 leng e5 lau7-bo2, sit8-chai7 chin put-heng7!  20) Lin2 tioh8 ki5-kiu5 Siong7-chu2, hou7 lin2 to5-lan7 e5 si5 be7 chai7 tang-thiN-si5 a2-si7 An-hioh-jit8 hoat-seng.  21) In-ui7 hit e5 si5-ki5 e7 u7 toa7 chai-lan7. Chit khoan2 chai-lan7 si7 tui3 chhong3-cho7 u2-tiu7 kau3 hian7-chai7 m7-bat u7 e5; chiong-lai5 ia7 choat8-tui3 be7 koh u7.  22) Hiah-e5 jit8-chi2 na7 bo5 chhek khah te2, chiu7 bo5 chit8 e5 lang5 e7-tang3 tit-tioh8 kiu3. Tan7-si7 Siong7-chu2 e7 ui7-tioh8 I e5 soan2-bin5, siok-toan2 hiah-e5 jit8-chi2.”
	23) “Hit e5 si5 na7 u7 lang5 ka7 lin2 kong2, ‘Lin2 khoaN3! Bi2-sai3-a ti7 chia!’ A2-si7 kong2, ‘Bi2-sai3-a ti7 hia!’, lin2 m7-thang siong-sin3.  24) In-ui7 ke2 Bi2-sai3-a kap ke2 tai7-gian5-jin5 e7 chhut-hian7 lai5 cho3 toa7 e5 sin5-chek kap ki5-su7, chin7-liong7 boeh lai5 be5-hek8 Siong7-chu2 e5 soan2-bin5.  25) Chit e5 tai7-chi3, Goa2 su7-sian ka7 lin2 keng2-ko3 a3.”
	26) “Sou2-i2 na7 u7 lang5 ka7 lin2 kong2, ‘Lin2 khoaN3! Bi2-sai3-a ti7 khong3-ia2!’ Lin2 m7-thang chhut-khi3; a2-si7 kong2, ‘Lin2 khoaN3! I ti7 pang5-keng lai7!’ Lin2 ia7 m7-thang siong-sin3.  27) In-ui7 chhin-chhiuN7 sih-na3 tui3 tang-peng5 sih, chio3 kau3 sai-peng5, Jin5-chu2 e5 chai3-lim5 ia7 si7 kap an2-ne kang7-khoan2.”
	28) “U7 sin-si e5 sou2-chai7 eng-a2 chiu7 e7 chu7-chip8 khi3 hia.”

Jin5-chu2 e5 chai3-lim5: (Kho2 13:24-27; Lou7 21:25-28)
	29) “Chiah-e5 chai-lan7 e5 jit8-chi2 chit8-e7 koe3, jit8-thau5 e7 ou-am3 khi3, goeh8 be7 hoat-chhut kng, chheN e7 tui3 thiN loh8-lai5, thiN-teng2 e5 ban7-siong7 long2 e7 tong7-iau5.  30) Hit e5 si5 Jin5-chu2 chai3-lim5 e5 i7-tiau7 e7 chhut-hian7 toa3 khong-tiong, te7-siong7 e5 kok chiong2-chok8 long2 e7 thi5-khau3, ia7 e7 khoaN3-kiN3 Jin5-chu2 toa3 toa7 koan5-leng5 kap eng5-iau7 che7 thiN-teng2 e5 hun5 kang3 loh8-lai5.  31) I e7 chhe-phai3 I e5 thian-sai3, pun5 hiang2-liang7 e5 la-pa kau3 si3-hng, tui3 thiN-piN hai2-kak chu7-chip8 I e5 soan2-bin5.”

Bu5-hoa-ko2-chhiu7 e5 kau3-hun3: (Kho2 13:28-31; Lou7 21:29-33)
	32) “Lin2 tioh8 tui3 bu5-hoa-ko2-chhiu7 lai5 hak8-sip8 chit8 e5 kau3-hun3. Chhiu7-oe chit8-e7 puh-iN2 hoat-hioh8 chhut-lai5 e5 si5, lin2 chiu7 chai-iaN2 he7-thiN teh-boeh kau3 a3.  33) Kap an2-ne kang7-khoan2, lin2 na7 khoaN3-tioh8 chiah-e5 tai7-chi3 e5 si5, lin2 chiu7 chai-iaN2 Jin5-chu2 i2-keng teh-boeh kau3 a3, sit8-chai7 lai5 kau3 mng5-khau2 a3!  34) Goa2 sit8-chai7 ka7 lin2 kong2! Chit se3-tai7 e5 lang5 iau2-boe7 si2 i2-cheng5, chiah-e5 it-chhe3 e5 tai7-chi3 tek-khak e7 hoat-seng.  35) ThiN-te7 e7 siau-biat8, tan7-si7 Goa2 e5 oe7 choat8-tui3 be7 siau-biat8.”

Bo5 lang5 chai-iaN2 hit e5 jit8-chi2 a2-si7 si5-khek: (Kho2 13:32-37; Lou7 17:26-30. 34-36)
	36) “Tan7-si7 koan-he7 hit e5 jit8-chi2 a2-si7 hit e5 si5-khek long2 bo5 lang5 chai-iaN2, lian5 KiaN2 ia7 m7 chai-iaN2; chi2-u7 Thian-hu7 chai-iaN2 na7-tiaN7.  37) Jin5-chu2 chai3-lim5 e5 si5 ia7 e7 chhin-chhiuN7Na2-a e5 si5-tai7 e5 cheng5-heng5.  38) Chiu7-si7 Toa7-chui2 iau2-boe7 lai5 e5 si5, lang5 chiau3-siong5 lim-chiah8 ke3-chhoa7, it-tit8 kau3 Na2-a jip8-khi3 toa7-chun5 hit jit8;  39) in long2 bo5 gi5-gou7  Toa7-chui2 e7 ka7 in chhiong liau2-liau2 khi3. Jin5-chu2 e5 chai3-lim5 e5 si5 ia7 e7 an2-ne.  40) Hit e5 si5 nng7 e5 lang5 ti7 chhan5-nih8, chit8 e5 e7 siu7 chhiuN2 chau2 khi3, chit8 e5 e7 lau5-toa3 hia;  41) nng7 e5 hu7-jin5-lang5 teh e chioh8-bo7, chit8 e5 e7 siu7 chhiuN2-chau2 khi3, chit8 e5 e7 lau5 toa3 hia.  42) Sou2-i2 lin2 tioh8 keng2-seng2, in-ui7 lin2 m7-chai lin2 e5 Chu2 tah chit8 jit8 e7 lai5.  43) Ka2-su2 chit8 ke e5 chu2-lang5 na7 chai-iaN2 am3-si5 kui2-tiam2 chhat8-a2 e7 lai5, i it-teng7 e7 chheN2-chheN2 teh kou3, be7 hou7 chhat8-a2 ou2 piah-khang jip8-lai5 i e5 chhu3-lai7. Che si7 chu7-beng5 chi li2.  44) Sou2-i2 lin2 tioh8 chun2-pi7 pian7-pian7, in-ui7 lin2 bo5 gi5-gou7 e5 si5 Jin5-chu2 e7 lai5.”

Tiong-sit8 kap bo5 tiong-sit8 e5 pok8-jin5: (Lou7 12:41-48)
	45) “Kiu3-keng3 sim2-mih lang5 si7 tiong-sit8 koh chhong-beng5 e5 lou5-pok8? I chiu7-si7 chu2-lang5 kau-tai3 i koan2 ki5-tha e5 lou5-pok8, chiau3-si5 hun-phoe3 chiah8-mih8 hou7 in hit e5 lang5.  46) I e5 chu2-lang5 tng2-lai5 khoaN3 tioh8 i an2-ne teh cho3 e5 si5, hit e5 lou5-pok8 chiu7 sit8-chai7 u7 hok-khi3!  47) Goa2 sit8-chai7 ka7 lin2 kong2, chu2-lang5 e7 chiong i it-chhe3 e5 chai5-san2 ui2-thok i koan2-li2.  48) Ka2-su2 i si7 chit8 e5 phaiN2 e5 lou5-pok8, i ka-ti7 sim-lai7 e7 siuN7 kong2, ‘goa2 e5 chu2-lang5 koh chin ku2 chiah e7 tng2-lai5’,  49) chiu7 khai-si2 phah i e5 tong7-su7, koh kap chiu2-sian cho3-hoe2 lim-chiah8.  50) Hit e5 lou5-pok8 bo5 gi5-gou7 e5 jit8, siuN7 be7 kau3 e5 si5, i e5 chu2-lang5 e7 tng2-lai5.  51) Chu2-lang5 e7 tang7-tang7 ka7 i heng5-hoat8, hou7 i kap gui7-sian7 e5 lang5 tu2-tioh8 kang7-khoan2 e5 mia7-un7. I e7 toa3 hia thi5-khau3, ka7-ge5 chhiat khi2.”

Te7 25 ChiuN7

Chap8 e5 chai7-sek-li2 e5 phi3-ju7:
	1) “Thian-kok chhin-chhiuN7 e7-bin7 e5 phi3-ju7: u7 chap8 e5 chai7-sek-li2, giah8 in e5 teng-hoe2 chhut-khi3 geng5-chiap sin-long5.  2) In tiong-kan u7 gou7 e5 gong7 e5, u7 gou7 e5 chhong-beng5 e5.  3) Gong7 e5 sui-jian5 u7 giah8 in e5 teng-hoe2, m7-ku2 bo5 leng7-goa7 toa3 iu5.  4) Chhong-beng5 e5 giah8 in e5 teng-hoe2, iu7-koh leng7-goa7 u7 toa3 iu5 te2 ti7 iu5-pan5.  5) Sin-long5 khah ban7 lai5, in soah long2 tuh-ku, chiu7 khun3-khi3.”
	6) “Kau3 poaN3-me5, u7 lang5 toa7-siaN hoah kong2, ‘Khi2-lai5, sin-long5 lai5 lou3! Lin2 chhut-lai5 geng5-chiap i!’  7) Hit e5 si5 hiah-e5 chai7-sek-li2 long2 chheN2 khi2-lai5, chun2-pi7 tiam2-teng.  8) Gong7 e5 ka7 chhong-beng5 e5 kong2, ‘Lin2 e5 iu5 tam7-poh8-a2 pun goan2. Goan2 e5 teng-hoe2 teh-boeh hoa-khi3 a3.’  9) Chhong-beng5 e5 ka7 in in3 kong2, ‘Be7 eng7-tit! KiaN-liau2 goan2 e5 iu5 bo5-kau3 lan2 kong-ke eng7. Lin2 leng5-kho2 ka-ti7 khi3 ka7 be7-iu5-e5 be2 khah hou2.’  10) Hiat-e5 gong7 e5 khi3 teh be2 iu5 e5 si5, sin-long5 kau3 a3. Hit gou7 e5 chun2-pi7 pian7-pian7 e5, chiu7 kap sin-long5 jip8-khi3 hu3 hun-ian3. Mng5 chiu7 koaiN khi2-lai5.”
	11) “Au7-lai5 hiah-e5 khi3 be2 iu5 e5 chai7-sek-li2 tng2-lai5, phah-mng5 kio3 kong2, ‘Sin-seN a3! Sin-seN a2! ChhiaN2 ka7 goan2 khui mng5!’  12) Tan7-si7 sin-long5 in3 kong2, ‘Goa2 sit8-chai7 ka7 lin2 kong2, Goa2 m7-bat lin2!’”  13) Ia5-sou choe3-au7 kong2, “Lin2 tioh8 keng2-seng2, in-ui7 lin2 m7 chai-iaN2 Chu2 e5 lai5-lim5 hit e5 jit8-chi2, ia7 m7 chai-iaN2 hit e5 si5-khek.”

SaN e5 lou5-pok8 e5 phi3-ju7: (Lou7 19:11-27)
	14) “Thian-kok ia7 chhin-chhiuN7 e7-bin7 e5 phi3-ju7: u7 chit8 e5 lang5 teh-boeh chhut-kok, i chiu7 kio3 i e5 lou5-pok8 lai5, chiong i e5 chai5-san2 kau-tai3 in.  15) I chiau3 kok-lang5 e5 chai5-leng5 kau-tai3 chai5-san2 hou7 in; chit8 e5 hou7 i gou7-chheng niu2 gin5, chit8 e5 hou7 i nng7-chheng, chit8 e5 hou7 i chit8-chheng, jian5-au7 i chiu7 chhut-hoat khi3.  16) Hit e5 nia2 gou7-chheng e5, sui5-si5 theh8 khi3 cho3 seng-li2, leng7-goa7 koh than3 gou7-chheng.  17) Hit e5 nia2 nng7-chheng e5, ia7 kang-khoan2, leng7-goa7 koh than3 nng7-chheng.  18) Tan7-si7 hit e5 nia2 chit8-chheng e5, chhut-khi3, thou5-kha kut8 chit8 khang, chiu7 chiong chu2-lang5 e5 chiN5 tai5 khi2-lai5.”
	19) “Keng-koe3 chin-ku2, chiah-e5 lou5-pok8 e5 chu2-lang5 tng2-lai5, chiu7 kap in sng3-siau3.  20) Hit e5 nia2 gou7-chheng e5 chiu7 lai5, ke theh8 gou7-chheng chhut-lai5, kong2: ‘Thau5-ke, li2 kau-tai3 goa2 gou7-chheng niu2 gin5; li2 khoaN3, goa2 leng7-goa7 koh than3 gou7-chheng.’  21) Chu2-lang5 ka7 i kong2: ‘Chin ho2, li2 si7 chit8 e5 ho koh chin7-tiong e5 lou5-pok8! Li2 ki3-jian5 tui3 sio2-sio2 e5 tai7-chi3 to kho3-tit-chu7, goa2 boeh hou7 li2 koan2-li2 chin toa7 e5 tia7-chi3; li2 jip8-lai5 hun-hiong2 goa2 e5 hi2-lok8!’  22) Jian5-au7 hit e5 nia2 nng7-chheng e5 ia7 lai5, kong2: ‘Thau5-ke, li2 kau-tai3 goa2 nng7-chheng; li2 khoaN3, goa2 leng7-goa7 koh than3 nng7-chheng.’  23) Chu2-lang5 ka7 i kong2: ‘Chin ho2, li2 si7 chit8 e5 ho2 koh chin7-tiong e5 lou5-pok8! Li2 ki3-jian5 tui3 sio2-sio2 e5 tai7-chi3 to kho3-tit-chu7, goa2 boeh hou7 li2 koan2-li2 chin toa7 e5 tai7-chi3; li2 jip8-lai5 hun-hiong2 goa2 e5 hi2-lok8!’   24) Choe3-au7 hit e5 nia2 chit8-chheng e5 ia7 lai5, kong2: ‘Thau5-ke, goa2 chai-iaN2 li2 si7 chit8 ui7 chin khek-pok8 e5 lang5, bo5 ia7-cheng2 ia7 boeh siu-seng5, bo5 cheng3-choh ia7 boeh siu-koah.  25) Goa2 sit8-chai7 chin kiaN, sou2-i2 chiong li2 e5 chiN5 heng5 li2.’  26) Chu2-lang5 in3 i kong2: ‘Li2 chit e5 kho2-ouN3 koh pin7-toaN7 e5 lou5-pok8! Li2 ki3-jian5 chai-iaN2 goa2 bo5 ia7-cheng2 ia7 boeh siu-seng5, bo5 cheng3-choh ia7 boeh siu-koah;  27) an2-ne li2 eng-kai tioh8 chiong goa2 e5 chiN5 kia3 toa3 gin5-hang5, tan2 goa2 tng2-lai5 e5 si5, thang nia2 pun2-chiN5 kap li7-sek chhut-lai5 heng5 goa2.  28) TaN lin2 tioh8 chiong hit chit8-chheng niu2 gin5 ka7 i theh8 khi2-lai5, kau hou7 hit e5 u7 chit8 ban7 niu2 gin5 e5.  29) In-ui7 i2-keng u7 e5, boeh ke-thiN hou7 i, hou7 i kah u7 chhun; bo5 e5, lian5 i sou2 u7 e5 chit8-sut-la2, ia7 boeh ka7 i theh8 khi2-lai5.  30) Chit e5 bo5 lou7-eng7 e5 lou5-pok8, lin2 tioh8 ka7 i koaN2 chhut-khi3 goa7-bin7 ou-am3 e5 sou2-chai7. I e7 toa3 hia thi5-khau3 ka7-ge5 chhiat-khi2.’”

Choe3-au7 e5 sim2-phoaN3:
	31) “Jin5-chu2 chhoa7 I e5 chiong3 thian-sai3 chai3-lim5 e5 si5, I e7 cho3 ong5 che7 toa3 po2-cho7,  32) e7 chu7-chip8 ban7-bin5 lai5 I e5 bin7-cheng5, chiong in hun-cho3 nng7 peng5, chhin-chhiuN7 bok8-chia2 chiong mi5-iuN5 kap soaN-iuN5 hun-khui.  33) I e7 chiong mi5-iuN5 pai5 toa3 I e5 chiaN3-peng5, soaN-iuN5 pai5 toa3 I e5 to3-peng5.  34) Hit e5 si5, kun-ong5 e7 ka7 khia7 toa3 I chiaN3-peng5 e5 peh-seN3 kong2: ‘Lin2 chiah-e5 siu7 Goa2 e5 Thian-hu7 sou2 chiok-hok e5 lang5, lai5 a3! Lin2 lai5 seng5-siu7 hit e5 tui3 chhong3-cho7 u2-tiu7 chiu7 i2-keng ka7 lin2 pi7-pan7 pian7-pian7 e5 ong5-kok.  35) In-ui7 Goa2 iau, lin2 u7 hou7 Goa2 chiah8; Goa2 chhui3-ta, lin2 u7 hou7 goa2 lim; Goa2 cho3 chhut-goa7-lang5, lin2 u7 chiap-thai7 Goa2;  36) Goa2 chhiah-sin lou7-the2 e5 si5, lin2 u7 hou7 Goa2 chheng7; Goa2 phoa3-peN7, lin2 u7 khoaN3-kou3 Goa2; Goa2 che7-kaN, lin2 lai5 tham3-hong2 Goa2.’  37) Hit e5 si5 gi7-jin5 e7 in3 I kong2: ‘Chu2 a3, sim2-mih si5 goan2 khoaN3-kiN3 Li2 iau hou7 Li2 chiah8, khoaN3-kiN3 Li2 chhui3-ta hou7 Li2 lim?  38) Sim2-mih si5 goan2 khoaN3-kiN3 Li2 cho3 chhut-goa7-lang5 u7 chiap-thai7 Li2, a2-si7 khoaN3-kiN3 	Li2 chhiah-sin lou7-the2 e5 si5 u7 hou7 Li2 chheng7?  39) Sim2-mih si5 goan2 khoaN3-kiN3 Li2 phoa3-peN7 a2-si7 che7-kaN u7 lai5 tham3-hong2 Li2?’  40) kun-ong5 e7 ka7 in hoe5-tap kong2, ‘Goa2 sit8-chai7 ka7 lin2 kong2, bo5-lun7 sim2-mih si5 lin2 na7 ui7-tioh8 Goa2 chiah-e5 hiaN-ti7 tiong hou7 lang5 khoaN3 siong7 bo5 khi2 e5 chit8-e5, lai5 cho3 chiah-e5 tai7-chi3, chiu7-si7 tui3 Goa2 cho3 e5.'’
	41) “Jian5-au7 Kun-ong5 e7 ka7 khia7 toa3 I to3-peng5 e5 lang5 kong2: ‘ Lin2 chiah-e5 kho2-ouN3 e5, li7-khui Goa2! Jip8-khi3 ui7-tioh8 Mou5-kui2 kap i e5 su3-chia2 sou2 pi7-pan7 eng2-oan2 e5 hoe2-nih!  42) In-ui7 Goa2 iau, lin2 bo5 hou7 goa2 chiah8; Goa2 chhui3-ta, lin2 bo5 hou7 Goa2 lim;  43) Goa2 cho3 chhut-goa7-lang5, lin2 bo5 chiap-thai7 Goa2; Goa2 chhiah-sin lou7-the2 e5 si5, lin2 bo5 hou7 Goa2 chheng7; Goa2 phoa3-peN7 a2-si7 che7-kaN e5 si5, lin2 bo5 lai5 tham3-hong2 Goa2.’  44) Hit e5 si5, in e7 in3 kong2: ‘chu2 a3, sim2-mih si5 goan2 khoaN3-kiN3 Li2 iau, a2-si7 chhui3-ta, a2-si7 cho3 chhut-goa7-lang5, a2-si7 chhiah-sin lou7-the2, a2-si7 phoa3-peN7, a2-si7 che7-kaN, bo5 pang-chan7 Li2?’  45) Kun-ong5 chiu7 e7 hoe5-tap in kong2, ‘Goa2 sit8-chai7 ka7 lin2 kong2, lin2 bo5 ui7-tioh8 chiah-e5 hou7 lang5 khoaN3 siong7 bo5 khi2 e5 chit8 e5 lai5 cho3 chiah-e5 tai7-chi3, chiu7-si7 bo5 pang-chan7 Goa2.’  46) Chiah-e5 lang5 e7 khi3 siu7 eng2-oan2 e5 heng5-hoat8, tan7-si7 gi7-jin5 e7 khi3 hiong2-siu7 eng2-seng.”

Te7 26 ChiuN

Ke3-bou5 boeh sat-hai7 Ia5-sou: (Kho2 14:1-2; Lou7 22:1-2; Iok 11:45-53)
	1) Ia5-sou kong2 chiah-e5 oe7 liau2-au7, chiu7 ka7 I e5 bun5-tou5 kong2:  2) “ Lin2 sou2 chai-iaN2, koh nng7 jit8 chiu7-si7 PoaN5-koe3-cheh; hit e5 si5 Jin5-chu2 e7 hou7 lang5 kau khi3 teng3 sip8-ji7-ke3.”
	3) Hit e5 si5-chun7, che3-si-tiuN2 kap Iu5-thai3-lang5 e5 tiuN2-lo2 chu7-chip8 ti7 toa7-che3-si Kai-a-hoat e5 kong-koan2.  4) Tai7-ke chham-siong5 boeh eng7 ke3-ti3 lai5 liah8 Ia5-sou, lai5 ka7 I sat-hai7.  5) Tan7-si7 in kong2, “M7-thang chai7 chek-ki5 tiong, kiaN-liau2 peh-seN3 e7 hoat-seng po7-tong7.”

Ia5-sou chai7 Pek-tai7-ni5 siu7 boah-iu5: (Kho2 14:3-9; Iok 12:1-8)
	6) U7 chit8 jit8, Ia5-sou ti7 Pek-tai7-ni5 ba5-hong peN7-lang5 Se-bun5 e5 chhu3 e5 si5,  7) u7 chit8 e5 hu7-jin5-lang5 toa3 chit8 e5 gek8-pan5, lai7-bin7 te2 kek8 ko-kui3 e5 phang-iu5, lai5 kau3 I hia. Ia5-sou teh che7-toh e5 si5, chit e5 hu7-jin5-lang5 chiong phang-iu5 to3 toa3 I e5 thau5-khak teng2.  8) Chiah-e5 bun5-tou5 khoaN3-kiN3 an2-ne chiu7 chin siu7-khi3, kong2, “Na2 boeh hiah-nih8 long7-hui3?  9) Chit pan5 phang-iu5 na7 theh8 khi3 be7, e7-tang3 be7 chin-che7 chiN5 lai5 kiu3-che3 san3-chhiah-lang5.”  10) Ia5-sou chai-iaN2 in teh siuN7 sim2-mih, chiu7 ka7 in kong2: “Lin2 ho5-pit thiau-lan5 chit e5 hu7-jin5-lang5? I si7 ui7-tioh8 Goa2 cho3 chit8 hang7 chin bi2-sian7 e5 su7.  11) In-ui7 u7 san3-chhiah-lang5 put-si5 kap lin2 cho3-hoe2. tan7-si7 Goa2 be7 siong5-siong5 kap lin2 cho3-hoe2.  12) I eng7 phang-iu5 to3 toa3 Goa2 e5 seng-khu, si7 boeh chun2-pi7 Goa2 e5 bai5-chong3.  13) Goa2 sit8-chai7 ka7 lin2 kong2, chit e5 Hok-im bo5-lun7 thoan5 kau3 se3-kai3 e5 sim2-mih kak-lok8, lang5 long2 e7 kong2-khi2 chit e5 hu7-jin5-lang5 sou2 cho3 e5 tai7-chi3 lai5 ki3-liam7 i."

Iu5-tai7 chhut-be7 Ia5-sou: (Kho2 14:10-11; Lou7 22:3-6)
	14) Hit e5 si5, chap8-ji7 e5 bun5-tou5 tiong hit e5 kio3-cho3 Ka-liok8 e5 Iu5-tai7, khi3 kiN3 che3-si-tiuN2,  15) ka7 in kong2, “Goa2 na7 chiong Ia5-sou kau hou7 lin2, lin2 boeh hou7 goa2 sim2-mih?” In chiu7 sng3 saN-chap8 e5 gin5-oan5 hou7 i.  16) Tui3 hit e5 si5 khi2, i chiu7 teh chhoe7 sek-tong3 e5 ki-hoe7, boeh chiong Ia5-sou kau hou7 in.

Ia5-sou kap bun5-tou5 chiah8 PoaN5-koe3-cheh e5 boan2-chhan: (Kho2 14:12-21; Lou7 22:7-14, 21-23; Iok 13:21-30)
	17) Bo5-kaN3-cheh e5 thau5 chit8 jit8, bun5-tou5 lai5 mng7 Ia5-sou kong2, “Li2 ai3 goan2 toa3 sim2-mih sou2-chai7 ka7 Li2 chun2-pi7 PoaN5-koe3-cheh e5 boan2-chhan?”  18) Ia5-sou kong2: “Lin2 jip8-khi3 siaN5-lai7 chhoe7 bou2 chit8 e5 lang5 kong2, ‘Lau7-su kong2: Goa2 e5 si5 teh-boeh kau3 a3; Goa2 boeh kap Goa2 e5 bun5-tou5 toa3 lin2 chhu3 koe3 PoaN5-koe3-cheh,’”  19) Bun5-tou5 chiu7 chiau3 Ia5-sou e5 hoan-hu3, khi3 chun2-pi7 PoaN5-koe3-cheh e5 boan2-chhan.
	20) Am3-si5 chit8-e7 kau3, Ia5-sou kap chap8-ji7 e5 bun5-tou5 cho3-hoe2 che7 toh.  21) In teh chiah8 e5 si5, Ia5-sou kong2, “Goa2 sit8-chai7 ka7 lin2 kong2, lin2 tiong-kan u7 chit8 e5 e7 chhut-be7 Goa2.”  22) In chiu7 hui-siong5 iu-chhiu5, chit8 e5 chit8 e5 khai-si2 mng7 I kong2, “Chu2 a3, kam2 si7 goa2?”  23) Ia5-sou in3 kong2: “Kap Goa2 cho3-hoe2 chhun chhiu2 loh8-khi3 poaN5-nih8 un3 chiah8-mih8 hit e5 lang5, e7 chhut-be7 Goa2.  24) Jin5-chu2 e7 chiau3 Seng3-keng sou2 ki3-chai3 an2-ne lai5 li7-khui se3-kan; tan7-si7 chhut-be7 Jin5-chu2 hit e5 lang5 tioh8 u7 chai-ho7! Hit e5 lang5 leng5-kho2 bo5 chhut-si3 khah ho2.”  25) Chhut-be7 Ia5-sou e5 Iu5-tai7 ia7 mng7 Ia5-sou kong2, “Lau7-su, kam2 si7 goa2?” Ia5-sou in3 i kong2, “Li2 ka7-ti7 kong2 chhut-lai5 a3.”

Chu2 e5 boan2-chhan: (Kho2 14:22-26; Lou7 22:15-20; 1 Ko-lim5-to 11:23-25)
	26) In teh chiah8 e5 si5, Ia5-sou theh8 mih8-pau khi2-lai5 chiok-sia7 liau2-au7, peh khui, pun hou7 bun5-tou5, kong2: “Lin2 theh8 khi3 chiah8! Che si7 Goa2 e5 seng-khu."” 27) Jian5-au7 I koh phang5 poe khi2-lai5, chiok-sia7 liau2-au7, phang5 hou7 in, kong2: “Lin2 long2 tioh8 lim.  28) In-ui7 che si7 Goa2 e5 hoeh, chiu7-si7 ui7-tioh8 boeh sia3-bian2 cheng3-lang5 e5 choe7, sou2 lau5 chhut-lai5 e5 beng5-iok e5 hoeh.  29) Goa2 ka7 lin2 kong2, tui3 hian7-chai7 khi2, it-tit8 kau3 Goa2 chai7 goa2 e5 Thian-hu7 e5 Ong5-kok tiong7-sin kap lin2 lim hit chit8 jit8, Goa2 choat8-tui3 be7 koh lim chit khoan2 e5 phu5-to5-chiu2.”
	30) In gim5 seng3-si liau2-au7, chiu7 chhut-hoat khi3 Kan-na2-soaN.

I7-gian5 Pi2-tek m7-jin7 Chu2: (Kho2 14:27-31; Lou7 22:31-34; Iok 13:36-38)
	31) Au7-lai5 Ia5-sou ka7 in kong2: “Eng-am3 lin2 tai7-ke tui3 Goa2 e5 sin3-sim e7 khi2 tong7-iau5; in-ui7 Seng3-keng u7 ki3-chai3 kong2, ‘Goa2 boeh phah bok8-chia2, iuN5-kun5 chiu7 e7 si3-soaN3 khi3.’  32) tan7-si7 Siong7-chu2 hou7 Goa2 hok8-hoat8 liau2-au7, boeh pi2 lin2 khah tai7-seng khi3 Ka-li7-li7 Seng2.”  33) Pi2-tek chiu7 hoat-gian5 kong2, “Ka2-su2 in tai7-ke tui3 Li2 e5 sin3-sim e7 khi2 tong7--iau5, goa2 choat8-tui3 be7.”  34) Ia5-sou ka7 i kong2: “Goa2 sit8-chai7 ka7 li2 kong2, eng-am3 ke iau2-boe7 thi5 i2-cheng5, li2 e7 saN pai2 m7 jin7 Goa2.”  35) Pi2-tek ka7 I kong2, “Chiu7-si7 goa2 tioh8 kap Li2 cho3-hoe2 si2, goa2 ia7 it-teng7 be7 m7 jin7 Li2.” Ki5-tha e5 bun5-tou5 ia7 long2 an2-ne kong2.

Ia5-sou chai7 Khek-se-ma2-ni5-hng5 ki5-to2: (Kho2 14:32-42; Lou7 22:39-46)
	36) Jian5-au7 Ia5-sou kap bun5-tou5 lai5 kau3 chit8 e5 sou2-chai7, mia5 kio3-cho3 Khek-se-ma2-ni5-hng5. I ka7 bun5-tou5 kong2, “Goa2 khi3 hia ki5-to2 e5 tiong-kan, lin2 che7 toa3 chia tan2 Goa2.”  37) I chiu7 chhoa7 Pi2-tek kap Se-pi2-thai3 hit nng7 e5 kiaN2 cho3-hoe2 khi3. I khi2 iu-bun7, kam2-kak hui-siong5 thong3-khou2,  38) chiu7 tui3 in kong2, “Goa2 e5 sim iu-siong kah boeh si2-khi3. Lin2 toa2 chia tan2-hau7, lan2 long2 mai3 khun3.”  39) I chiu7 kiaN5 khah chin3-cheng5, bin7 phak loh8-khi3 thou5-kha ki5-to2, kong2: “Goa2 e5 Hu7-chhin, na7-si7 e7-eng7-tit, mai3 hou7 Goa2 lim chit poe khou2-poe! Tan7-si7 m7-thang chiau3 Goa2 e5 i3-su3, tioh8 chiau3 Li2 e5 i3-su3.”
	40) Jian5-au7 Ia5-sou tng2-lai5 bun5-tou5 hia khoaN3-kiN3 in teh khun3, chiu7 ka7 Pi2-tek kong2: “Lin2 saN e5 kam2 chin-chiaN3 bo5 hoat-tou7 mai3 khun3 kap Goa2 cho3-hoe2 chit8 tiam2-cheng ku2?  41) Lin2 m7-thang khun3-khi3, tioh8 ki5-to2, chiah be7 ham7-loh8 iu2-hek8. Lin2 sim iu2 i3 tan7-si7 lek8 put-chiok.”
42) Ia5-sou te7-ji7 pai2 koh khi3 ki5-to2 kong2:”Goa2 e5 Hu7-chhin, chit poe khou2-poe na7 bo5 Goa2 lim be7-eng7-tit, chiu7 chiau3 Li2 e5 chi2-i3 sit8-heng5!”  43) Ia5-sou koh tng2-khi3, khoaN3-kiN3 in iau2-ku2 teh khun3, in-ui7 in e5 bak8-chiu chin siap.
44) Ia5-sou koh li7-khui in, te7-saN pai2 khi3 ki5-to2, ia7-si7 kong2 kang7-khoan2 hiah-e5 oe7.  45) Choe3-au7 I tng2-khi3 bun5-tou5 hia, ka7 in kong2: “Lin2 iau2 teh khun3, iau2 teh hiu-sek si7 bo5? Lin2 khoaN3! Jin5-chu2 teh-boeh hou7 lang5 chhut-be7, kau hou7 choe7-jin5 e5 chhiu2-thau5, hit e5 si5 i2-keng kau3 a3!  46) Khi2-lai5, lan2 lai5 khi3! Lin2 khoaN3, chhut-be7 Goa2 hit e5 lang5 lai5 a7.”

Ia5-sou hou7 lang5 liah8-khi3: (Kho2 14:43-50; Lou7 22:47-53; Iok 18:3-12)
47) Ia5-sou iau2 teh kong2-oe7 e5 si5, chap8-ji7 bun5-tou5 e5 chit8 e5, Iu5-tai7 lai5 kau3 ui7. Hiah-e5 che3-si-tiuN2 kap Iu5-thai3-lang5 e5 tiuN2-lo2 sou2 phai3 chit8 toa7 tin7 lang5 giah8 kiam3 kap thui5-a2, ia7 kap i cho3-hoe2 lai5.  48) Hit e5 chhut-be7-chia2 su7-sian u7 kap in tho3 chit8 e5 am3-ho7 kong2: “Goa2 ka7 I chim hit e5 lang5 chiu7-si7 Ia5-sou, chek-si5 khi3 kau3 Ia5-sou e5 bin7-cheng5 kong2 “Lau7-su, peng5-an, “chiu7 ka7 I chim.  50) Ia5-sou ka7 Iu5-tai7 kong2, “Peng5-iu2 a3, li2 boeh cho3 e5 kin2 cho3.” Hiah-e5 lang5 chiu7 oa2-lai5 he7-chhiu2 liah8 Ia5-sou, ka7 I liah8 tiau5-tiau5.  51) Hit e5 si5, u7 chit8 e5 kap Ia5-sou cho3-hoe2 e5 bun5-tou5, chhun chhiu2 thiu kiam3 khi2-lai5, tui3 toa7-che3-si e5 lou5-pok8 phut loh8-khi3, ka7 i siah chit8 e5 hiN7-a2 khi2-lai5.  52) Ia5-sou ka7 i kong2: “siu li2 e5 kiam3 jip8-khi3 goan5-ui7; in-ui7 giah8 kiam3 e5 lang5, it-teng7 e7 si2 chai7 kiam3-ha7.  53) Li2 siuN7 Goa2 kam2 be7-tang3 kiu5 goa2 e5 Thian-hu7 sui5-si5 ka7 Goa2 chhe-phai3 chap8-ji7 kun-thoan5 khah-ke e5 thian-sai3 lai5 po2-hou7 Goa2, si7 bo5?  54) Tan7-si7 Goa2 na7 an2-ne cho3, Seng3-keng sou2 kong2 it-teng7 tioh8 an2-ne hoat-seng chit e5 tai7-chi3, boeh an3-choaN2 e7-tang3 eng3-giam7?”
55) Hit e5 si5, Ia5-sou ka7 cheng3-lang5 kong2: “Lin2 kam2 tioh8 giah8 kiam3 kap thui5-a2 chhut-lai5 liah8 goa2? Be7-su boeh liah8 chit8 e5 thou2-hui2! Goa2 tak8-jit8 che7 ti7 Seng-tian7 lai7 ka3-si7 chiah-e5 tai7-chi3 long2 si7 boeh eng3-giam7 tai7-gian5-jin5 ti7 Seng3-keng sou2 ki3-chai3 e5 oe7!”
Hit e5 si5 bun5-tou5 long2 pang3-sak Ia5-sou to5-chau2 khi3.

Ia5-sou chai7 Kong-gi7-hoe7 siu7-sim2: (Kho2 14:53-65; Lou7 22:54-55, 63-71; Iok 18:13-14,19-24)
57) Hiah-e5 liah8 Ia5-sou e5 lang5, ah I khi3-kau3 Toa7-che3-si Kai-a-hoat e5 kong-koan2, keng-hak8-chia2 kap Iu5-thai3-lang5 e5 tiuN2-lo2 ia7 i2-keng chu7-chip8 ti7 hia.  58) Pi2-tek li7 hng7-hng7 toe3 Ia5-sou khi3-kau3 Toa7-che3-si kong-koan2 e5 lai7-tiaN5. I jip8-khi3 hit lai7-bin7, kap hiah-e5 siu2-oe7 tau3-tin7 che7-le7, siuN7-boeh khoaN3 chit e5 tai7-chi3 e5 kiat-kiok8.  59) Che3-si-tiuN2 kap choan5-the2 Kong-gi7-hoe7 e5 gi7-oan5 teh chhoe7 ke2 cheng3-ki3 lai5 ko5 Ia5-sou, thang ka7 I teng7 si2-choe7;  60) sui-jian5 u7 chin-che7 lang5 lai5 cho3 gui7-cheng3, tan7-si7 in chhoe7 bo5 poaN3-hang7 cheng3-ki3. Choe3-au7 u7 nng7 e5 lang5 chhut-lai5,  61) kong2, “Chit e5 lang5 bat kong2, ‘Goa2 e7-tang3 hui2-hoai7 Siong7-chu2 e5 seng3-tian7, saN jit8 lai7 e7-tang3 koh kian3-cho7 khi2-lai5.’”
62) Toa7-che3-si khia7 khi2-lai5 ka7 Ia5-sou kong2, “Chiah-e5 lang5 theh8-chhut cheng3-ki3 lai5 ko3 Li2, Li2 na2 bo5 boeh tap-pian7?”  63) Tan7-si7 Ia5-sou tiam7-tiam7 bo5 in3. Toa7-che3-si koh ka7 I kong2: “Gao2 chi2 eng2-seng e5 Siong7-chu2, beng7-leng7 Li2 ka7 goan2 kong2, khoaN3 Li2 si7 Bi2-sai3-a, Siong7-chu2 e5 KiaN2 a2 m7-si7?”  64) Ia5-sou in3 i kong2: “Li2 ka-ti7 kong2 chhut-lai5 a3. TaN Goa2 boeh koh ka7 li2 kong2, tui3 hian7-chai7 khi2, lin2 e7 khoaN3-kiN3 Jin5-chu2 che7 ti7 choan5-leng5-chia2 e5 chiaN3-peng5, ia7 e7 che7 thiN-teng2 e5 hun5 kang3 loh8-lai5.”  65) ThiaN-tioh8 an2-ne, Toa7-che3-si chiu7 thiah-phoa3 ka-ti7 e5 goa7-saN, kong2: “I i2-keng kong2-chhut siat-tok8 Siong7-chu2 e5 oe7 a7; lan2 kam2 iau2 u7 koh su-iau3 cheng3-jin5? Lin2 khoaN3! Lin2 chit-chun7 i2-keng u7 thiaN-tioh8 I kong2-chhut siat-tok8 Siong7-chu2 e5 oe7 a7.  66) Lin2 siuN7 an3-choaN2?” In in3 kong2 “Eng-kai ka7 I chhu2 si2-heng5!”
67) Jian5-au7 in phui3-noa7 toa3 Ia5-sou e5 bin7, eng7 kun5-thau5-bo2 ka7 i cheng, ia7 u7 e5 eng7 chhiu2 ka7 I sian3,  68) kong2, “Bi2-sai3-a! Li2 na7 si7 tai7-gian5-jin5, ioh khoaN3 sim2-mih lang5 ka7 Li2 phah!”

Pi2-tek m7-jin7 Ia5-sou: (Kho2 14:66-72; Lou7 22:56-62; Iok 18:15-18,25-27)
69) Pi2-tek ti7 goa7-bin7 e5 tiaN5-nih8 teh che7 e5 si5, u7 chit8 e5 chhe-eng7 e5 cha-bou2-gin2-na2 oa2-lai5 ka7 i kong2, “Li2 ia7 u7 kap hit e5 Ka-li7-li7-lang5 Ia5-sou tau3-tin7.”  70) Pi2-tek ti7 cheng3-lang5 e5 bin7-cheng5 m7 seng5-jin7, chiu7 kong2, “goa2 m7-chai li2 teh kong2 sim2-mih.”  71) Pi2-tek kiaN5 chhut-khi3 kau3 toa7 mng7-khau2 e5 si5, iu7-koh u7 leng7-goa7 chit8 e5 chhe-eng7 e5 cha-bou2-gin2-na2 khoaN3-kiN3 i, chiu7 ka7 ti7 hia e5 lang5 kong2, “Chit e5 lang5 u7 kap Na2-sat-lek8-lang5 Ia5-sou tau3-tin7.”   72) Pi2-tek iu7-koh m7 seng5-jin7, soah chiu3-choa7 kong2, “Goa2 m7-bat hit e5 lang5.”  73) Keng-koe3 bo5 loa7 ku2, hiah-e5 khia7 ti7 piN-a e5 lang5, oa2-lai5 ka7 Pi2-tek kong2: “Li2 khak-sit8 si7 siok8 ti7 in hit tong2 e5, in-ui7 thiaN li2 e5 khiuN-khau2 chiu7 e7 chai-iaN2.”  74) Pi2-tek chiu3-choa7 kong2: “Goa2 na7 kong2 peh8-chhat8, goan7 Siong7-chu2 chek-hoat8 goa2! Goa2 m7-bat hit e5 lang5.” Tu2-tu2 hit e5 si5, ke chiu7 thi5.  75) Pi2-tek chiu7 siuN7-khi2 Ia5-sou tui3 i sou2 kong2 e5 oe7 kong2, “Ke thi5 i2-cheng5, li2 e7 saN pai2 m7 seng5-jin7 Goa2.” I chiu7 chhut-khi3 goa7-bin7, toa7-siaN thi5-khau3.

Te7 27 ChiuN

Ia5-sou hou7 lang5 ah kau3 Pi2-liap8-to hia: (Kho2 15:1; Lou7 23:1-2; Iok 18:28-32)
	1) ThiN chit8-e7 kng, chiong3 che3-si-tiuN2 kap peh-seN3 tiong e5 tiuN2-lo2, saN-kap ke3-ek8 boeh ham7-hai7 Ia5-sou, boeh ka7 I chhu2 si2-heng5.  2) In chiong Ia5-sou pak8 khi2-lai5, chiu7 an I khi3 kau hou7 Chong2-tok Pi2-liap8-to.

Iu5-tai7 chu7-sat: (Heng5-toan7 1:18-19)
