	3) Au7-lai5 chhut-be7 Ia5-sou e5 Iu5-tai7, khoaN3-kiN3 Ia5-sou i2-keng hou7 lang5 teng7-choe7, chin hou7-hoe2, chiu7 theh8 hit saN-chap8 e5 gin5-oan5 khi3 heng5 hiah-e5 che3-si-tiuN2 kap tiuN2-lo2.  4) I kong2: “Goa2 u7 hoan7-choe7; goa2 u7 chhut-be7 chit8 e5 bo5 choe7 e5 lang5, hai7 I khi3 si2.” In in3 kong2, “Che kap goan2 u7 sim2-mih koan-he7? Che si7 li2 ka-ti7 e5 tai7-chi3!”  5) Iu5-tai7 chiong hiah-e5 gin5-oan5 hiat toa3 seng3-tian7 e5 lai7-bin7 chiu7 li7-khui in, chhut-khi3 tiau3-si2.
	6) Hiah-e5 che3-si-tiuN2 khioh hiah-e5 gin5-oan5 khi2-lai5 kong2, “chiau3 Lut8-hoat e5 kui-teng7, chiah-e5 chiN5 m7-thang khng3 jip8-khi3 seng3-tian7 e5 kim-khou3, in-ui7 che si7 hai7-si2 lang5 e5 kang-chiN5.”  7) In chham-siong5 liau2-au7, chiu7 koat-teng7 eng7 chiah-e5 chiN5 khi3 be2 sio-hui5 e5 lang5 e5 hng5, thang cho3 chhut-goa7-lang5 e5 bong7-te7.  8) Sou2-i2 hit e5 hng5 kau3 kin-na2-jit8 iau2 kio3-cho3 “hoeh e5 hng5”.
	9,10) Chit e5 tai7-chi3 si7 eng3-giam7 tai7-gian5-jin5 Ia5-li7-bi2 sou2 kong2 e5 oe7, kong2: “chiau3 Siong7-chu2 sou2 beng7-leng7 Goa2 e5, in theh8 hit saN-chap8 e5 gin5-oan5, khi3 be2 sio-hui5 e5 lang5 e5 hng5. (Chit e5 ke3-siau3 si7 I2-sek-liat8-lang5 be2 chit8 e5 lang5 e5 ke3-chiN5.)”

Pi2-liap8-to sim2-mng7 Ia5-sou: (Kho2 15:2-5; Lou7 23:3-5; Iok 18:33-38)
	11) Ia5-sou khia7 ti7 Chong2-tok Pi2-liap8-to e5 bin7-cheng5, Chong2-tok sim2-mng7 I kong2, “Li2 si7 Iu5-thai3-lang5 e5 ong5 si7 bo5?” Ia5-sou in3 kong2, “Chiau3 li2 kong2 an2-ne.”  12) Tan7-si7 che3-si-tiuN2 kap tiuN2-lo2 khong3-ko3 I e5 si5, I long2 bo5 in3 poaN3-ku3.  13) Sou2-i2 Pi2-liap8-to ka7 I kong2, “Li2 kam bo5 thiaN-kiN3 in sou2 khong3-ko3 Li2 chiah-e5 choe7-chng7?”  14) Tan7-si7 Ia5-sou lian5 chit8 ku3 oe7 ia7 m7 ka7 i in3, chong2-tok soah kam2-kak hui-siong5 bok8-beng5 ki5-biau7.

Ia5-sou pi7 phoaN3 si2-heng5: (Kho2 15:6-15; Lou7 23:13-25; Iok 18:39-19:16)
	15) Mui2-ni5 e5 PoaN5-koe3-cheh, chiau3 koan3-le7 Chong2-tok long2 u7 pang3 chit8 e5 bin5-chiong3 sou2 iau-kiu5 e5 hoan7-lang5 chhut-khi3.  16) Hit e5 si5 u7 chit8 e5 chhut-mia5 e5 haon7-lang5, mia5 kio3-cho3 Pa-liap8-pa e5 Ia5-sou.  17) Sou2-i2 kun5-chiong3 chu7-chip8 e5 si5, Pi2-liap8-to mng7 in kong2: “Lin2 ai3 goa2 pang tah chit8 e5 hoan7-lang5 hou7 lin2? Si7 kio3-cho3 Pa-liap8-pa e5 Ia5-sou, a2-si7 hit e5 chheng-hou cho3 Ki-tok e5 Ia5-sou?”  18) Pi2-liap8-to beng5-beng5 chai-iaN2 si7 inui7 chit-tou3 chiah chiong Ia5-sou kau hou7 i.
	19) Pi2-liap8-to iau2 teh sim2-mng7 e5 si5, i e5 hu-jin5 chhe lang5 lai5 ka7 i kong2: “Hit e5 gi7-jin5 e5 tai7-chi3, li2 chhian-ban7 m7-thang kan-siap8; in-ui7 chang-am3 ui7-tioh8 I, goa2 u7 bang7- kiN3 chit8 e5 phaiN2-bang7.”
	20) Chiah-e5 che3-si-tiuN2 kap tiuN2-lo2 chiu7 sian3-tong7 bin5-chiong3, kio3 in tioh8 iau-kiu5 Pi2-liap8-to pang3 Pa-liap8-pa, chiong Ia5-sou chhu2 si2-heng5.  21) Chong2-tok mng7 in kong2, “Chit nng7 lang5 e5 tiong-kan, lin2 ai3 goa2 pang3 tah chit8 e5?” In kong2, “Pa-liap8-pa.”  22) Pi2-liap8-to mng7 in kong2, “An2-ne, hit e5 chheng-hou cho3 Ki-tok e5 Ia5-sou, goa2 tioh8 an3-choaN2 ka7 I pan7?” Cheng3-lang5 long2 in3 kong2, “Ka7 I teng3 sip8-ji7-ke3.”  23) Pi2-liat8-to mng7 in kong2, “Si7 an3-choaN2? I u7 hoan7 tioh8 sim2-mih choe7?” In koh-khah toa7 siaN hoah kong2, “Ka7 I teng3 sip8-ji7-ke3.”  24) Pi2-liap8-to chai-iaN2 i2-keng bo5 chhai2-kang, tian-to3 e7 in2-khi2 po7-tong7, i chiu7 phang3 chui2 lai5 toa3 cheng3-lang5 e5 bin7-cheng5 se2-chhiu2, iu7-koh kong2, “Hou7 chit e5 lang5 si2, m7-si7 goa2 e5 chek-jim7. Lin2 ka-ti7 tioh8 hu7-chek!”  25) Cheng-lang5 hoe5-tap kong2, “Ka7 chit e5 lang5 chhu2 si2-heng5 e5 chek-jim7, hou7 goan2 kap goan2 e5 kiaN2-sun lai5 tam-tng!”  26) An2-ne Pi2-liap8-to chiu7 ka7 in pang3 Pa-liap8-pa, tan7-si7 beng7-leng7 lang5 eng7 piN phah Ia5-sou, jian5-au7 chiong I kau hou7 in khi3 teng3 sip8-ji7-ke3.

Peng-su7 hi3-lang7 Ia5-sou: (Kho2 15:16-20; Iok 19:2-3)
	27) Jian5-au7 Chong2-tok e5 peng-su7 ah Ia5-sou jipkh8i Chong2-tok-hu2, tiau3-chip8 choan5-tui7 e5 peng-su7 lai5 ka7 I ui5-le7.  28) In thng3 Ia5-sou e5 saN khi2-lai5, ka7 I chheng7 chit8 nia2 chu-ang-sek e5 tng5-phau3,  29) koh eng7 chhi3-a2 piN7 chit8 teng2 ong5-koan ti3 toa3 I e5 thau5-khak-teng2, chiong chit8 ki lou5-tek-a2 hou7 I giah8 toa3 chiaN3-chhiuN2, jian5-au7 in chiah kui7 toa3 I e5 bin7-cheng5 hi3-lang7 I kong2, “Iu5-thai3-lang5 e5 Ong5, ban7-soe3!”  30) In ka7 I phui3-noa7, giah8 hit ki lou5-tek-a2 khil2ai sut I e5 thau5-khak.  31) In hi3-lang7 Ia5-sou liau2-au7, chiu7 ka7 I thng3 hit nia2 chu-ang-sek e5 tng5-phau3 khi2-lai5, koh ka7 I chheng7 I ka-ti7 e5 saN, jian5-au7 ka7 I ah chhut-khi3 boeh teng2 sip8-ji7-ke3.

Ia5-sou pi7-teng3 sip8-ji7-ke3: (Kho2 15:21-32; Lou7 23:26-43; Iok 19:17-27)
	32) Peng-su7 ah Ia5-sou chhut-lai5 e5 si5, tu2-tioh8 chit8 e5 Kou2-li7-nai7-lang5, kio3-cho3 Se-bun5. In kiong5-pek i gia5 Ia5-sou e5 sip8-ji7-ke3.  33) In lai5 kau3 chit8 e5 sou2-chai7 kio3-cho3 Kok-kok-tha. Chit e5 te7-mia5 e5 i3-su3 chiu7-si7 “Thau5-khak-oaN2 e5 sou2-chai7.”  34) Peng-su7 eng7 chham khou2-taN2 e5 chiu2 hou7 Ia5-sou lim; I tamchit8-e7 chiu7 m7 koh lim.
	35) In chiong Ia5-sou teng3 sip8-ji7-ke3 liau2-au7, chiu7 thiu khau-a2 lai5 pun I e5 saN.  36) Jian5-au7 in che7 toa3 hia kou3-siu2 I.  37) Ti7 Ia5-sou e5 thau5-khak-boe2-teng2, in teng3 chit8 e5 pai5, sia2 I e5 choe7-chng7 kong2: “chit e5 lang5 si7 Iu5-thai3-lang5 e5 Ong5 ---Ia5-sou.”  38) Hit e5 si7 ia7 u7 nng7 e5 kiong-to7 kap Ia5-sou cho3-hoe2 pi7-teng3 sip8-ji7-ke3, chit8 e5 ti7 I e5 chiaN3-peng5, chit8 e5 ti7 I e5 to3-peng5.
	39) Tui3 hia keng-koe3 e5 lang5 bu2-jiok8 I, io5-thau5 kong2:  40) “Ai a3! Li2 chit e5 boeh hui2-hoai7 seng3-tian7, saN-jit8 lai7 boeh koh tiong7-kian3 e5! Li2 na7-si7 Siong7-chu2 e5 KiaN2, taN tioh8 kiu3 Li2 ka-ti7, tui3 sip8-ji7-ke3-teng2 loh8-lai5!”  41) Hiah-e5 che3-si-tiuN2, keng-hak8-chia2 i2-kip8 tiuN2-lo2 ia7-si7 an2-ne hi3-lang7 I, kong2:  42) “I kiu3 pat8-lang5, be7-tang3 kiu3 ka-ti7! I si7 I2-sek-liat8-lang5 e5 Ong5 a3! TaN I na7 tui3 sip8-ji7-ke3-teng2 loh8-lai5, goan2 chiu7 boeh sin3 I!  43) I sin3-kho3 Siong7-chu2. Siong7-chu2 na7 boeh kiu3 I,  taN tioh8 lai5 kiu3 I; in-ui7 I u7 kong2: ‘Goa2 si7 Siong7-chu2 e5 KiaN2!’”  44) Sim7-chi3 kap I cho3-hoe2 hou7 lang5 teng3 sip8-ji7-ke3 hit nng7 e5 kiong5-to7, ia7 an2-ne bu2-jiok8 I.

Ia5-sou e5 si2-bong5: (Kho2 15:33-41; Lou7 23:44-49; Iok 19:28-30)
	45) Tui3 tiong-tau3 khi2 saN tiam2-cheng ku2 choan5-te7 long2 pian3-cho3 ou-ou am3-am3.  46) chha-put-to e7-pou-si5 saN tiam2, Ia5-sou toa7-siaN hoah kong2: “I2-li7, I2-li7, liap8-ma2, sat-pok-tai7-ni5!” i3-su3 chiu7-si7 kong2: “Goa2 e5 Siong7-chu2, Goa2 e5 Siong7-chu2! Li2 an3-choaN2 pang3-sak goa2?”  47) Ti7 piN-a teh khia7 e5 lang5, u7 e5 thiaN-kiN3 chiu7 kong2, “Chit e5 lang5 teh kio3 I2-li7-a.”  48) Ki5-tiong u7 chit8 e5 lang5 chek-si5 chau2-khi3 theh8 hai2-mi5, chim3 sng-khi3 e5 chiu2, pak8 toa3 lou5-tek-a2 boe2 boeh hou7 I lim.  49) Ki5-tha e5 lang5 kong2, “Lan2 lai5 tan2 khoaN3 I2-li7-a e7 lai5 kiu3 I a2 be7!”  50) Ia5-sou koh toa7 kio3 chit8 siaN, chiu7 tng7-khui3.
	51) Hut-jian5-kan, koa3 ti7 seng3-tian7 lai7 e5 pou3-li5 tui3 teng2-bin7 kau3 e7-bin7 lih8 cho3 nng7 peng5. Te7 toa7 tin2-tang7, chioh8-poaN5 piak-lih8,  52) bong7 ia7 piak-khui, u7 chin-che7 i2-keng si2-khi3 e5 Siong7-chu2 e5 chu2-bin5 koh-oah8 khi2-lai5.  53) Ia5-sou hok8-hoat8 liau2-au7, tui3 bong7-nih8 chhut-lai5 chiah-e5 lang5 jip8-khi3 Seng3-siaN5. U7 chin-che7 lang5 khoaN3-kiN3 in.
	54) Lian5-tiuN2 kap hiah-e5 teh kou3-siu2 Ia5-sou e5 peng-su7, chit8-e7 khoaN3-kiN3 te7-tang7 kap sou2 hoat-seng chiah-e5 tai7-chi3, chiu7 hui-siong5 tioh8-kiaN, kong2, “Chit e5 lang5 chin-chiaN3 si7 Siong7-chu2 e5 KiaN2.”  55) Ti7 hia u7 chin-che7 hu7-jin5-lang5 li7 hng7-hng7 teh khoaN3. In chiu7-si7 tui3 Ka-li7-li7 Seng2 lai5 kin-toe3 Ia5-sou, koh teh su7-hau7 I e5.  56) Ki5-tiong u7 Boat8-tai7-liap8-lang5 Ma2-li7-a, Nga2-kok kap Iok-sek e5 lau7-bo2 Ma2-li7-a, ia7 u7 Se-pi2-thai3 e5 bou2.

Ia5-sou e5 bai5-chong3: (Kho2 15:42-47; Lou7 23:50-56; Iok 19:38-42)
	57) ThiN i2-keng am3 a3, u7 chit8 e5 A-li7-ma2-thai3 e5 ho2-giah8-lang5 lai5 kau3 Ia5-lou7-sat-leng2. I e5 mia5 kio3-cho3 Iok-sek, ia7 si7 Ia5-sou e5 chit8 e5 bun5-tou5.  58) Chit e5 lang5 khi3 kiN3 Pi2-liap8-to, chheng2-kiu5 siu-bai5 Ia5-sou e5 sin-si. Pi2-liap8-to chiu7 hoan-hu3 lang5 kau sin-si hou7 i.  59) Iok-sek nia2 Ia5-sou e5 sin-si, eng7 chheng-khi3 e5 iu3 te7-a2 pou3 ka7 I pau khi2-lai5,  60) an-chong3 toa3 Iok-sek ka-ti7 e5 bong7. Chit e5 bong7 si7 Iok-sek choe3-kin7 chiah phah chioh8-piah cho3 ho2 e5. Jian5-au7 Iok-sek lian3 chit8 liap8 toa7 chioh8 that toa3 bong7-khau2, chiu7 li7-khui hia.  61) Hit e5 si5 Boat8-tai7-liap8-lang5 Ma2-li7-a kap iau2 chit8 e5 Ma2-li7-a che7 ti7 bong7 e5 tui3-bin7.

Phai3 oe7-peng siu2-bong7:
	62) Te7-ji7 jit8, chiu7-si7 pai3 gou7 e5 keh-tng2-jit8, hiah-e5 che3-si-tiuN2 kap Hoat-li7-sai3-phai3 e5 lang5, cho3-hoe2 lai5 Chong2-tok-hu2 kiN3 Pi2-liap8-to,  63) kong2: “Chong2-tok tai7-jin5, goan2 e7-ki3-tit hit e5 phian3-chu2 iau2 teh oah8 e5 si5, bat kong2, ‘SaN-jit8 au7, Siong7-chu2 it-teng7 e7 hou7 Goa2 hok8-hoat8.’  64) Sou2-i2 chhiaN2 li2 phai3 oe7-peng khi3 kou3 hit e5 bong7, kou3 kau3 te7-saN jit8. I e5 bun5-tou5 chiah be7 lai5 thau kng I e5 sin-si khi3, chiah ka7 cheng3-lang5 kong2, ‘I i2-keng tui3 si2-lang5 e5 tiong-kan hok8-hoat8 a7.’ Na7 an2-ne, choe3-au7 chit e5 phian3-kiok8 chiu7 e7 pi2 khi2-thau5 koh-khah li7-hai7.”  65) Pi2-liap8-to ka7 in kong2, “Lin2 chhoa7 oe7-peng khi3, ho2-ho2 khi3 kou3-siu2 hit e5 bong7!”  66) In chiu7 khi3 bong7 hia, eng7 hong-tiau5 hong hit liap8 chioh8-thau5 khi2-lai5, lau5 oe7-peng toa3 hia kou3-siu2.

Te7 28 ChiuN

Ia5-sou e5 hok8-hoat8: (Kho2 16:1-10; Lou7 24:1-12; Iok 20:1-10)
	1) An-hioh-jit8 koe3 liau2-au7, Le2-pai3-jit8, thiN teh-boeh kng e5 si5, Boat8-tai7-liap8-lang5 Ma2-li7-a kap leng7-goa7 chit8 e5 Ma2-li7-a khi3 khoaN3 hit e5 bong7.  2) Hut-jian5-kan u7 toa7 te7-tang7, in-ui7 u7 chit8 ui7 Chu2 e5 thian-sai3 tui3 thiN-teng2 loh8-lai5, lian3-khui hit liap8 chioh8-thau5, che7 toa3 chioh8-thau5 teng2.  3) I e5 iong5-mau7 chhin-chhiuN7 sih-na3, i e5 saN peh8 kah chhin-chhiuN7 she.  4) Hiah-e5 oe7-peng kiaN kah phih8-phih8-chhoah, soah pian3-cho3 chhin-chhiuN7 si2-lang5.
	5) Hit-ui7 thian-sai3 ka7 hiah-e5 hu7-jin5-lang5 kong2: “Lin2 m7-bian2 kiaN, in-ui7 goa2 chai-iaN2 lin2 teh chhoe7 Hit-ui7 hou7 lang5 teng3 sip8-ji7-ke3 e5 Ia5-sou.  6) I bo5 ti7 chia, in-ui7 I chiau3 I i2-cheng5 sou2 kong2 e5, i2-keng hok8-hoat8 a7. Lin2 lai5 khoaN3 an-ti3 Ia5-sou e5 sou2-chai7.  7) TaN lin2 tioh8 koaN2-kin2 ka7 I e5 bun5-tou5 kong2: ‘I i2-keng tui3 si2-lang5 e5 tiong-kan hok8-hoat8 a7; I boeh pi2 lin2 khah tai7-seng khi3 Ka-li7-li7 Seng2. Ti7 hia lin2 e7 kiN3-tioh8 I! TaN goa2 i2-keng ka7 lin2 kong2 a3.”  8) In chiu7 koaN2-kin2 li7-khui hit e5 bong7, ia7 chin kiaN, ia7 toa7 hoaN-hi2, chau2 khi3 po3-ko3 Ia5-sou e5 bun5-tou5.
	9) Ti7 lou7-tiong, hut-jian5-kan Ia5-sou tu2-tioh8 in, ka7 in kong2. “Tai7-ke peng5-an!” In chiu7 oa2-khi3 Ia5-sou hia, lam2 I e5 kha, phak loh8-khi3 Ia-sou e5 bin7-cheng5 keng3-pai3 I.  10) Ia5-sou chiu7-ka7 in kong2: “M7-bian2 kiaN. Lin2 tioh8 khi3 hoan-hu3 Goa2 e5 hiaN-ti7, kio3 in khi3 Ka-li7-li7 Seng2, ti7 hia in chiu7 e7 kiN3-tioh8 Goa2.”

Oe7-peng e5 po3-ko3:
	11) Chiah-e5 hu7-jin5-lang5 iau2 ti7 lou7-nih8 teh kiaN5 e5 si5, u7 chit8-koa2 teh kou3-siu2 bong7 e5 oe7-peng to3-tng2-khi3 siaN5-lai7, chiong sou2 hoat-seng it-chhe3 e5 tai7-chi3, long2 ka7 chiah-e5 che3-si-tiuN2 po3-ko3.  12) Che3-si-tiuN2 chiu7 kap tiuN2-lo2 khui-hoe7, cho3-hoe2 chham-siong5 liau2-au7, theh8 chin-che7 chiN5 be2-siu  hiah-e5 oe7-peng,  13) kong2: “Lin2 tioh8 an2-ne kong2: ‘Am3-si5 goan2 teh khun3 e5 si5 Ia5-sou e5 bun5-tou5 lai5 thau kng I e5 sin-si khi3,’  14) Ban7-it Chong2-tok na7 chai-iaN2 chit e5 tai7-chi3, goan2 chiah kong2 hou7 i liau2-kai2, po2 lin2 bo5 tai7-chi3.”  15) Hiah-e5 oe7-peng theh8-tioh8 hiah-e5 chiN5, chiu7 chiau3 in sou2 hoan-hu3 e5 khi3 cho3. Chit e5 iau-gian5 chai7 Iu5-thai3-lang5 e5 tiong-kan it-tit8 liu5-thoan5 kau3 kin-na2-jit8.

Ia5-sou tui3 I e5 bun5-tou5 hian2-hian7: (Kho2 16:14-18; Lou7 24:36-49; Iok 20:19-23; Heng5-toan7 1:6-8)
	16) Chap8-it e5 bun5-tou5 khi3 Ka-li7-li7 Segn2, khi3-kau3 Ia5-sou ka7 in chi2-teng7 hit cho7 soaN-teng2.  17) In chit8-e7 khoaN3-kiN3 Ia5-sou, chiu7 kui7 loh8-khi3 pai3 I, tan7-si7 u7 e5 lang5 u7 teh giau5-gi5.  18) Ia5-sou oa2-lai5 ka7 in kong2: “Siong7-chu2 i2-keng chiong thiN-teng2 te7-e7 it-chhe3 e5 koan5-peng3 long2 kau hou7 Goa2 a3.  19) Sou2-i2 lin2 tioh8 khi3 chio ban7-bin5 lai5 cho3 Goa2 e5 bun5-tou5. Tioh8 hong7 Seng3 Hu7, Seng3 Chu2, Seng3 Leng5 e5 mia5 ka7 in si-heng5 se2-le2.  20) Ia7 tioh8 ka3-si7 in chun-siu2 Goa2 sou2 beng7-leng7 lin2 e5 it-chhe3. Lin2 tioh8 chai-iaN2, Goa2 e7 siong5-siong5 kap lin2 tong5-chai7, it-tit8 kau3 se3-kai3 e5 boat8-jit8.”
